########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/jobshots/server.js
########################################################################################################################

/* server.js */
import express from 'express';
import puppeteer from 'puppeteer-core';
import fs from 'fs';
import fsp from 'fs/promises';
import path from 'path';
import os from 'os';

const app = express();
const PORT = Number(process.env.PORT || 3000);

const SAVE_DIR = process.env.SAVE_DIR || '/shots';
const MAX_CONCURRENCY = Number(process.env.MAX_CONCURRENCY || 1);
const MAX_SAVED = Number(process.env.MAX_SAVED || 100);
const DELETE_AFTER_SERVE = String(process.env.DELETE_AFTER_SERVE || '0') === '1';
const NAV_TIMEOUT = Number(process.env.NAV_TIMEOUT || 50000);

let active = 0;
const queue = [];

/* ---------- concurrency ---------- */
function acquire() {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const tryTake = () => {
      if (active < MAX_CONCURRENCY) {
        active++;
        resolve(() => {
          active--;
          if (queue.length) queue.shift()();
        });
      } else {
        queue.push(tryTake);
      }
    };
    tryTake();
  });
}

/* ---------- fs helpers ---------- */
async function ensureSaveDir() {
  try { await fsp.mkdir(SAVE_DIR, { recursive: true }); } catch (err) { }
}

async function cleanupOldFiles() {
  try {
    const files = await fsp.readdir(SAVE_DIR);
    const pngs = files.filter(f => /\.png$/i.test(f));
    if (pngs.length > MAX_SAVED) {
      const stats = await Promise.all(pngs.map(async fn => {
        const st = await fsp.stat(path.join(SAVE_DIR, fn));
        return { fn, mtime: st.mtimeMs };
      }));
      stats.sort((a, b) => a.mtime - b.mtime);
      const removeCount = pngs.length - MAX_SAVED;
      for (let i = 0; i < removeCount; i++) {
        try { await fsp.unlink(path.join(SAVE_DIR, stats[i].fn)); } catch (err) { }
      }
    }
  } catch (err) { }
}

/* ---------- chromium launch ---------- */
function resolveExecutable() {
  const candidates = [
    process.env.PUPPETEER_EXECUTABLE_PATH,
    '/usr/bin/chromium',
    '/usr/bin/chromium-browser',
    '/usr/bin/google-chrome-stable',
    '/usr/bin/google-chrome'
  ].filter(Boolean);
  for (const p of candidates) {
    try { if (fs.existsSync(p)) return p; } catch (err) { }
  }
  return undefined;
}

async function launchBrowser() {
  const exe = resolveExecutable();
  const args = [
    '--no-sandbox',
    '--disable-setuid-sandbox',
    '--disable-dev-shm-usage',
    '--disable-gpu',
    '--disable-software-rasterizer',
    '--hide-scrollbars',
    '--disable-extensions',
    '--disable-background-timer-throttling'
  ];
  return puppeteer.launch({
    args,
    headless: 'new',
    executablePath: exe,
    timeout: 20000
  });
}

/* ---------- helpers ---------- */
function sanitizeName(s) {
  return String(s || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/g, '_');
}

/* ---------- routes ---------- */
app.get('/shot', async (req, res) => {
  const release = await acquire();
  let browser;
  try {
    const rawUrl = String(req.query.url || '');
    if (!rawUrl) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'missing url' });

    const initial = /^https?:\/\//i.test(rawUrl) ? rawUrl : `http://${rawUrl}`;
    let target;
    try { target = new URL(initial); } catch (err) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'invalid url' });
    }

    const mode = String(req.query.mode || 'story');
    if (mode === 'story') {
      target.searchParams.set('screenshot', '1');
      target.searchParams.set('mode', 'story');
    } else if (mode === 'post') {
      target.searchParams.set('screenshot', '1');
      target.searchParams.set('mode', 'post');
    }

    const url = target.toString();
    const selector = req.query.selector ? String(req.query.selector) : null;
    // بالای هندلر /shot
    const jobCounter = String(req.query._job_counter || Date.now());
    const baseName = `shot_${jobCounter}`;
    const savePath = path.join(SAVE_DIR, `${baseName}.png`);


    await ensureSaveDir();
    browser = await launchBrowser();
    const page = await browser.newPage();
    await page.setViewport(mode === 'story' ? { width: 1080, height: 1920 } :
      mode === 'square' ? { width: 1080, height: 1080 } :
        { width: 1080, height: 1500 });

    console.log('[jobshots] navigating to:', url);
    await page.setRequestInterception(true);
    page.on('request', (req) => {
      const url = req.url();
      if (
        req.resourceType() === 'media' ||
        req.resourceType() === 'image' ||
        (
          req.resourceType() === 'font' &&
          !url.includes('asamarketing.ir') // فونت‌های داخلی مجاز، خارجی بلاک
        ) ||
        url.includes('googletagmanager') ||
        url.includes('google-analytics') ||
        url.includes('doubleclick') ||
        url.includes('facebook') ||
        url.includes('instagram.com') ||
        url.includes('tiktok') ||
        url.includes('ads') ||
        url.includes('tracker')
      ) {
        req.abort();
      } else {
        req.continue();
      }
    });


    try {
      await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: ['domcontentloaded', 'networkidle2'], timeout: 30000 });
      /*await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded', timeout: NAV_TIMEOUT });*/
    } catch (err) {
      console.warn('[jobshots] goto timeout, fallback screenshot', err.message);
    }

    if (mode === 'story') {
      await page.addStyleTag({
        content: `
          #shot-fallback .body-text {
            column-count: 1 !important;
            column-gap: 0 !important;
            max-width: 800px !important;   /* عرض متن کمتر بشه (قبلاً 1080px بود) */
            margin: 0 auto !important;     /* متن بیاد وسط */
            padding: 0 40px !important;    /* فاصله از کناره‌ها بیشتر بشه */
          }
        `
      });

      let targetEl = null;
      const candidates = selector ? [selector] : [
        '#shot-fallback',
        '.listing',
        'article',
        'main',
        '.post',
        '.job',
        '.content'
      ];
      for (const sel of candidates) {
        try {
          await page.waitForSelector(sel, { timeout: 3000 });
          const el = await page.$(sel);
          if (el) { targetEl = el; break; }
        } catch (err) { }
      }
      if (targetEl) {
        const box = await targetEl.boundingBox();
        if (box && box.width > 1 && box.height > 1) {
          await targetEl.screenshot({ path: savePath });
        } else {
          await page.screenshot({ path: savePath, fullPage: false });
        }
      } else {
        await page.screenshot({ path: savePath, fullPage: false });
      }
    } else {
      await page.screenshot({ path: savePath, fullPage: false });
    }

    console.log('[jobshots] screenshot saved at', savePath);
    res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'image/png');
    res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', `inline; filename="${baseName}.png"`);
    const stream = fs.createReadStream(savePath);
    stream.on('error', (err) => {
      console.error('[jobshots] stream error:', err?.message);
      if (!res.headersSent) res.status(500).json({ error: 'stream_error' });
    });
    stream.on('end', async () => {
      if (DELETE_AFTER_SERVE) {
        try { await fsp.unlink(savePath); } catch (err) { }
      }
    });
    stream.pipe(res);

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[jobshots] error:', err?.stack || err);
    if (!res.headersSent) {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'screenshot_failed', detail: String(err?.message || err) });
    }
  } finally {
    if (browser) { try { await browser.close(); } catch (err) { } }
    release();
  }
});

/* ---------- health & metrics ---------- */
app.get('/health', (req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, active, queued: queue.length }));
app.get('/metrics', (req, res) => res.json({
  active,
  queued: queue.length,
  maxConcurrency: MAX_CONCURRENCY,
  totalRamMB: Math.round(os.totalmem() / 1024 / 1024)
}));

/* ---------- start ---------- */
(async () => {
  await ensureSaveDir();
  app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`jobshots listening on :${PORT} SAVE_DIR=${SAVE_DIR}`));
})();

/* ---------- shutdown ---------- */
process.on('SIGINT', () => process.exit(0));
process.on('SIGTERM', () => process.exit(0));
process.on('uncaughtException', (err) => {
  console.error('[jobshots] uncaughtException:', err?.stack);
  process.exit(1);
});
process.on('unhandledRejection', (reason) => {
  console.error('[jobshots] unhandledRejection:', reason);
  process.exit(1);
});

FILE: src/src/api/routers/job_router.py
########################################################################################################################

# /root/ASASANAT1/src/api/routers/job_router.py
import asyncio
import subprocess
from fastapi import APIRouter, Form
from fastapi.responses import RedirectResponse

router = APIRouter()

# وضعیت jobها (ساده)
running_jobs: dict[str, subprocess.Popen] = {}

# تعریف jobها و دستور اجرای آنها
JOB_COMMANDS = {
    "company_crawler": ["python", "-m", "src.company.runner"],
    "company_worker":  ["python", "-m", "src.company.pipeline.worker"],
    "news_collector":  ["python", "-m", "src.news.collector"],
    "news_sender":     ["python", "-m", "src.news.send"],
}

@router.post("/start")
async def start_job(job: str = Form(...)):
    if job in running_jobs:
        return {"status": "already_running", "job": job}
    if job not in JOB_COMMANDS:
        return {"status": "unknown_job", "job": job}

    proc = subprocess.Popen(JOB_COMMANDS[job])
    running_jobs[job] = proc
    return {"status": "started", "job": job, "pid": proc.pid}

@router.post("/stop")
async def stop_job(job: str = Form(...)):
    proc = running_jobs.get(job)
    if not proc:
        return {"status": "not_running", "job": job}
    proc.terminate()
    proc.wait(timeout=5)
    del running_jobs[job]
    return {"status": "stopped", "job": job}

@router.get("/status")
async def job_status():
    statuses = {}
    for job, proc in running_jobs.items():
        statuses[job] = {"pid": proc.pid, "running": (proc.poll() is None)}
    return statuses

# /root/ASASANAT1/src/bot/api/main.py
from fastapi import FastAPI
from src.bot.api.router import router as api_router
from src.bot.panel.router import router as panel_router
from src.company.api.router import router as company_router
from src.news.api.router import router as news_router
from src.api.routers import admin_router, job_router  # اگر اینها در src/api/routers تعریف شده‌اند

app = FastAPI(title="AsaSanat Bot API", version="1.0.0")

# --- APIهای داخلی ---
app.include_router(api_router, prefix="/api", tags=["api"])

# --- پنل ادمین HTML ---
app.include_router(panel_router, prefix="/panel", tags=["panel"])

# --- مدیریت شرکت‌ها ---
app.include_router(company_router, prefix="/company", tags=["company"])

# --- مدیریت خبرها ---
app.include_router(news_router, prefix="/news", tags=["news"])

# --- مدیریت ادمین و jobها ---
app.include_router(admin_router, prefix="/admin", tags=["admin"])
app.include_router(job_router, prefix="/jobs", tags=["jobs"])


@app.get("/")
def root():
    return {
        "service": "AsaSanat Bot API",
        "version": "1.0.0",
        "routers": [
            "/api",
            "/panel",
            "/company",
            "/news",
            "/admin",
            "/jobs",
        ],
    }

#/root/ASASANAT1/src/bot/api/router.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Header
from typing import Optional

from ..utils.security import require_api_key
from ..utils.db import add_crawler_log, add_sender_log, upsert_post

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api", tags=["api"])

@router.post("/report/crawler")
def report_crawler(level: str, message: str, source: Optional[str] = None, x_api_key: Optional[str] = Header(default=None)):
    require_api_key(x_api_key)
    add_crawler_log(level=level, message=message, source=source)
    return {"ok": True}

@router.post("/report/sender")
def report_sender(level: str, message: str, channel: Optional[str] = None, post_id: Optional[str] = None, x_api_key: Optional[str] = Header(default=None)):
    require_api_key(x_api_key)
    add_sender_log(level=level, message=message, channel=channel, post_id=post_id)
    return {"ok": True}

@router.post("/posts/upsert")
def posts_upsert(status: str, external_id: Optional[str] = None, title: Optional[str] = None, error: Optional[str] = None, x_api_key: Optional[str] = Header(default=None)):
    require_api_key(x_api_key)
    upsert_post(external_id=external_id, title=title, status=status, error=error)
    return {"ok": True}

from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
import os
from typing import Optional
from pathlib import Path
import asyncio
import logging

from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, Header, HTTPException
from aiogram import Bot, Dispatcher
from aiogram.client.default import DefaultBotProperties
from aiogram.enums import ParseMode
from aiogram.types import Update, Message
from aiogram.fsm.storage.memory import MemoryStorage
from aiogram.exceptions import TelegramRetryAfter

from .menus.handlers import register_menu_handlers
from .utils.commands import set_bot_commands
from .utils.config import ensure_data_dir
from .utils.db import create_tables

from .api.router import router as api_router
from .panel.router import router as admin_router

from src.company.api.router import router as company_router
from src.news.api.router import router as news_router

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

env_path = find_dotenv(usecwd=True)
if env_path and Path(env_path).exists():
    load_dotenv(env_path, override=True)

BOT_TOKEN = os.getenv("bot_token")
WEBHOOK_HOST = os.getenv("WEBHOOK_HOST", "").rstrip("/")
WEBHOOK_PATH = os.getenv("WEBHOOK_PATH", "/webhook")
WEBHOOK_URL = f"{WEBHOOK_HOST}{WEBHOOK_PATH}"
WEBHOOK_SECRET_TOKEN = os.getenv("WEBHOOK_SECRET_TOKEN", "")
DROP_PENDING_UPDATES = os.getenv("DROP_PENDING_UPDATES", "true").lower() == "true"

if not BOT_TOKEN:
    raise RuntimeError("❌ bot_token در محیط تنظیم نشده است")
if not WEBHOOK_HOST.startswith("https://"):
    raise RuntimeError("❌ WEBHOOK_HOST باید با https شروع شود")

bot = Bot(token=BOT_TOKEN, default=DefaultBotProperties(parse_mode=ParseMode.HTML))
dp = Dispatcher(storage=MemoryStorage())
register_menu_handlers(dp)

app = FastAPI(title="Telegram Bot Webhook + Admin Panel")
app.state.bot = bot
app.state.dp = dp

app.include_router(company_router)
app.include_router(news_router)
app.include_router(api_router)
app.include_router(admin_router)

@app.on_event("startup")
async def on_startup():
    ensure_data_dir()
    create_tables()

    try:
        await bot.set_webhook(
            url=WEBHOOK_URL,
            secret_token=WEBHOOK_SECRET_TOKEN or None,
            drop_pending_updates=DROP_PENDING_UPDATES,
            allowed_updates=[
                "message",
                "edited_message",
                "channel_post",
                "edited_channel_post",
                "callback_query",
                "inline_query",
                "chosen_inline_result",
                "poll",
                "poll_answer",
                "my_chat_member",
                "chat_member"
            ]
        )
        try:
            await set_bot_commands(bot)
        except TelegramRetryAfter as e:
            logger.warning(f"⚠️ Flood control: retry after {e.retry_after} sec. Skipping set_my_commands.")
        except Exception as ex:
            logger.error(f"⚠️ Failed to set bot commands: {ex}")

        logger.info(f"✅ Webhook set: {WEBHOOK_URL}")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"❌ Failed to set webhook: {e}")

    logger.info("📡 News pipeline ready (disabled by default)")

@app.on_event("shutdown")
async def on_shutdown():
    try:
        await bot.delete_webhook()
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"⚠️ Failed to delete webhook: {e}")
    try:
        await bot.session.close()
    except Exception:
        pass
    logger.info("🛑 Webhook deleted and bot session closed")

@app.get(WEBHOOK_PATH)
def webhook_get():
    return {"status": "Webhook endpoint is POST-only"}

@app.post(WEBHOOK_PATH)
async def telegram_webhook(
    request: Request,
    x_telegram_bot_api_secret_token: Optional[str] = Header(default=None)
):
    if WEBHOOK_SECRET_TOKEN and x_telegram_bot_api_secret_token != WEBHOOK_SECRET_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Invalid secret token")

    payload = await request.json()
    update = Update.model_validate(payload, context={"bot": bot})
    await dp.feed_update(bot, update)
    return {"ok": True}

@app.get("/panel")
def panel_status():
    return {"webhook": WEBHOOK_URL}

@dp.message()
async def echo_handler(message: Message):
    if message.text and not message.text.startswith("/"):
        logger.info(f"📌 CHAT_ID={message.chat.id}, USER_ID={message.from_user.id}")
    await message.answer(f"شما گفتید: {message.text}")

# /src/bot/menus/handlers.py
import os
import math
import logging
from src import logger_setup

from aiogram import types, Dispatcher, F
from aiogram.fsm.context import FSMContext
from aiogram.fsm.state import StatesGroup, State
from aiogram.types import MenuButtonDefault, InlineKeyboardMarkup, InlineKeyboardButton
from aiogram.filters import CommandStart, Command
from sqlalchemy import or_, func

from .keyboards import build_keyboard
from ..utils.commands import set_bot_commands
from src.db.session import SessionLocal
from src.db.models import Post
from src.services import repository  # توابع علاقه‌مندی و کوئری‌ها

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# --- تنظیمات ---
PAGE_SIZE = 10
admin_chat_id = int(os.getenv("adminchat_id", "0"))
SUPPORT_CONTACT = os.getenv("SUPPORT_CONTACT", "تماس: 0912xxxxxxx")


# --- ابزار ---
def is_admin_chat(message: types.Message) -> bool:
    return bool(message.chat and message.chat.id == admin_chat_id)

async def _safe_ack(call: types.CallbackQuery):
    try:
        await call.answer(cache_time=0, show_alert=False)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.debug("call.answer ignored error: %r", e)

def _shorten(s: str, n: int = 180) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip().replace("\r", " ").replace("\n", " ")
    return s if len(s) <= n else (s[: n - 1] + "…")


# --- دستورات پایه ---
async def start_command(message: types.Message):
    await message.answer("سلام! به ربات ASASANAT خوش اومدی 🚀", reply_markup=build_keyboard())

async def help_command(message: types.Message):
    await message.answer(
        "دستورات:\n"
        "/start — شروع و نمایش منو\n"
        "/menu — نمایش منوی فعلی\n"
        "/help — راهنما\n"
        "/about — درباره ما\n"
        "/resetmenu — ریست منو (ادمین)"
    )

async def about_command(message: types.Message):
    await message.answer("ASASANAT — دستیار کاریابی و مدیریت آگهی‌ها. نسخه: 1.0")

async def show_menu(message: types.Message):
    await message.answer("منوی فعلی:", reply_markup=build_keyboard())

async def reset_menu_handler(message: types.Message):
    if not is_admin_chat(message):
        await message.answer("⛔️ دسترسی غیرمجاز.")
        return
    bot = message.bot
    await bot.delete_my_commands()
    await bot.set_chat_menu_button(menu_button=MenuButtonDefault())
    await set_bot_commands(bot)
    await message.answer("✅ منو و دستورات به‌روز شدند.", reply_markup=build_keyboard())


# --- FSM States ---
class PostJobStates(StatesGroup):
    title       = State()
    description = State()
    confirm     = State()

class SearchStates(StatesGroup):
    query = State()


# --- کال‌بک منو ---
async def menu_callback(call: types.CallbackQuery, state: FSMContext):
    await _safe_ack(call)
    raw = call.data or ""
    logger.info("callback data = %r", raw)

    try:
        if not raw.startswith("menu:"):
            return

        action = raw.split("menu:", 1)[1]

        # 🔍 جستجوی شغل
        if action == "search_jobs":
            await call.message.answer("🔍 لطفاً عنوان شغل را وارد کن:")
            await state.set_state(SearchStates.query)

        # 📝 ثبت آگهی
        elif action == "post_job":
            await state.clear()
            await call.message.answer("📝 عنوان آگهی را وارد کن:")
            await state.set_state(PostJobStates.title)

        # ❤️ علاقه‌مندی‌ها
        elif action == "favorites":
            await _send_favorites(call, page=1)

        # 📂 مدیریت آگهی‌ها (فعلاً همان علاقه‌مندی‌ها)
        elif action == "manage_jobs":
            await _send_favorites(call, page=1)

        # 📊 آمار بازار کار
        elif action == "stats":
            await call.message.answer("📊 آمار بازار کار در حال آماده‌سازی است.")

        # 💳 تعرفه و پرداخت
        elif action == "pricing":
            text = (
                "💳 تعرفه و پرداخت:\n"
                "— طرح پایه: 199,000 تومان/ماه\n"
                "— طرح حرفه‌ای: 499,000 تومان/ماه\n"
                "— طرح سازمانی: سفارشی\n\n"
                f"{SUPPORT_CONTACT}"
            )
            await call.message.answer(text)

        # 📞 پشتیبانی
        elif action == "support":
            await call.message.answer(f"📞 پشتیبانی:\n{SUPPORT_CONTACT}")

        # بازگشت به منوی اصلی
        elif action == "root":
            await call.message.answer("منوی فعلی:", reply_markup=build_keyboard())

        # پیش‌فرض
        else:
            await call.message.answer(f"⚠️ دکمه «{action}» هنوز پیاده‌سازی نشده است.")

    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception("menu_callback error: %s", e)
        await call.message.answer("⚠️ خطایی رخ داد. لطفاً دوباره تلاش کنید.")


# --- علاقه‌مندی‌ها ---
def _fav_list_keyboard(page: int, total: int) -> InlineKeyboardMarkup:
    total_pages = max(1, math.ceil(total / PAGE_SIZE))
    page = max(1, min(page, total_pages))

    buttons = []

    # ردیف ناوبری
    nav_row = []
    if page > 1:
        nav_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text="⬅️ قبلی", callback_data=f"fav:list:{page-1}"))
    # نشانگر صفحه (دکمه غیرفعال: با noop)
    nav_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text=f"{page}/{total_pages}", callback_data="noop"))
    if page < total_pages:
        nav_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text="بعدی ➡️", callback_data=f"fav:list:{page+1}"))
    if nav_row:
        buttons.append(nav_row)

    # برگشت به منوی اصلی
    buttons.append([InlineKeyboardButton(text="🏠 منوی اصلی", callback_data="menu:root")])

    return InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=buttons)

async def fav_toggle(call: types.CallbackQuery):
    await _safe_ack(call)
    try:
        _, _, post_id_str = (call.data or "").split(":", 2)
        post_id = int(post_id_str)
    except Exception:
        await call.answer("شناسه نامعتبر", show_alert=False)
        return

    user_id = call.from_user.id
    added = repository.toggle_favorite(user_id, post_id)
    msg = "✅ به علاقه‌مندی‌ها اضافه شد" if added else "❌ از علاقه‌مندی‌ها حذف شد"
    await call.answer(msg, show_alert=False)

async def fav_list_paged(call: types.CallbackQuery):
    await _safe_ack(call)
    try:
        page = int((call.data or "").split(":")[-1])
        if page < 1:
            page = 1
    except Exception:
        page = 1
    await _send_favorites(call, page)

async def _send_favorites(call: types.CallbackQuery, page: int):
    user_id = call.from_user.id
    total = repository.count_favorites(user_id)
    if total == 0:
        await call.message.answer("❤️ هنوز موردی در علاقه‌مندی‌ها نداری.")
        return

    items = repository.list_favorites(user_id, limit=PAGE_SIZE, offset=(page-1)*PAGE_SIZE)
    lines = []
    for p in items:
        serial = p.get("serial_code") or "-"
        title  = (p.get("title") or "").strip()
        snippet = _shorten(title or (p.get("processed_text") or p.get("raw_text") or ""))
        lines.append(f"• {serial}\n{snippet}")

    text = "علاقه‌مندی‌ها:\n\n" + "\n\n".join(lines)
    kb = _fav_list_keyboard(page=page, total=total)
    try:
        await call.message.edit_text(text, reply_markup=kb)
    except Exception:
        await call.message.answer(text, reply_markup=kb)


# --- جستجو ---
async def search_handle_query(message: types.Message, state: FSMContext):
    q_raw = (message.text or "").strip()
    if not q_raw:
        await message.answer("🔍 عبارت جستجو خالی است. لطفاً متن بنویس.")
        return

    q = q_raw.lower()
    try:
        with SessionLocal() as db:
            rows = (
                db.query(Post)
                .filter(
                    or_(
                        func.lower(Post.title).like(f"%{q}%"),
                        func.lower(Post.processed_text).like(f"%{q}%"),
                        func.lower(Post.raw_text).like(f"%{q}%"),
                    )
                )
                .order_by(Post.created_at.desc())
                .limit(PAGE_SIZE)
                .all()
            )
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception("DB search error: %s", e)
        await message.answer("⚠️ خطا در جستجو. بعداً دوباره تلاش کن.")
        await state.clear()
        return

    if not rows:
        await message.answer("⚠️ موردی یافت نشد. عبارت دیگری امتحان کن.")
        await state.clear()
        return

    lines = []
    for p in rows:
        title = (p.title or "").strip()
        body  = (p.processed_text or p.raw_text or "").strip()
        snippet = _shorten(title or body)
        source = getattr(p, "source_channel", "") or "-"
        jdate  = getattr(p, "jalali_date", "") or "-"
        serial = getattr(p, "serial_code", "") or "-"
        lines.append(f"• {serial}\n{snippet}\nکانال: {source} | تاریخ: {jdate}")

    await message.answer("نتایج اخیر:\n\n" + "\n\n".join(lines))
    await state.clear()


# --- FSM ثبت آگهی ---
async def cancel_if_command(message: types.Message, state: FSMContext) -> bool:
    if message.text and message.text.startswith("/"):
        await state.clear()
        await message.answer("⛔️ فرآیند ثبت آگهی لغو شد.")
        return True
    return False

async def post_job_title(message: types.Message, state: FSMContext):
    if await cancel_if_command(message, state):
        return
    text = (message.text or "").strip()
    if not text:
        await message.answer("⚠️ عنوان خالی است. لطفاً دوباره وارد کن:")
        return
    await state.update_data(title=text)
    await message.answer("✅ عنوان ثبت شد. توضیحات آگهی را وارد کن:")
    await state.set_state(PostJobStates.description)

async def post_job_description(message: types.Message, state: FSMContext):
    if await cancel_if_command(message, state):
        return
    text = (message.text or "").strip()
    if not text:
        await message.answer("⚠️ توضیحات خالی است. لطفاً دوباره وارد کن:")
        return
    await state.update_data(description=text)
    data = await state.get_data()
    preview = (
        f"📋 پیش‌نمایش آگهی:\n"
        f"عنوان: {data.get('title', '-')}\n"
        f"توضیحات: {data.get('description', '-')}\n\n"
        "برای تایید «تایید» بنویس یا با هر دستور / فرآیند را لغو کن."
    )
    await message.answer(preview)
    await state.set_state(PostJobStates.confirm)

async def post_job_confirm(message: types.Message, state: FSMContext):
    if await cancel_if_command(message, state):
        return
    text = (message.text or "").strip().lower()
    if text in ("تایید", "تاييد", "yes", "ok", "okay", "confirm"):
        # در صورت نیاز می‌تونی اینجا ذخیره‌سازی در DB را اضافه کنی
        await message.answer("🎉 آگهی شما ثبت شد.")
    else:
        await message.answer("⛔️ تایید نشد.")
    await state.clear()


# --- هندلرهای کمکی ---
async def noop_handler(call: types.CallbackQuery):
    # فقط برای دکمه‌های نمایشی مثل نشانگر صفحه
    await _safe_ack(call)


# --- ثبت هندلرها ---
def register_menu_handlers(dp: Dispatcher):
    # دستورات پایه
    dp.message.register(start_command, CommandStart())
    dp.message.register(help_command,  Command("help"))
    dp.message.register(about_command, Command("about"))
    dp.message.register(show_menu,     Command("menu"))
    dp.message.register(reset_menu_handler, Command("resetmenu"))

    # کال‌بک منو
    dp.callback_query.register(menu_callback, F.data.startswith("menu:"))

    # علاقه‌مندی‌ها
    dp.callback_query.register(fav_toggle, F.data.startswith("fav:toggle:"))
    dp.callback_query.register(fav_list_paged, F.data.startswith("fav:list:"))

    # دکمه‌های نمایشی
    dp.callback_query.register(noop_handler, F.data == "noop")

    # جستجو
    dp.message.register(search_handle_query, SearchStates.query)

    # FSM آگهی
    dp.message.register(post_job_title,       PostJobStates.title)
    dp.message.register(post_job_description, PostJobStates.description)
    dp.message.register(post_job_confirm,     PostJobStates.confirm)



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/bot/menus/keyboards.py
########################################################################################################################

# /app/src/bot/menus/keyboards.py
import os
import json
import logging
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from aiogram.types import InlineKeyboardMarkup, InlineKeyboardButton
from src import logger_setup

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

MENU_JSON_PATH = os.getenv(
    "MENU_JSON_PATH",
    "/app/src/bot/data/menu.json"
)

DEFAULT_MENU_SPEC: List[List[Dict[str, str]]] = [
    [
        {"text": "🔍 جستجوی شغل", "callback_data": "menu:search_jobs"},
        {"text": "📝 ثبت آگهی",   "callback_data": "menu:post_job"},
    ],
    [
        {"text": "❤️ علاقه‌مندی‌ها", "callback_data": "menu:favorites"},
        {"text": "📂 مدیریت آگهی‌ها", "callback_data": "menu:manage_jobs"},
    ],
    [
        {"text": "📊 آمار بازار کار", "callback_data": "menu:stats"},
    ],
    [
        {"text": "💳 تعرفه و پرداخت", "callback_data": "menu:pricing"},
    ],
    [
        {"text": "📞 پشتیبانی", "callback_data": "menu:support"},
    ],
]

def _ensure_menu_file():
    try:
        os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(MENU_JSON_PATH), exist_ok=True)
        if not os.path.isfile(MENU_JSON_PATH):
            with open(MENU_JSON_PATH, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                json.dump({"rows": DEFAULT_MENU_SPEC, "version": 2}, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
            logger.info("✅ Default menu.json created at %s", MENU_JSON_PATH)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning("⚠️ Failed to create default menu.json: %s", e)

def _load_menu_spec() -> List[List[Dict[str, str]]]:
    _ensure_menu_file()
    try:
        with open(MENU_JSON_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            data = json.load(f)
        if isinstance(data, dict) and "rows" in data and isinstance(data["rows"], list):
            data = data["rows"]
        if isinstance(data, list) and all(isinstance(row, list) for row in data):
            for row in data:
                for btn in row:
                    if not isinstance(btn, dict):
                        raise ValueError("Invalid button type")
                    if "text" not in btn:
                        raise ValueError("Button missing 'text'")
                    if not ("callback_data" in btn or "data" in btn or "url" in btn):
                        raise ValueError("Button needs 'callback_data', 'data', or 'url'")
            logger.info("✅ Menu loaded from %s with %d rows", MENU_JSON_PATH, len(data))
            return data
        else:
            raise ValueError("Menu JSON must be a 2D list")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning("⚠️ Menu JSON load failed (%s). Using default menu.", e)
    logger.info("ℹ️ Menu loaded with %d rows (default)", len(DEFAULT_MENU_SPEC))
    return DEFAULT_MENU_SPEC

def build_keyboard(spec: List[List[Dict[str, Any]]] | None = None) -> InlineKeyboardMarkup:
    spec = spec or _load_menu_spec()
    rows = []
    for row in spec:
        buttons = []
        for b in row:
            text = str(b.get("text", "")).strip()
            cb   = b.get("callback_data") or b.get("data")
            url  = b.get("url")
            if not text:
                continue
            if url:
                buttons.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text=text, url=url))
            else:
                buttons.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text=text, callback_data=str(cb or "")))
        if buttons:
            rows.append(buttons)
    return InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=rows)

#/root/ASASANAT1/src/bot/panel/admin.py
@router.get("/stats")
def get_stats(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
    total_posts = db.query(Post).count()
    sent_posts = db.query(Post).filter(Post.status == "sent").count()
    failed_posts = db.query(Post).filter(Post.status == "failed").count()
    success_rate = (sent_posts / total_posts * 100) if total_posts else 0
    return {
        "total_posts": total_posts,
        "sent_posts": sent_posts,
        "failed_posts": failed_posts,
        "success_rate": round(success_rate, 2)
    }

#/root/ASASANAT1/src/bot/panel/api.py

from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, Header, HTTPException, Body
from pydantic import BaseModel
from datetime import datetime
from ..utils.db import SessionLocal, CrawlerLog, SenderLog, Post
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
from pathlib import Path

env_path = find_dotenv(usecwd=True)
if env_path and Path(env_path).exists():
    load_dotenv(env_path, override=True)

router = APIRouter(tags=["Report"])

API_KEY = os.getenv("PANEL_API_KEY", "dev-key")
def require_api_key(x_api_key: str = Header(...)):
    if x_api_key != API_KEY:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid API key")


# 1) مدل Pydantic برای بادی لاگ
class LogPayload(BaseModel):
    worker: str
    level: str
    message: str

@router.post("/log")
def report_log(
    payload: LogPayload,
    _: bool = Depends(require_api_key)
):
    """ثبت یک لاگ عمومی"""
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        if payload.worker.lower() == "crawler":
            db.add(CrawlerLog(
                level=payload.level,
                message=payload.message,
                source=payload.worker
            ))
        else:
            db.add(SenderLog(
                level=payload.level,
                message=payload.message,
                channel=payload.worker
            ))
        db.commit()
    return {"ok": True}


# 2) مدل Pydantic برای وضعیت پست
class PostStatusPayload(BaseModel):
    post_id: int
    status: str
    error: str | None = None

@router.post("/post_status")
def report_post_status(
    payload: PostStatusPayload,
    _: bool = Depends(require_api_key)
):
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        post = db.query(Post).filter(Post.id == payload.post_id).first()
        if post:
            post.status = payload.status
            post.error = payload.error
            post.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()
            db.commit()
    return {"ok": True}


# 3) مدل Pydantic برای heartbeat
class HeartbeatPayload(BaseModel):
    worker: str

@router.post("/heartbeat")
def report_heartbeat(
    payload: HeartbeatPayload,
    _: bool = Depends(require_api_key)
):
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        db.add(CrawlerLog(
            level="HEARTBEAT",
            message="alive",
            source=payload.worker
        ))
        db.commit()
    return {"ok": True}

function table(list, cols){
  let h = '<table><thead><tr>'+cols.map(c=>`<th>${c}</th>`).join('')+'</tr></thead><tbody>';
  for(const row of list){ h += '<tr>'+cols.map(c=>`<td>${row[c]??''}</td>`).join('')+'</tr>'; }
  return h + '</tbody></table>';
}

@router.get("/api/stats")
def admin_stats(_: bool = Depends(require_basic_auth)):
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        posts_total = db.query(Post).count()
        posts_sent = db.query(Post).filter(Post.status == "sent").count()
        posts_failed = db.query(Post).filter(Post.status == "failed").count()
        crawler_cnt = db.query(CrawlerLog).count()
        sender_cnt = db.query(SenderLog).count()
    return {
        "posts": {"total": posts_total, "sent": posts_sent, "failed": posts_failed},
        "logs": {"crawler": crawler_cnt, "sender": sender_cnt},
    }

@router.get("/api/logs")
def admin_logs(type: str, limit: int = 50, _: bool = Depends(require_basic_auth)):
    limit = max(1, min(limit, 200))
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        if type == "crawler":
            q = db.query(CrawlerLog).order_by(CrawlerLog.id.desc()).limit(limit).all()
            items = [dict(id=o.id, timestamp=o.timestamp, level=o.level, source=o.source, message=o.message) for o in q]
        elif type == "sender":
            q = db.query(SenderLog).order_by(SenderLog.id.desc()).limit(limit).all()
            items = [dict(id=o.id, timestamp=o.timestamp, level=o.level, channel=o.channel, post_id=o.post_id, message=o.message) for o in q]
        else:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="type must be crawler or sender")
    return {"items": items}

@router.get("/api/posts")
def admin_posts(limit: int = 50, _: bool = Depends(require_basic_auth)):
    limit = max(1, min(limit, 200))
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        q = db.query(Post).order_by(Post.id.desc()).limit(limit).all()
        items = [dict(
            id=o.id, external_id=o.external_id, title=o.title, status=o.status,
            error=o.error, created_at=o.created_at, updated_at=o.updated_at
        ) for o in q]
    return {"items": items}

# --- کنترل Jobها ---
@router.get("/api/jobs/status")
def admin_jobs_status(_: bool = Depends(require_basic_auth)):
    statuses = {}
    for job, proc in job_router.running_jobs.items():
        statuses[job] = {"pid": proc.pid, "running": (proc.poll() is None)}
    for job in job_router.JOB_COMMANDS.keys():
        if job not in statuses:
            statuses[job] = {"pid": None, "running": False}
    return statuses

# /root/ASASANAT1/src/bot/utils/commands.py
from aiogram import Bot
from aiogram.types import BotCommand
from aiogram.exceptions import TelegramRetryAfter

async def set_bot_commands(bot: Bot):
    fa_commands = [
        BotCommand(command="start", description="شروع و نمایش منو"),
        BotCommand(command="menu", description="نمایش منوی فعلی"),
        BotCommand(command="help", description="راهنما"),
        BotCommand(command="about", description="درباره ما"),
    ]
    try:
        await bot.set_my_commands(fa_commands, language_code="fa")
    except TelegramRetryAfter as e:
        print(f"⚠️ Flood control: retry after {e.retry_after} sec. Skipping set_my_commands.")
    except Exception as ex:
        print(f"⚠️ Failed to set bot commands: {ex}")

#src/bot/utils/config.py
import json
import os
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Literal, Optional, Tuple
from pathlib import Path

BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))  # src/bot
DATA_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "data")  # src/bot/data
MENU_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "menu.json")

USE_NEW_MENU = True

MenuButtonType = Literal["url", "callback"]
MenuItem = Dict[str, Any]

DEFAULT_MENU = {
  "rows": [
    [
      {"text": "🔍 جستجوی شغل", "type": "callback", "data": "menu:search_jobs"},
      {"text": "📝 ثبت آگهی",   "type": "callback", "data": "menu:post_job"}
    ],
    [
      {"text": "❤️ علاقه‌مندی‌ها", "type": "callback", "data": "menu:favorites"},
      {"text": "📂 مدیریت آگهی‌ها", "type": "callback", "data": "menu:manage_jobs"}
    ],
    [
      {"text": "📊 آمار بازار کار", "type": "callback", "data": "menu:stats"}
    ],
    [
      {"text": "💳 تعرفه و پرداخت", "type": "callback", "data": "menu:pricing"}
    ],
    [
      {"text": "📞 پشتیبانی", "type": "callback", "data": "menu:support"}
    ]
  ],
  "version": 2
}

def ensure_data_dir() -> None:
    if not os.path.isdir(DATA_DIR):
        os.makedirs(DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)

def validate_menu(menu: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:
    if not isinstance(menu, dict):
        return False, "Menu must be a JSON object"
    if "rows" not in menu or not isinstance(menu["rows"], list):
        return False, "Menu must have 'rows' as a list"
    for r_idx, row in enumerate(menu["rows"]):
        if not isinstance(row, list):
            return False, f"Row {r_idx} must be a list"
        for c_idx, btn in enumerate(row):
            if not isinstance(btn, dict):
                return False, f"Button at row {r_idx} col {c_idx} must be an object"
            if "text" not in btn or not isinstance(btn["text"], str) or not btn["text"].strip():
                return False, f"Button at row {r_idx} col {c_idx} missing 'text'"
            if btn.get("type") not in ("url", "callback"):
                return False, f"Button at row {r_idx} col {c_idx} invalid 'type'"
            if btn["type"] == "url" and ("data" not in btn or not str(btn["data"]).startswith(("http://", "https://"))):
                return False, f"URL button at row {r_idx} col {c_idx} must have valid 'data' as URL"
            if btn["type"] == "callback" and ("data" not in btn or not isinstance(btn["data"], str)):
                return False, f"Callback button at row {r_idx} col {c_idx} must have 'data' string"
    return True, None

def load_menu() -> Dict[str, Any]:
    ensure_data_dir()
    if not os.path.isfile(MENU_FILE):
        save_menu(DEFAULT_MENU)
        return DEFAULT_MENU
    try:
        with open(MENU_FILE, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            menu = json.load(f)
        ok, err = validate_menu(menu)
        if not ok:
            raise ValueError(err or "Invalid menu schema")
        return menu
    except Exception:
        # fallback
        save_menu(DEFAULT_MENU)
        return DEFAULT_MENU

def save_menu(menu: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    ensure_data_dir()
    ok, err = validate_menu(menu)
    if not ok:
        raise ValueError(err or "Invalid menu")
    with open(MENU_FILE, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(menu, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

#src/bot/utils/db.py
import os
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional

from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, String, Text, DateTime
from sqlalchemy.orm import declarative_base, sessionmaker

from .config import DATA_DIR

DB_PATH = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "app.db")
ENGINE = create_engine(f"sqlite:///{DB_PATH}", connect_args={"check_same_thread": False})
SessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=ENGINE, autocommit=False, autoflush=False)
Base = declarative_base()

# جداول
class CrawlerLog(Base):
    __tablename__ = "crawler_logs"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, index=True)
    level = Column(String(20), default="INFO", index=True)
    message = Column(Text, nullable=False)
    source = Column(String(100), nullable=True)

class SenderLog(Base):
    __tablename__ = "sender_logs"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, index=True)
    level = Column(String(20), default="INFO", index=True)
    message = Column(Text, nullable=False)
    channel = Column(String(100), nullable=True)
    post_id = Column(String(100), nullable=True)

class Post(Base):
    __tablename__ = "posts"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    external_id = Column(String(100), nullable=True, index=True)  # آیدی بیرونی/مرجع
    title = Column(String(255), nullable=True)
    status = Column(String(50), default="pending", index=True)    # pending/sent/failed/queued/...
    error = Column(Text, nullable=True)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, index=True)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)

def create_tables():
    os.makedirs(DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    Base.metadata.create_all(ENGINE)

# Helperهای درج
def add_crawler_log(level: str, message: str, source: Optional[str] = None):
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        db.add(CrawlerLog(level=level, message=message, source=source))
        db.commit()

def add_sender_log(level: str, message: str, channel: Optional[str] = None, post_id: Optional[str] = None):
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        db.add(SenderLog(level=level, message=message, channel=channel, post_id=post_id))
        db.commit()

def upsert_post(external_id: Optional[str], title: Optional[str], status: str, error: Optional[str] = None):
    with SessionLocal() as db:
        obj = None
        if external_id:
            obj = db.query(Post).filter(Post.external_id == external_id).first()
        if not obj:
            obj = Post(external_id=external_id, title=title, status=status, error=error)
            db.add(obj)
        else:
            obj.title = title or obj.title
            obj.status = status
            obj.error = error
            obj.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()
        db.commit()

#root/ASASANAT1/src/bot/utils/reporter.py
import os
import logging
import requests
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
from src import logger_setup

# بارگذاری .env در همه پروسه‌ها
env_path = find_dotenv(usecwd=True)
if env_path and Path(env_path).exists():
    load_dotenv(env_path, override=True)

logger = logging.getLogger("bot.utils.reporter")


API_BASE = os.getenv("PANEL_API_BASE", "http://localhost:8000/admin/api/report")
API_KEY  = os.getenv("PANEL_API_KEY", "dev-key")

HEADERS = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "X-API-Key": API_KEY,
}


def report_log(worker: str, message: str, level: str = "INFO") -> bool:
    """ثبت لاگ عمومی crawler یا sender"""
    try:
        resp = requests.post(
            f"{API_BASE}/log",
            headers=HEADERS,
            json={"worker": worker, "level": level, "message": message},
            timeout=3
        )
        if resp.status_code != 200:
            logger.error("report_log failed [%s]: %s – %s", resp.status_code, resp.text, message)
            return False

        logger.info("➔ report_log OK for %s: %s", worker, message)
        return True

    except requests.RequestException as exc:
        logger.exception("report_log exception for %s: %s", worker, exc)
        return False


def report_post_status(worker: str, post_id: int, status: str, error: str = None) -> bool:
    """ثبت وضعیت هر پست"""
    if not isinstance(post_id, int):
        # ignore non-integer post_id
        return False

    payload = {"worker": worker, "post_id": post_id, "status": status}
    if error:
        payload["error"] = error

    try:
        resp = requests.post(
            f"{API_BASE}/post_status",
            headers=HEADERS,
            json=payload,
            timeout=3
        )
        if resp.status_code != 200:
            logger.error("report_post_status failed [%s]: %s – %s", resp.status_code, resp.text, payload)
            return False

        logger.info("➔ report_post_status OK for %s:%d %s", worker, post_id, status)
        return True

    except requests.RequestException as exc:
        logger.exception("report_post_status exception for %s: %s", worker, exc)
        return False


def report_heartbeat(worker: str) -> bool:
    """ثبت heartbeat برای مانیتور زنده"""
    try:
        resp = requests.post(
            f"{API_BASE}/heartbeat",
            headers=HEADERS,
            json={"worker": worker},
            timeout=2
        )
        if resp.status_code != 200:
            logger.error("report_heartbeat failed [%s]: %s", resp.status_code, resp.text)
            return False
        logger.debug("➔ heartbeat OK for %s", worker)
        return True

    except requests.RequestException as exc:
        logger.exception("report_heartbeat exception for %s: %s", worker, exc)
        return False


class Reporter:
    def __init__(self, module: str):
        self.module = module

    def info(self, data: dict):
        # تبدیل dict به متن و ارسال به report_log
        msg = f"{data}"
        report_log(self.module, msg, level="INFO")

    def error(self, data: dict):
        msg = f"{data}"
        report_log(self.module, msg, level="ERROR")

    def debug(self, data: dict):
        msg = f"{data}"
        report_log(self.module, msg, level="DEBUG")

FILE: src/src/bot/utils/security.py
########################################################################################################################

import os
import secrets
from fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status
from fastapi.security import HTTPBasic, HTTPBasicCredentials
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv

env_path = find_dotenv(usecwd=True)
if env_path and Path(env_path).exists():
    load_dotenv(env_path, override=True)

security = HTTPBasic()

ADMIN_USER = os.getenv("ADMIN_USER", "admin")
ADMIN_PASS = os.getenv("ADMIN_PASS")
API_KEY = os.getenv("API_KEY")

def require_basic_auth(credentials: HTTPBasicCredentials = Depends(security)):
    correct_user = secrets.compare_digest(credentials.username, ADMIN_USER)
    correct_pass = ADMIN_PASS is not None and secrets.compare_digest(credentials.password, ADMIN_PASS)
    if not (correct_user and correct_pass):
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
            detail="Unauthorized",
            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Basic"},
        )
    return True

def require_api_key(key: str):
    if not API_KEY or not secrets.compare_digest(key or "", API_KEY):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid API key")

# src/company/api/router.py

from fastapi import APIRouter, Request, Form, HTTPException, Header, Body, Response, Cookie
from fastapi.responses import HTMLResponse, RedirectResponse, JSONResponse
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from src.company.db.session import SessionLocal
from src.company.db.models import CompanyStaging, Company
from src.company.pipeline.worker import import_staging
from src.company.runner import run_company_crawl
import os, hmac, time, html

API_TOKEN = os.getenv("COMPANY_API_TOKEN", "change-me")
SESSION_SECRET = os.getenv("COMPANY_SESSION_SECRET", "change-me-2")
SESSION_TTL_SEC = 3600

router = APIRouter(prefix="/company", tags=["company"])

def _constant_time_equal(a: str, b: str) -> bool:
    return hmac.compare_digest(a or "", b or "")

def auth(authorization: str = Header(None)):
    if not authorization or not authorization.startswith("Bearer "):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")
    token = authorization.split(" ", 1)[1]
    if not (API_TOKEN and _constant_time_equal(token, API_TOKEN)):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")

def _issue_session_cookie(resp: Response):
    ts = str(int(time.time()))
    sig = hmac.new(SESSION_SECRET.encode("utf-8"), ts.encode("utf-8"), "sha256").hexdigest()
    value = f"{ts}.{sig}"
    # HttpOnly + Secure (در dev ممکنه بدون HTTPS باشه؛ در prod حتما Secure=True)
    resp.set_cookie(
        "company_session",
        value,
        max_age=SESSION_TTL_SEC,
        httponly=True,
        secure=False,
        samesite="Strict",
        path="/company",
    )

def _verify_session_cookie(session_cookie: str | None):
    if not session_cookie:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")
    try:
        ts_str, sig = session_cookie.split(".", 1)
        ts = int(ts_str)
    except Exception:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")
    if (int(time.time()) - ts) > SESSION_TTL_SEC:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Session expired")
    expected = hmac.new(SESSION_SECRET.encode("utf-8"), ts_str.encode("utf-8"), "sha256").hexdigest()
    if not _constant_time_equal(sig, expected):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")

# --- Review page ---
@router.get("/review", response_class=HTMLResponse)
def review_page(response: Response, authorization: str = Header(None)):
    # احراز اولیه با Header، سپس صدور سشن کوکی برای ارسال فرم‌های بعدی بدون توکن
    auth(authorization)
    _issue_session_cookie(response)

    s: Session = SessionLocal()
    rows = s.query(CompanyStaging).filter(
        CompanyStaging.status.in_(["staged","needs_review","exported"])
    ).limit(50).all()
    s.close()

    html_out = "<h2>Company Review</h2><table border=1>"
    html_out += "<tr><th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Confidence</th><th>Action</th></tr>"
    for r in rows:
        parsed = r.parsed or {}
        name = html.escape(parsed.get('name') or "")
        conf = r.confidence if r.confidence is not None else 0.0
        html_out += f"<tr><td>{r.id}</td><td>{name}</td><td>{conf}</td>"
        # فرم بدون توکن در URL؛ سشن کوکی HttpOnly برای POST تأیید می‌شود
        html_out += (
            f"<td><form method='post' action='/company/review/{r.id}'>"
            "<button name='action' value='publish'>Publish</button>"
            "<button name='action' value='reject'>Reject</button></form></td></tr>"
        )
    html_out += "</table>"
    return HTMLResponse(content=html_out)

@router.post("/review/{staging_id}")
def review_action(
    staging_id: int,
    action: str = Form(...),
    company_session: str | None = Cookie(default=None)
):
    # تأیید سشن کوکی، بدون نیاز به توکن در URL یا Header
    _verify_session_cookie(company_session)
    if action == "publish":
        import_staging(staging_id, actor="admin")
    elif action == "reject":
        s: Session = SessionLocal()
        st = s.query(CompanyStaging).filter(CompanyStaging.id == staging_id).first()
        if st:
            st.status = "rejected"
            s.commit()
        s.close()
    else:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Invalid action")
    return RedirectResponse("/company/review", status_code=303)

# --- Crawl endpoint ---
@router.post("/crawl")
def crawl_endpoint(seed_urls: list[str] = Body(default=[]), authorization: str = Header(None)):
    auth(authorization)
    return run_company_crawl(seed_urls or ["https://example.com/contact"])

# --- Staging list ---
@router.get("/staging", response_class=HTMLResponse)
def staging_list(authorization: str = Header(None)):
    auth(authorization)
    s: Session = SessionLocal()
    rows = s.query(CompanyStaging).order_by(CompanyStaging.id.desc()).limit(50).all()
    s.close()
    html_out = "<h2>Company Staging (last 50)</h2><table border=1>"
    html_out += "<tr><th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Phones</th><th>City</th><th>Province</th><th>Confidence</th></tr>"
    for r in rows:
        p = r.parsed or {}
        name = html.escape(p.get('name') or "")
        phones = ";".join([html.escape(x) for x in (p.get("phones") or [])])
        city = html.escape(p.get('city') or "")
        province = html.escape(p.get('province') or "")
        conf = r.confidence if r.confidence is not None else 0.0
        html_out += f"<tr><td>{r.id}</td><td>{name}</td><td>{phones}</td><td>{city}</td><td>{province}</td><td>{conf}</td></tr>"
    html_out += "</table>"
    return HTMLResponse(content=html_out)

# --- Companies list ---
@router.get("/companies", response_class=HTMLResponse)
def companies_list(authorization: str = Header(None)):
    auth(authorization)
    s: Session = SessionLocal()
    rows = s.query(Company).order_by(Company.id.desc()).limit(50).all()
    s.close()
    html_out = "<h2>Companies (last 50)</h2><table border=1>"
    html_out += "<tr><th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Slug</th><th>Website</th><th>Phones</th><th>Verified</th></tr>"
    for c in rows:
        name = html.escape(c.name or "")
        slug = html.escape(c.slug or "")
        website = html.escape(c.website or "")
        phones = ";".join([html.escape(x) for x in (c.phones or [])])
        verified = '✅' if c.verified else '❌'
        html_out += f"<tr><td>{c.id}</td><td>{name}</td><td>{slug}</td><td>{website}</td><td>{phones}</td><td>{verified}</td></tr>"
    html_out += "</table>"
    return HTMLResponse(content=html_out)

# src/company/config.py

from dataclasses import dataclass
import os
MODEL_PRIMARY = os.getenv("COMPANY_MODEL_PRIMARY", "llama-3.1-8b-instant")
MODEL_FALLBACK = os.getenv("COMPANY_MODEL_FALLBACK", "llama-3.3-70b-versatile")


LIMITS = {
    "requests_per_minute": 30,
    "tokens_per_minute": 6000,
    "requests_per_day": 14400,
    "tokens_per_day": 500000
}


@dataclass
class SourceWeights:
    official: float = 1.0
    company_site: float = 0.95
    government: float = 1.0
    b2b: float = 0.6
    news: float = 0.7
    social: float = 0.4
    maps: float = 0.8

@dataclass
class Thresholds:
    auto_publish_conf: float = 0.85
    review_min_conf: float = 0.30
    phone_auto_conf: float = 0.90
    fuzzy_same: float = 0.90
    fuzzy_merge_candidate_min: float = 0.75
    proximity_meters: int = 100

@dataclass
class CrawlPolicy:
    per_host_rps: float = 0.5
    max_retries: int = 3
    backoff_base: float = 1.6
    user_agent: str = "Mozilla/5.0 (CompanyCrawler/1.0)"

SOURCE_WEIGHTS = SourceWeights()
THRESHOLDS = Thresholds()
CRAWL = CrawlPolicy()

-- src/company/db/migrations/001_init.sql

-- companies (main)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS companies (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  canonical_name TEXT,
  slug TEXT UNIQUE,
  industry TEXT,
  products JSONB,
  raw_materials JSONB,
  ceo TEXT,
  phones JSONB,
  emails JSONB,
  website TEXT,
  address TEXT,
  city TEXT,
  province TEXT,
  postal_code TEXT,
  location_lat DOUBLE PRECISION,
  location_lng DOUBLE PRECISION,
  established_year INT,
  staff_count INT,
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
  source_evidence JSONB,   -- [{field,value,url,source_type,confidence,fetched_at}]
  field_confidences JSONB, -- {"name":0.9,"phones":0.95,...}
  confidence DOUBLE PRECISION,
  verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()
);

-- companies_staging
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS companies_staging (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  raw_json JSONB,
  parsed JSONB,            -- normalized fields
  source_evidence JSONB,   -- list of sources
  field_confidences JSONB, -- per-field
  confidence DOUBLE PRECISION,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'staged', -- staged|needs_review|exported|imported|rejected
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()
);

-- company_audit
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS company_audit (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  company_id INT REFERENCES companies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  field_name TEXT,
  before JSONB,
  after JSONB,
  actor TEXT,             -- system/n8n/admin
  reason TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_companies_canonical ON companies (canonical_name);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_companies_city ON companies (province, city);

# src/company/db/models.py
from sqlalchemy.orm import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, Text, Float, String, JSON, Boolean
from sqlalchemy import DateTime, func

Base = declarative_base()

class Company(Base):
    __tablename__ = "companies"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    name = Column(Text, nullable=False)
    canonical_name = Column(Text, index=True)
    slug = Column(String, unique=True, index=True)
    industry = Column(Text)
    products = Column(JSON)       # list[str]
    raw_materials = Column(JSON)  # list[str]
    ceo = Column(Text)
    phones = Column(JSON)         # list[str] (normalized E.164)
    emails = Column(JSON)         # list[str]
    website = Column(Text)
    address = Column(Text)
    city = Column(Text)
    province = Column(Text)
    postal_code = Column(Text)
    location_lat = Column(Float)
    location_lng = Column(Float)
    established_year = Column(Integer)
    staff_count = Column(Integer)
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    source_evidence = Column(JSON)     # list[dict]
    field_confidences = Column(JSON)   # dict[str,float]
    confidence = Column(Float)
    verified = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=func.now())
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=func.now(), onupdate=func.now())

class CompanyStaging(Base):
    __tablename__ = "companies_staging"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    raw_json = Column(JSON)            # raw meta like sha1, path
    parsed = Column(JSON)              # parsed fields
    source_evidence = Column(JSON)     # list[dict]
    field_confidences = Column(JSON)   # dict[str,float]
    confidence = Column(Float)
    status = Column(String, default="staged", index=True)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=func.now())

class CompanyAudit(Base):
    __tablename__ = "company_audit"
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    company_id = Column(Integer, index=True)
    field_name = Column(Text)
    before = Column(JSON)
    after = Column(JSON)
    actor = Column(Text)
    reason = Column(Text)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=func.now())

# src/company/pipeline/agent.py
import os, requests, json, time, re, hashlib
from src.bot.utils.reporter import Reporter

rep = Reporter(module="company_agent")

GROQ_API_KEY = os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY", "")
GROQ_URL = "https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions"
MODEL_PRIMARY = os.getenv("COMPANY_MODEL_PRIMARY", "llama-3.1-8b-instant")
MODEL_FALLBACK = os.getenv("COMPANY_MODEL_FALLBACK", "llama-3.3-70b-versatile")

SYSTEM_PROMPT = (
    "اطلاعات شرکت را به صورت JSON ساختاریافته و فقط JSON خالص برگردان.\n"
    "فیلدها: name, canonical_name, ceo, phones, emails, website, address, city, province, postal_code, products, raw_materials.\n"
    "phones را E.164 و emails را لیست بده. اگر مطمئن نیستی، مقدار null بده."
)

def _headers():
    if not GROQ_API_KEY:
        raise RuntimeError("GROQ_API_KEY not set in env")
    return {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {GROQ_API_KEY}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

def _parse_json(content: str) -> dict:
    # تلاش برای یافتن JSON معتبر
    try:
        return json.loads(content)
    except Exception:
        m = re.search(r"```json\s*(\{.*?\})\s*```", content, re.DOTALL)
        if not m:
            m = re.search(r"(\{.*\})", content, re.DOTALL)
        if not m:
            # خروجی نامعتبر
            rep.warn({"event": "agent_nonjson"})
            return {}
        try:
            return json.loads(m.group(1))
        except Exception:
            rep.warn({"event": "agent_json_parse_fail"})
            return {}

def _cache_key(text: str) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha256((text or "").encode("utf-8", errors="ignore")).hexdigest()

_AGENT_CACHE: dict[str, dict] = {}
AGENT_TTL_SEC = 3600
AGENT_CACHE_MAX = int(os.getenv("COMPANY_AGENT_CACHE_MAX", "1000"))

def _cache_get(key: str):
    item = _AGENT_CACHE.get(key)
    if not item:
        return None
    if (time.time() - item.get("_ts", 0)) > AGENT_TTL_SEC:
        return None
    return item.get("data")

def _cache_set(key: str, data: dict):
    # محدودسازی اندازه کش
    if len(_AGENT_CACHE) >= AGENT_CACHE_MAX:
        # ساده: حذف قدیمی‌ترین آیتم
        oldest_key = min(_AGENT_CACHE.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1].get("_ts", 0))[0]
        _AGENT_CACHE.pop(oldest_key, None)
    _AGENT_CACHE[key] = {"_ts": time.time(), "data": data}

def call_groq_agent(prompt_text: str, model: str = None, timeout: int = 20) -> dict:
    if not GROQ_API_KEY:
        rep.debug({"event": "agent_skipped", "reason": "no_api_key"})
        return {}
    m = model or MODEL_PRIMARY
    key = _cache_key(f"{m}|{prompt_text}")
    cached = _cache_get(key)
    if cached is not None:
        return cached

    payload = {
        "model": m,
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt_text}
        ]
    }
    attempts = 0
    while attempts < 3:
        try:
            resp = requests.post(GROQ_URL, headers=_headers(), json=payload, timeout=timeout)
            if resp.status_code == 200:
                j = resp.json()
                content = j.get("choices", [{}])[0].get("message", {}).get("content", "")
                out = _parse_json(content)
                if out:
                    _cache_set(key, out)
                    return out
                else:
                    # خروجی نامعتبر؛ تلاش بعدی یا مدل fallback
                    rep.warn({"event": "agent_empty_or_invalid"})
                    attempts += 1
                    continue
            elif resp.status_code in (429, 500, 502, 503, 504):
                rep.error({"event": "agent_retry", "status": resp.status_code})
                time.sleep(1.5 * (attempts + 1))
                attempts += 1
            else:
                rep.error({"event": "agent_fail", "status": resp.status_code, "body": resp.text[:300]})
                if m != MODEL_FALLBACK:
                    m = MODEL_FALLBACK
                    payload["model"] = m
                    attempts += 1
                else:
                    break
        except Exception as e:
            rep.error({"event": "agent_exc", "error": str(e)})
            time.sleep(1.5 * (attempts + 1))
            attempts += 1
    return {}
