# src/company/pipeline/crawler.py

import os
import time
import asyncio
import signal
import uuid
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Tuple
from urllib.parse import urlparse

from src.bot.utils.reporter import Reporter
from src.company.pipeline.fetcher import fetch_url
from src.company.pipeline.fetcher_js import fetch_page_js
from src.company.pipeline.link_extractor import extract_profile_links, extract_pagination_links
from src.company.pipeline.profile_extractor import extract_profile

from src.company.pipeline.extractors import rule_based_extract, ai_extract_from_text
from src.company.pipeline.normalizers import (
    normalize_text, canonicalize_name, normalize_phone, unique_list
)
from src.company.pipeline.enrich import field_confidence, overall_confidence
from src.company.pipeline.raw_store import save_raw_html
from src.company.pipeline.staging import stage
from src.company.pipeline.validate import ParsedCompany
from src.company.pipeline.dedupe import same_by_phone, same_by_domain

# Reporter with run context
RUN_ID = os.getenv("COMPANY_RUN_ID") or uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]
rep = Reporter(module="company_crawler")

# --- Runtime control
STOP_REQUESTED = False
def _handle_stop(signum, frame):
    global STOP_REQUESTED
    STOP_REQUESTED = True
    rep.info({"event": "stop_requested", "signal": signum, "run_id": RUN_ID})

signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle_stop)
signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle_stop)


# --- Configurable limits (env or defaults)
def _envf(key: str, default: float) -> float:
    try:
        return float(os.getenv(key, str(default)))
    except Exception:
        return default

def _envi(key: str, default: int) -> int:
        try:
            return int(os.getenv(key, str(default)))
        except Exception:
            return default

AGENT_RPS = _envf("COMPANY_AGENT_RPS", 0.5)             # AI rate limit
HTML_MIN_LEN = _envi("COMPANY_HTML_MIN_LEN", 800)        # minimal html length to trust
JS_TIMEOUT_MS = _envi("COMPANY_JS_TIMEOUT_MS", 15000)    # JS render timeout

# Crawl scope limits
MAX_PAGES_DEFAULT = _envi("COMPANY_MAX_PAGES", 1)
MAX_PROFILE_LINKS_DEFAULT = _envi("COMPANY_MAX_PROFILE_LINKS", 5)
MAX_PROFILES_DEFAULT = _envi("COMPANY_MAX_PROFILES", 5)
REQUEST_DELAY_SEC_DEFAULT = _envf("COMPANY_REQUEST_DELAY_SEC", 0.8)

def _is_list_page(url: str) -> bool:
    u = url.lower()
    return ("business-center" in u) or ("search" in u) or ("directory" in u)

def _ai_safe(prompt_text: str) -> Dict:
    """
    AI extraction with resilient fallback and logging.
    Returns {} if AI is unavailable or fails; never raises.
    Respects AGENT_RPS.
    """
    if not prompt_text:
        return {}
    # rate-limit the agent
    time.sleep(max(1.0 / AGENT_RPS, 0.1))
    try:
        out = ai_extract_from_text(prompt_text) or {}
        if out:
            rep.info({"event": "ai_ok", "seed_text_len": len(prompt_text), "keys": list(out.keys()), "run_id": RUN_ID})
        else:
            rep.warn({"event": "ai_empty", "seed_text_len": len(prompt_text), "run_id": RUN_ID})
        return out
    except Exception as ae:
        rep.error({"event": "ai_error", "error": str(ae), "run_id": RUN_ID})
        return {}

def _merge_parsed(rb: Dict, ai: Dict) -> Dict:
    """
    Merge rule-based and AI outputs, prefer AI when non-null.
    """
    merged = {**rb}
    for k, v in ai.items():
        if v is not None:
            merged[k] = v
    return merged

def _normalize_enrich(url: str, parsed: Dict) -> Dict:
    """
    Normalize fields, validate pydantic; confidences are computed by caller.
    """
    parsed["name"] = normalize_text(parsed.get("name"))
    parsed["canonical_name"] = canonicalize_name(parsed.get("name"))
    parsed["phones"] = unique_list([p for p in (normalize_phone(x) for x in parsed.get("phones", [])) if p])

    # Pydantic light validation (non-fatal)
    try:
        parsed = ParsedCompany(**parsed).dict()
    except Exception as ve:
        rep.error({"event": "parsed_validation_failed", "url": url, "error": str(ve), "run_id": RUN_ID})
    return parsed

def _process_html(url: str, html: str) -> Dict:
    """
    Full process pipeline for a single HTML:
    - rule-based extraction
    - AI assist (safe)
    - merge
    - normalize + validate
    """
    rb = rule_based_extract(html, url)
    seed_text = rb.get("name") or rb.get("address") or rb.get("website") or url
    ai = _ai_safe(seed_text)
    parsed = _merge_parsed(rb, ai)
    parsed = _normalize_enrich(url, parsed)
    return parsed

def _fetch_with_js_fallback(url: str) -> Tuple[int, str, str]:
    """
    Fetch with HTML length check; if short or non-200, attempt JS render.
    Returns (status, html, mode) where mode is 'http' or 'js'.
    """
    status, html = fetch_url(url)
    mode = "http"
    if (status != 200 or not html or len(html) < HTML_MIN_LEN):
        try:
            html = asyncio.run(fetch_page_js(url, timeout_ms=JS_TIMEOUT_MS))
            status = 200 if html else status
            mode = "js"
            rep.info({"event": "js_render_used", "url": url, "len": len(html or ""), "run_id": RUN_ID})
        except Exception as e:
            rep.error({"event": "js_render_fail", "url": url, "error": str(e), "run_id": RUN_ID})
    return status, html or "", mode

def _dedupe_seen(parsed_list: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
    """
    Lightweight dedupe by phone/domain.
    """
    out: List[Dict] = []
    for cand in parsed_list:
        if not cand:
            continue
        dupe = False
        for prev in out:
            if same_by_phone(cand, prev) or same_by_domain(cand, prev):
                dupe = True
                break
        if not dupe:
            out.append(cand)
    return out

def crawl(
    seed_urls: List[str],
    max_pages: int = MAX_PAGES_DEFAULT,
    max_profile_links: int = MAX_PROFILE_LINKS_DEFAULT,
    max_profiles: int = MAX_PROFILES_DEFAULT,
    request_delay_sec: float = REQUEST_DELAY_SEC_DEFAULT
) -> Dict:
    """
    Entry crawl for mixed seeds: list pages and direct profiles.
    Limits:
    - max_pages: total list pages processed
    - max_profile_links: per list-page profile link limit
    - max_profiles: cap staged profiles for the whole run
    """
    staged = 0
    failed = 0
    pages_processed = 0
    profiles_processed = 0
    seq = 0  # per-run sequence counter for logs

    rep.info({
        "event": "crawl_start",
        "seed_count": len(seed_urls),
        "limits": {"max_pages": max_pages, "max_profile_links": max_profile_links, "max_profiles": max_profiles},
        "run_id": RUN_ID
    })

    for url in seed_urls:
        if STOP_REQUESTED:
            rep.warn({"event": "crawl_stopped", "reason": "stop_flag", "run_id": RUN_ID})
            break

        host = urlparse(url).netloc
        status, html, mode = _fetch_with_js_fallback(url)
        seq += 1
        rep.info({"event": "seed_fetch_result", "seq": seq, "url": url, "status": status, "mode": mode, "len": len(html), "run_id": RUN_ID})

        if status != 200 or not html:
            failed += 1
            rep.error({"event": "seed_fetch_error", "url": url, "status": status, "run_id": RUN_ID})
            continue

        try:
            if _is_list_page(url):
                if pages_processed >= max_pages:
                    rep.warn({"event": "pages_limit_reached", "pages_processed": pages_processed, "run_id": RUN_ID})
                    continue

                pages_processed += 1

                profile_links = extract_profile_links(html, url)[:max_profile_links]
                rep.info({"event": "discovered_profiles", "count": len(profile_links), "from": url, "run_id": RUN_ID})

                parsed_batch: List[Dict] = []
                for purl in profile_links:
                    if STOP_REQUESTED:
                        rep.warn({"event": "crawl_stopped_mid_profiles", "run_id": RUN_ID})
                        break
                    if profiles_processed >= max_profiles:
                        rep.warn({"event": "profiles_limit_reached", "profiles_processed": profiles_processed, "run_id": RUN_ID})
                        break

                    pstatus, phtml, pmode = _fetch_with_js_fallback(purl)
                    seq += 1
                    rep.info({"event": "profile_fetch", "seq": seq, "url": purl, "status": pstatus, "mode": pmode, "len": len(phtml), "run_id": RUN_ID})

                    if pstatus != 200 or not phtml:
                        failed += 1
                        rep.error({"event": "profile_fetch_error", "url": purl, "status": pstatus, "run_id": RUN_ID})
                        continue

                    raw_meta = save_raw_html(phtml, purl)
                    parsed = _process_html(purl, phtml)

                    # Defensive: if parsed too thin, still stage minimal rule-based
                    if not parsed.get("name") and not parsed.get("phones") and not parsed.get("address"):
                        rb_min = rule_based_extract(phtml, purl)
                        parsed = _merge_parsed(rb_min, {})  # minimal
                        parsed = _normalize_enrich(purl, parsed)
                        rep.warn({"event": "parsed_too_thin_fallback_rb", "url": purl, "run_id": RUN_ID})

                    evidence = {
                        "url": purl,
                        "type": "official" if "isipo" in urlparse(purl).netloc else "page",
                        "fetched_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
                    }
                    fc = field_confidence(parsed, evidence)
                    conf = overall_confidence(fc)

                    sid = stage(
                        parsed=parsed,
                        raw_json=raw_meta,
                        source_evidence=evidence,
                        field_confidences=fc,
                        confidence=conf,
                        status="staged"
                    )
                    profiles_processed += 1
                    staged += 1
                    parsed_batch.append(parsed)
                    rep.info({"event": "staged", "staging_id": sid, "confidence": conf, "url": purl, "run_id": RUN_ID})

                    time.sleep(request_delay_sec)

                # Optional: stage list page summary if phones found
                parsed_list = _process_html(url, html)
                if parsed_list.get("phones"):
                    raw_meta_list = save_raw_html(html, url)
                    evidence_list = {"url": url, "type": "page", "fetched_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}
                    fc_list = field_confidence(parsed_list, evidence_list)
                    conf_list = overall_confidence(fc_list)
                    sid_list = stage(
                        parsed=parsed_list,
                        raw_json=raw_meta_list,
                        source_evidence=evidence_list,
                        field_confidences=fc_list,
                        confidence=conf_list,
                        status="staged"
                    )
                    staged += 1
                    rep.info({"event": "staged_list_page", "staging_id": sid_list, "confidence": conf_list, "url": url, "run_id": RUN_ID})

                # Batch dedupe report (informational)
                deduped = _dedupe_seen(parsed_batch)
                rep.info({"event": "batch_dedupe", "in": len(parsed_batch), "out": len(deduped), "run_id": RUN_ID})

            else:
                # Direct profile page
                if profiles_processed >= max_profiles:
                    rep.warn({"event": "profiles_limit_reached", "profiles_processed": profiles_processed, "run_id": RUN_ID})
                    continue

                pstatus, phtml, pmode = status, html, mode
                seq += 1
                rep.info({"event": "direct_profile_fetch", "seq": seq, "url": url, "status": pstatus, "mode": pmode, "len": len(phtml), "run_id": RUN_ID})

                raw_meta = save_raw_html(phtml, url)
                parsed = _process_html(url, phtml)

                if not parsed.get("name") and not parsed.get("phones") and not parsed.get("address"):
                    rb_min = rule_based_extract(phtml, url)
                    parsed = _merge_parsed(rb_min, {})
                    parsed = _normalize_enrich(url, parsed)
                    rep.warn({"event": "parsed_too_thin_fallback_rb", "url": url, "run_id": RUN_ID})

                evidence = {
                    "url": url,
                    "type": "official" if "isipo" in host else "page",
                    "fetched_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
                }
                fc = field_confidence(parsed, evidence)
                conf = overall_confidence(fc)
                sid = stage(
                    parsed=parsed,
                    raw_json=raw_meta,
                    source_evidence=evidence,
                    field_confidences=fc,
                    confidence=conf,
                    status="staged"
                )
                profiles_processed += 1
                staged += 1
                rep.info({"event": "staged", "staging_id": sid, "confidence": conf, "url": url, "run_id": RUN_ID})

        except Exception as e:
            failed += 1
            rep.error({"event": "crawl_process_error", "url": url, "error": str(e), "run_id": RUN_ID})
            continue

    rep.info({
        "event": "crawl_done",
        "staged": staged, "failed": failed,
        "pages_processed": pages_processed, "profiles_processed": profiles_processed,
        "run_id": RUN_ID
    })
    return {"staged": staged, "failed": failed, "pages_processed": pages_processed, "profiles_processed": profiles_processed}

def crawl_business_center(
    start_url: str,
    max_pages: int = MAX_PAGES_DEFAULT,
    max_profile_links: int = MAX_PROFILE_LINKS_DEFAULT,
    request_delay_sec: float = REQUEST_DELAY_SEC_DEFAULT
) -> List[Dict]:
    """
    Focused crawl for a Business-Center:
    - respects max_pages and max_profile_links
    - returns parsed dicts; does NOT stage (pure function for testing)
    """
    results: List[Dict] = []
    visited_pages = set()
    to_visit = [start_url]

    pages_processed = 0

    while to_visit:
        if STOP_REQUESTED:
            rep.warn({"event": "stop_requested_bc", "run_id": RUN_ID})
            break

        url = to_visit.pop(0)
        if url in visited_pages:
            continue
        visited_pages.add(url)

        status, html, mode = _fetch_with_js_fallback(url)
        rep.info({"event": "bc_fetch_page", "url": url, "status": status, "mode": mode, "len": len(html), "run_id": RUN_ID})
        if status != 200 or not html:
            continue

        # Extract profile links
        profile_links = extract_profile_links(html, url)[:max_profile_links]
        rep.info({"event": "bc_profile_links", "count": len(profile_links), "page": url, "run_id": RUN_ID})
        for plink in profile_links:
            s, h, pmode = _fetch_with_js_fallback(plink)
            rep.info({"event": "bc_fetch_profile", "url": plink, "status": s, "mode": pmode, "len": len(h), "run_id": RUN_ID})
            if s == 200 and h:
                data = extract_profile(h)
                if data:
                    results.append(data)
            time.sleep(request_delay_sec)

        # Pagination
        pages_processed += 1
        if pages_processed >= max_pages:
            rep.warn({"event": "bc_pages_limit_reached", "pages_processed": pages_processed, "run_id": RUN_ID})
            break

        new_pages = extract_pagination_links(html, url)
        for np in new_pages:
            if np not in visited_pages and np not in to_visit:
                to_visit.append(np)

        time.sleep(request_delay_sec)

    rep.info({"event": "bc_done", "pages_processed": pages_processed, "results": len(results), "run_id": RUN_ID})
    return results

# src/company/pipeline/dedupe.py
from rapidfuzz import fuzz

def same_by_phone(a: dict, b: dict) -> bool:
    return bool(set(a.get("phones",[])).intersection(set(b.get("phones",[]))))

def same_by_domain(a: dict, b: dict) -> bool:
    return a.get("website") and b.get("website") and (a["website"] == b["website"])

def same_by_name(a: dict, b: dict, threshold: float=0.9) -> bool:
    return fuzz.token_set_ratio(a.get("canonical_name",""), b.get("canonical_name",""))/100 >= threshold

# src/company/pipeline/enrich.py
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple

def aggregate_field_evidence(field_values: List[Dict]) -> Tuple[str | None, float]:
    """
    field_values: [{"value": "...", "weight": 0.95}, ...]
    returns: (best_value, aggregated_confidence 0..1)
    """
    if not field_values:
        return None, 0.0
    groups = {}
    for ev in field_values:
        val = ev.get("value")
        w = float(ev.get("weight", 0.5))
        if not val: 
            continue
        groups.setdefault(val, 0.0)
        groups[val] += w
    best_val = max(groups.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1])[0]
    total_weight = sum(groups.values())
    # normalize confidence between 0..1
    conf = min(1.0, groups[best_val] / max(total_weight, 1.0))
    return best_val, round(conf, 3)

def field_confidence(parsed: Dict, evidence: Dict) -> Dict[str, float]:
    # ساده و پارامتری: وزن بالاتر برای منابع رسمی
    src_type = evidence.get("type")
    src_w = 1.0 if src_type in ("official", "government") else 0.6
    return {
        "name": 0.85 if parsed.get("name") else 0.0,
        "phones": (0.7 + 0.25 * src_w) if parsed.get("phones") else 0.0,
        "emails": 0.65 if parsed.get("emails") else 0.0,
        "address": (0.7 + 0.25 * src_w) if parsed.get("address") else 0.0,
        "website": 0.8 if parsed.get("website") else 0.0,
        "ceo": 0.55 if parsed.get("ceo") else 0.0,
    }

def overall_confidence(fc: Dict[str, float]) -> float:
    vals = [v for v in fc.values() if v > 0]
    return round(sum(vals) / len(vals), 3) if vals else 0.0

# src/company/pipeline/export.py
import json
import pandas as pd
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from ..db.session import SessionLocal
from ..db.models import CompanyStaging

COLUMNS = [
    "staging_id","name","canonical_name","ceo","phones","emails","website",
    "address","city","province","confidence","sources","field_confidences","action","notes"
]

def export_staging_xlsx(path: str, limit: int=100) -> int:
    session: Session = SessionLocal()
    try:
        rows = (session.query(CompanyStaging)
                .filter(CompanyStaging.status.in_(["staged","needs_review"]))
                .order_by(CompanyStaging.id.asc())
                .limit(limit).all())
        data = []
        for r in rows:
            p = r.parsed or {}
            src_list = r.source_evidence or []
            if not isinstance(src_list, list):
                src_list = [src_list]
            src_str = "; ".join([f"{item.get('type','?')}:{item.get('url','')}" for item in src_list])
            fc = r.field_confidences or {}
            fc_str = ", ".join([f"{k}:{v}" for k, v in fc.items()])
            data.append({
                "staging_id": r.id,
                "name": p.get("name"),
                "canonical_name": p.get("canonical_name"),
                "ceo": p.get("ceo"),
                "phones": ";".join(p.get("phones", []) or []),
                "emails": ";".join(p.get("emails", []) or []),
                "website": p.get("website"),
                "address": p.get("address"),
                "city": p.get("city"),
                "province": p.get("province"),
                "confidence": r.confidence,
                "sources": src_str,
                "field_confidences": fc_str,
                "action": "",
                "notes": "",
            })
        df = pd.DataFrame(data, columns=COLUMNS)
        try:
            with pd.ExcelWriter(path, engine="openpyxl") as writer:
                df.to_excel(writer, index=False)
        except Exception as e:
            # لاگ خطا و ادامه
            print(f"⚠️ export failed: {e}")
        for r in rows:
            r.status = "exported"
        session.commit()
        return len(rows)
    finally:
        session.close()

# src/company/pipeline/extractors.py
import re
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from .agent import call_groq_agent

PHONE_RE = re.compile(r'(?:\+?98|0)?\d{8,11}')
EMAIL_RE = re.compile(r'[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}')
CEO_HINTS = ['مدیرعامل', 'مدیر عامل', 'CEO', 'Chief Executive', 'مدیریت']

CITY_HINTS = ["تهران","قم","مشهد","اصفهان","شیراز","تبریز","کرج","پاکدشت","بندرعباس","یزد","قزوین","اراک","اهواز"]
PROVINCE_HINTS = [
    "استان تهران","استان قم","استان البرز","استان فارس","استان خراسان رضوی","استان اصفهان",
    "استان خوزستان","استان هرمزگان","استان یزد","استان قزوین","استان مرکزی"
]

def rule_based_extract(html: str, url: str) -> dict:
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    text = soup.get_text(" ", strip=True)

    phones = list({m.group() for m in PHONE_RE.finditer(text)})
    emails = list({m.group() for m in EMAIL_RE.finditer(text)})

    title = soup.find(['h1','h2'])
    page_title = soup.find('title')
    name = None
    if title:
        name = title.get_text(strip=True)
    elif page_title:
        # try to trim site suffixes
        name = re.sub(r'[\|\-–].*$', '', page_title.get_text(strip=True)).strip()

    ceo = None
    for hint in CEO_HINTS:
        m = re.search(hint + r'\s*[:\-]\s*([^\n\r]+)', text)
        if m:
            ceo = m.group(1).strip()
            break

    address = None
    # priority on semantic selectors
    for node in soup.select("address, .address, .location, [itemprop='address']"):
        seg = node.get_text(" ", strip=True)
        if len(seg) > 12:
            address = seg
            break
    if not address:
        for node in soup.find_all(text=re.compile(r'(آدرس|نشانی|address|location)', re.IGNORECASE)):
            seg = node.parent.get_text(" ", strip=True)
            if len(seg) > 15:
                address = seg
                break

    city = next((c for c in CITY_HINTS if c in (address or "") or c in text), None)
    province = next((p for p in PROVINCE_HINTS if p in (address or "") or p in text), None)

    return {
        "name": name,
        "phones": phones,
        "emails": emails,
        "ceo": ceo,
        "address": address,
        "city": city,
        "province": province,
        "website": url.split('/')[2] if '//' in url else url,
        "source": {"url": url, "type": "page"},
    }

def ai_extract_from_text(seed_text: str) -> dict:
    if not seed_text:
        return {}
    try:
        return call_groq_agent(seed_text)
    except Exception:
        return {}

# src/company/pipeline/fetcher.py
import time
from typing import Tuple, Optional
from urllib.parse import urlparse
from urllib import robotparser
import requests
from requests.adapters import HTTPAdapter
from urllib3.util.retry import Retry
from src.company.config import CRAWL
from src.bot.utils.reporter import Reporter

rep = Reporter(module="company_fetcher")

session = requests.Session()
retry = Retry(
    total=CRAWL.max_retries,
    backoff_factor=CRAWL.backoff_base,
    status_forcelist=(429, 500, 502, 503, 504),
    allowed_methods=frozenset(["GET", "HEAD"]),
    raise_on_status=False,
)
adapter = HTTPAdapter(max_retries=retry, pool_connections=20, pool_maxsize=50)
session.mount("http://", adapter)
session.mount("https://", adapter)

_ROBOTS_CACHE: dict[str, tuple[robotparser.RobotFileParser, float, Optional[float]]] = {}
ROBOTS_TTL = 3600  # 1h
_LAST_REQUEST: dict[str, float] = {}

def _parse_crawl_delay(text: str) -> Optional[float]:
    # ساده: اولین Crawl-delay اعمال می‌شود
    for line in text.splitlines():
        line = line.strip()
        if line.lower().startswith("crawl-delay:"):
            try:
                val = float(line.split(":", 1)[1].strip())
                if val >= 0.0:
                    return val
            except Exception:
                continue
    return None

def _get_robots(host: str, robots_url: str):
    now = time.time()
    item = _ROBOTS_CACHE.get(host)
    if item and (now - item[1]) < ROBOTS_TTL:
        return item[0], item[2]
    rp = robotparser.RobotFileParser()
    rp.set_url(robots_url)
    crawl_delay = None
    try:
        resp = requests.get(robots_url, timeout=3)
        if resp.status_code == 200 and resp.text:
            rp.parse(resp.text.splitlines())
            crawl_delay = _parse_crawl_delay(resp.text)  # استخراج Crawl-delay
        else:
            rp.read()
    except Exception as e:
        rep.error({"event": "robots_read_error", "host": host, "error": str(e)})
    _ROBOTS_CACHE[host] = (rp, now, crawl_delay)
    return rp, crawl_delay

def _robots_allowed(url: str, user_agent: str) -> bool:
    try:
        parsed = urlparse(url)
        robots_url = f"{parsed.scheme}://{parsed.netloc}/robots.txt"
        rp, _ = _get_robots(parsed.netloc, robots_url)
        allowed = rp.can_fetch(user_agent, url)
        rep.info({"event":"robots_check","url":url,"allowed":allowed})
        return allowed
    except Exception as e:
        rep.error({"event":"robots_error","url":url,"error":str(e)})
        return True

def respect_rps(host: str):
    # مقدار پیش‌فرض هم سه‌تایی باشه
    _, _, crawl_delay = _ROBOTS_CACHE.get(host, (None, 0.0, None))
    if crawl_delay is not None:
        min_interval = max(crawl_delay, 0.2)
    else:
        min_interval = max(1.0 / CRAWL.per_host_rps, 0.2)
    now = time.time()
    last = _LAST_REQUEST.get(host, 0.0)
    wait = max(0.0, min_interval - (now - last))
    if wait > 0:
        time.sleep(wait)
    _LAST_REQUEST[host] = time.time()

def fetch_url(url: str, timeout: int = 20) -> Tuple[int, str]:
    ua = CRAWL.user_agent
    host = urlparse(url).netloc

    if not _robots_allowed(url, ua):
        rep.error({"event":"fetch_blocked_by_robots","url":url})
        return 403, ""

    respect_rps(host)
    headers = {"User-Agent": ua}
    try:
        rep.info({"event":"fetch_started","url":url})
        resp = session.get(
            url,
            headers=headers,
            timeout=(8, timeout),  # (connect, read)
            verify=True
        )
        text = resp.text or ""
        rep.info({"event":"fetch_done","url":url,"status":resp.status_code,"len":len(text)})
        return resp.status_code, text
    except requests.RequestException as e:
        rep.error({"event":"fetch_failed","url":url,"error":str(e)})
        return 0, ""

# src/company/pipeline/fetcher_js.py

try:
    from playwright.async_api import async_playwright
except ImportError:
    async_playwright = None

async def fetch_page_js(url: str, timeout_ms: int = 15000) -> str:
    if async_playwright is None:
        raise RuntimeError("playwright not installed")
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        try:
            ctx = await browser.new_context()
            page = await ctx.new_page()
            await page.goto(url, timeout=timeout_ms)
            await page.wait_for_timeout(1200)
            return await page.content()
        finally:
            await browser.close()

# src/company/pipeline/geocode.py
import time, hashlib, requests
from typing import Tuple

_GEOCODE_CACHE: dict[str, tuple[float|None, float|None, float]] = {}
GEOCODE_TTL_SEC = 7 * 24 * 3600

def _key(addr: str) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha256(addr.strip().encode('utf-8', 'ignore')).hexdigest()

def geocode_address(addr: str) -> Tuple[float | None, float | None]:
    if not addr:
        return None, None
    key = _key(addr)
    item = _GEOCODE_CACHE.get(key)
    now = time.time()
    if item and (now - item[2]) < GEOCODE_TTL_SEC:
        return item[0], item[1]
    try:
        resp = requests.get(
            "https://nominatim.openstreetmap.org/search",
            params={"q": addr, "format": "json", "limit": 1},
            headers={"User-Agent": "CompanyCrawler/1.0 (contact: ops@example.com)"},
            timeout=10
        )
        resp.raise_for_status()
        j = resp.json()
        if j:
            lat, lon = float(j[0]["lat"]), float(j[0]["lon"])
            _GEOCODE_CACHE[key] = (lat, lon, now)
            return lat, lon
    except Exception:
        pass
    _GEOCODE_CACHE[key] = (None, None, now)
    return None, None



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/company/pipeline/link_extractor.py
########################################################################################################################

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from urllib.parse import urljoin, urlparse

def extract_profile_links(html: str, base_url: str) -> list[str]:
    if not html:
        return []
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
    base_host = urlparse(base_url).netloc
    links = []

    # حالت اصلی
    for a in soup.select("a.td-title[href^='/biz/']"):
        href = a.get("href")
        if href:
            u = urljoin(base_url, href)
            if urlparse(u).netloc == base_host:
                links.append(u)

    # fallback: هر لینکی که به /biz/ اشاره کنه
    if not links:
        for a in soup.select("a[href*='/biz/']"):
            href = a.get("href")
            if href:
                u = urljoin(base_url, href)
                if urlparse(u).netloc == base_host:
                    links.append(u)

    # حذف تکراری‌ها
    seen, out = set(), []
    for u in links:
        if u not in seen:
            seen.add(u)
            out.append(u)
    return out



def extract_pagination_links(html: str, base_url: str) -> list[str]:
    """استخراج لینک صفحات بعدی (pagination)"""
    if not html:
        return []
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
    base_host = urlparse(base_url).netloc
    pages = []

    # لینک‌های صفحه‌بندی معمولاً در <a class="page-link"> یا مشابه هستند
    for a in soup.select("a[href*='Business-Center']"):
        href = a.get("href")
        if not href:
            continue
        u = urljoin(base_url, href)
        if urlparse(u).netloc == base_host and "Business-Center" in u:
            pages.append(u)

    # حذف تکراری‌ها
    seen, out = set(), []
    for u in pages:
        if u not in seen:
            seen.add(u)
            out.append(u)
    return out

# src/company/pipeline/normalizers.py
import re
import phonenumbers

PERSIAN_MAP = {'ي': 'ی', 'ك': 'ک', '‌': ' ', 'ـ': '', '\u200c': ' ', '\u202f': ' '}

def normalize_text(s: str | None) -> str | None:
    if not s: return s
    for k, v in PERSIAN_MAP.items():
        s = s.replace(k, v)
    return re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', s).strip()

def canonicalize_name(name: str | None) -> str | None:
    if not name: return None
    name = normalize_text(name)
    name = re.sub(r'\b(شرکت|صنایع|گروه|کارخانه|سهامی عام|سهامی خاص)\b', '', name)
    return re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', name).strip().lower()

def normalize_phone(value: str) -> str | None:
    if not value:
        return None
    try:
        pn = phonenumbers.parse(value, "IR")
        if not phonenumbers.is_possible_number(pn) or not phonenumbers.is_valid_number(pn):
            return None
        return phonenumbers.format_number(pn, phonenumbers.PhoneNumberFormat.E164)
    except Exception:
        s = re.sub(r'[^0-9+]', '', value)
        if s.startswith('0'): s = '+98' + s[1:]
        if s.startswith('98') and not s.startswith('+'): s = '+' + s
        return s if s.startswith('+98') else None

def unique_list(xs: list[str]) -> list[str]:
    seen, out = set(), []
    for x in xs:
        if x and x not in seen:
            seen.add(x); out.append(x)
    return out

FILE: src/src/company/pipeline/profile_extractor.py
########################################################################################################################

from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re

def extract_profile(html: str) -> dict:
    if not html:
        return {}
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
    text = soup.get_text(" ", strip=True)
    data = {}

    # عنوان آگهی
    title = soup.select_one("h1")
    if title:
        data["title"] = title.get_text(strip=True)

    # استان
    m = re.search(r"استان\s*:\s*([^\s,]+)", text)
    if m:
        data["province"] = m.group(1)

    # شهر
    m = re.search(r"شهر\s*:\s*([^\s,]+)", text)
    if m:
        data["city"] = m.group(1)

    # نام صاحب آگهی
    owner = soup.select_one("div.FirstNameLabelClone, span.OwnerAd")
    if owner:
        data["name"] = owner.get_text(strip=True)
    else:
        m = re.search(r"نام\s*:\s*([^\n\r]+)", text)
        if m:
            data["name"] = m.group(1).strip()

    # آدرس (فقط تا قبل از "تلفن" یا "وب سایت")
    addr = soup.select_one("span.tcphone1")
    if addr:
        raw_addr = addr.get_text(strip=True)
    else:
        m = re.search(r"آدرس\s*:\s*([^\n\r]+)", text)
        raw_addr = m.group(1).strip() if m else ""

    if raw_addr:
        # حذف بخش‌های اضافی
        raw_addr = re.split(r"(تلفن|وب\s*سایت|واتساپ)", raw_addr)[0].strip()
        data["address"] = raw_addr

    # شماره تلفن‌ها
    phones = []
    for div in soup.select("div.TelTrade, span#TelLabelClone"):
        t = div.get_text(" ", strip=True)
        for m in re.findall(r"\d{2,5}[- ]?\d{5,}", t):
            phones.append(m.strip())
    # fallback regex روی کل متن
    if not phones:
        for m in re.findall(r"\d{2,5}[- ]?\d{5,}", text):
            phones.append(m.strip())
    if phones:
        data["phones"] = sorted(set(phones))

    # وب‌سایت
    m = re.search(r"(https?://[^\s]+)", text)
    if m:
        data["website"] = m.group(1)

    # توضیحات
    desc = soup.select_one("span#DetailLabel, div.AlhtextCd")
    if desc:
        data["description"] = desc.get_text(" ", strip=True)

    # تصویر اصلی
    img = soup.select_one("img#Pic")
    if img and img.get("src"):
        data["image"] = img["src"]

    return data

# src/company/pipeline/raw_store.py
import os, gzip, hashlib, tempfile
from datetime import datetime

def save_raw_html(html: str, url: str, base_dir: str = "./data/raw") -> dict:
    os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)
    sha1 = hashlib.sha1(html.encode("utf-8", errors="ignore")).hexdigest()
    final = os.path.join(base_dir, f"{sha1}.html.gz")
    # نوشتن در فایل موقت سپس replace اتمیک
    fd, tmp_path = tempfile.mkstemp(prefix=f".{sha1}.", suffix=".tmp", dir=base_dir)
    os.close(fd)
    try:
        with gzip.open(tmp_path, "wt", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write(html)
        os.replace(tmp_path, final)
    finally:
        # اگر هرطور باقی موند، پاک‌سازی
        if os.path.exists(tmp_path):
            try:
                os.remove(tmp_path)
            except Exception:
                pass
    return {"raw_path": final, "sha1": sha1, "url": url, "fetched_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}

# src/company/pipeline/staging.py
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from ..db.session import SessionLocal
from ..db.models import CompanyStaging
import os
import requests
from datetime import datetime

N8N_COMPANY_WEBHOOK_URL = os.getenv("N8N_COMPANY_WEBHOOK_URL", "http://n8n:5678/webhook/company")
N8N_SECRET_HEADER_NAME = os.getenv("N8N_SECRET_HEADER_NAME", "X-NEWS-SECRET")
N8N_SECRET_TOKEN = os.getenv("N8N_SECRET_TOKEN", "S3cReT_123")

def notify_n8n(parsed, plink, confidence, row_id):
    payload = {
        "title": parsed.get("title") or parsed.get("name"),
        "excerpt": parsed.get("description"),
        "phones": parsed.get("phones"),
        "address": parsed.get("address"),
        "image": parsed.get("image"),
        "url": plink,
        "confidence": confidence,
        "staging_id": row_id,
    }
    headers = {N8N_SECRET_HEADER_NAME: N8N_SECRET_TOKEN}
    try:
            r = requests.post(N8N_COMPANY_WEBHOOK_URL, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)
            print("✅ Sent to n8n company:", r.status_code)
    except Exception as e:
            print("⚠️ Failed to notify n8n company:", e)

def stage(parsed: dict, raw_json: dict, source_evidence: dict | list,
          field_confidences: dict, confidence: float, status: str="staged") -> int:
    s: Session = SessionLocal()
    os.makedirs("./data", exist_ok=True)
    try:
        sources = source_evidence if isinstance(source_evidence, list) else [source_evidence]
        row = CompanyStaging(
            raw_json=raw_json,
            parsed=parsed,
            source_evidence=sources,
            field_confidences=field_confidences,
            confidence=confidence,
            status=status,
        )
        s.add(row)
        s.commit()

        # بعد از ذخیره موفق، اطلاع به n8n
        plink = raw_json.get("url") if isinstance(raw_json, dict) else None
        notify_n8n(parsed, plink, confidence, row.id)

        return row.id
    finally:
        s.close()

FILE: src/src/company/pipeline/test_run_crawler.py
########################################################################################################################

import sys, traceback
from src.company.pipeline.fetcher import fetch_url
from src.company.pipeline.link_extractor import extract_profile_links
from src.company.pipeline.profile_extractor import extract_profile
from src.company.pipeline.staging import stage

TEST_URL = "https://iran-tejarat.com/Business-Center/شهرک-صنعتی-عباس-آباد.html"

def save_debug_html(name, html):
    path = f"/tmp/{name}.html"
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(html)
    print(f"💾 HTML ذخیره شد: {path} (len={len(html)})")

def main():
    print("🚀 شروع تست دیباگ روی:", TEST_URL)

    try:
        # 1) واکشی صفحه لیست
        status, html = fetch_url(TEST_URL)
        print(f"[FETCH LIST] status={status}, len={len(html)}")
        if status != 200 or not html:
            print("❌ نتونستیم صفحه لیست رو واکشی کنیم")
            return
        save_debug_html("list_page", html)

        # 2) استخراج لینک پروفایل‌ها
        profile_links = extract_profile_links(html, TEST_URL)
        print(f"[LINKS] تعداد لینک پروفایل پیدا شد: {len(profile_links)}")
        for i, link in enumerate(profile_links[:5], start=1):
            print(f"  {i}. {link}")

        if not profile_links:
            print("❌ هیچ لینکی پیدا نشد. احتمالا selector اشتباهه یا HTML تغییر کرده.")
            return

        # 3) واکشی اولین پروفایل برای بررسی
        plink = profile_links[0]
        print(f"\n--- تست پروفایل: {plink}")
        s, h = fetch_url(plink)
        print(f"[FETCH PROFILE] status={s}, len={len(h)}")
        if s == 200 and h:
            save_debug_html("profile_page", h)
            parsed = extract_profile(h)
            print("[PARSED]", parsed)

            if parsed:
                try:
                    sid = stage(
                        parsed,
                        raw_json={"html_len": len(h)},
                        source_evidence={"url": plink, "type": "b2b"},
                        field_confidences={},
                        confidence=0.9
                    )
                    print(f"✅ staged id={sid}")
                except Exception as e:
                    print("❌ stage error:", e)
                    traceback.print_exc(file=sys.stdout)
            else:
                print("❌ extractor چیزی برنگردوند")
        else:
            print("❌ واکشی پروفایل شکست خورد")

    except Exception as e:
        print("❌ خطا در اجرای تست:", e)
        traceback.print_exc(file=sys.stdout)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# src/company/pipeline/validate.py
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional, List

class ParsedCompany(BaseModel):
    name: Optional[str]
    canonical_name: Optional[str]
    ceo: Optional[str]
    phones: Optional[List[str]]
    emails: Optional[List[str]]
    website: Optional[str]
    address: Optional[str]
    city: Optional[str]
    province: Optional[str]
    postal_code: Optional[str]
    products: Optional[List[str]]
    raw_materials: Optional[List[str]]

FILE: src/src/company/pipeline/worker.py

# src/company/pipeline/worker.py
from sqlalchemy import select
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from datetime import datetime
import json

from src.bot.utils.reporter import Reporter
from src.company.db.session import SessionLocal, engine
from src.company.db.models import Company, CompanyStaging, CompanyAudit
from src.company.pipeline.normalizers import canonicalize_name, normalize_phone

rep = Reporter(module="company_worker")

def _canon_list(lst):
    if not lst:
        return []
    return sorted([x for x in lst if x])

def _json_equal(a, b):
    return json.dumps(a, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False) == json.dumps(b, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False)

def _apply_changes(s: Session, company: Company, parsed: dict, actor: str):
    changes = []

    def setf(field, newv):
        oldv = getattr(company, field)
        if field == "phones":
            newv = _canon_list([normalize_phone(x) for x in (newv or []) if x])
            oldv = _canon_list(oldv or [])
        elif field in ("emails", "products", "raw_materials"):
            newv = _canon_list(newv or [])
            oldv = _canon_list(oldv or [])
        if newv is not None and not _json_equal(newv, oldv):
            setattr(company, field, newv)
            changes.append((field, oldv, newv))

    setf("name", parsed.get("name"))
    setf("canonical_name", canonicalize_name(parsed.get("name")))
    setf("slug", (canonicalize_name(parsed.get("name")) or "").replace(" ", "-"))
    setf("industry", parsed.get("industry"))
    setf("products", parsed.get("products"))
    setf("raw_materials", parsed.get("raw_materials"))
    setf("ceo", parsed.get("ceo"))
    setf("phones", parsed.get("phones"))
    setf("emails", parsed.get("emails"))
    setf("website", parsed.get("website"))
    setf("address", parsed.get("address"))
    setf("city", parsed.get("city"))
    setf("province", parsed.get("province"))
    setf("postal_code", parsed.get("postal_code"))
    setf("location_lat", parsed.get("location_lat"))
    setf("location_lng", parsed.get("location_lng"))
    setf("source_evidence", parsed.get("source_evidence"))
    setf("field_confidences", parsed.get("field_confidences"))
    setf("confidence", parsed.get("confidence"))
    company.verified = bool(parsed.get("confidence", 0.0) >= 0.85)

    for field, before, after in changes:
        s.add(CompanyAudit(
            company_id=company.id,
            field_name=field,
            before=before,
            after=after,
            actor=actor,
            reason="import",
            created_at=datetime.utcnow()
        ))
    return changes

def import_staging(staging_id: int, actor: str = "admin") -> bool:
    s: Session = SessionLocal()
    try:
        st = s.query(CompanyStaging).filter(CompanyStaging.id == staging_id).first()
        if not st:
            rep.error({"event": "import_not_found", "staging_id": staging_id})
            return False

        parsed = st.parsed or {}
        canonical = canonicalize_name(parsed.get("name"))

        # اگر Postgres بود، از upsert استفاده کن
        if engine.dialect.name == "postgresql":
            from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import insert
            values = {
                "name": parsed.get("name"),
                "canonical_name": canonical,
                "slug": (canonical or "").replace(" ", "-"),
                "industry": parsed.get("industry"),
                "products": parsed.get("products"),
                "raw_materials": parsed.get("raw_materials"),
                "ceo": parsed.get("ceo"),
                "phones": _canon_list([normalize_phone(x) for x in (parsed.get("phones") or []) if x]),
                "emails": _canon_list(parsed.get("emails") or []),
                "website": parsed.get("website"),
                "address": parsed.get("address"),
                "city": parsed.get("city"),
                "province": parsed.get("province"),
                "postal_code": parsed.get("postal_code"),
                "location_lat": parsed.get("location_lat"),
                "location_lng": parsed.get("location_lng"),
                "source_evidence": st.source_evidence,
                "field_confidences": st.field_confidences,
                "confidence": st.confidence,
                "verified": bool(st.confidence and st.confidence >= 0.85),
            }
            stmt = insert(Company).values(**values).on_conflict_do_update(
                index_elements=['canonical_name'],
                set_=values
            )
            res = s.execute(stmt)
            s.commit()
            # تلاش برای گرفتن id از نتیجه ممکنه مستقیم نباشه؛ یکبار select بزنیم
            company = s.execute(select(Company).where(Company.canonical_name == canonical)).scalar_one()
            rep.info({"event": "import_upserted", "staging_id": staging_id, "company_id": company.id})
        else:
            candidate = s.execute(select(Company).where(Company.canonical_name == canonical)).scalar_one_or_none()
            if candidate is None:
                company = Company(
                    name=parsed.get("name"),
                    canonical_name=canonical,
                    slug=(canonical or "").replace(" ", "-"),
                    products=parsed.get("products"),
                    raw_materials=parsed.get("raw_materials"),
                    ceo=parsed.get("ceo"),
                    phones=_canon_list([normalize_phone(x) for x in (parsed.get("phones") or []) if x]),
                    emails=_canon_list(parsed.get("emails") or []),
                    website=parsed.get("website"),
                    address=parsed.get("address"),
                    city=parsed.get("city"),
                    province=parsed.get("province"),
                    postal_code=parsed.get("postal_code"),
                    location_lat=parsed.get("location_lat"),
                    location_lng=parsed.get("location_lng"),
                    source_evidence=st.source_evidence,
                    field_confidences=st.field_confidences,
                    confidence=st.confidence,
                    verified=bool(st.confidence and st.confidence >= 0.85),
                )
                s.add(company)
                s.commit()
                rep.info({"event": "import_inserted", "staging_id": staging_id, "company_id": company.id})
            else:
                changes = _apply_changes(s, candidate, parsed, actor)
                s.commit()
                rep.info({
                    "event": "import_updated",
                    "staging_id": staging_id,
                    "company_id": candidate.id,
                    "changed_fields": [f for f, _, _ in changes]
                })

        st.status = "imported"
        s.commit()
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        rep.error({"event": "import_error", "staging_id": staging_id, "error": str(e)})
        s.rollback()
        return False
    finally:
        s.close()



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/company/runner.py

# src/company/runner.py
from src.company.pipeline.crawler import crawl
from src.bot.utils.reporter import Reporter  # reuse
import json, os

def run_company_crawl(seed_urls: list[str]):
    rep = Reporter(module="company_crawler")
    rep.info({"event":"start","seed_count":len(seed_urls)})
    res = crawl(seed_urls)
    rep.info({"event":"done","result":res})
    return res

if __name__ == "__main__":
    seeds_env = os.getenv("COMPANY_SEEDS","")
    seeds = [u.strip() for u in seeds_env.split(",") if u.strip()]
    if not seeds:
        # نمونه برای تست
        seeds = ["https://example.com/contact"]
    print(json.dumps(run_company_crawl(seeds), ensure_ascii=False))

#/root/ASASANATBOT/src/core/config.py

from __future__ import annotations
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Union, Optional
from pydantic import Field, field_validator, model_validator
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings, SettingsConfigDict
import json, ast, logging, os
import logging
from src import logger_setup

# مسیرهای پیشنهادی برای config.json — ترتیب تلاش خواندن
CONFIG_PATHS = [
    "/root/ASASANATBOT/config.json",
    os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "config.json"),
]

logger = logging.getLogger("asa.config")

def _resolve_env_if_needed(value: Any) -> Any:
    """
    اگر مقدار یک رشته بزرگ (ENV_NAME) بود و به نظر اسم متغیر محیطی بود،
    مقدار واقعی را از env می‌گیرد؛ در غیر این صورت همان مقدار را برمی‌گرداند.
    """
    if not isinstance(value, str):
        return value
    v = value.strip()
    # heuristic: نام متغیر محیطی معمولاً با حروف بزرگ و underscore همراه است
    if v and v.upper() == v and ("_" in v or v.isalpha() and len(v) <= 32):
        return os.getenv(v, "")
    return value

def load_config(path: Optional[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    خواندن config.json (اگر موجود باشد) و پر کردن مقادیر حساس از env.
    خروجی: دیکشنری ساده که می‌توان برای ساخت Settings یا استفاده مستقیم به کار برد.
    """
    config_file = path or next((p for p in CONFIG_PATHS if os.path.exists(p)), None)
    cfg: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    if config_file:
        try:
            with open(config_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
                cfg = json.load(fh) or {}
        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception("Failed to load config file %s: %s", config_file, e)
            cfg = {}
    else:
        # fallback to minimal defaults
        cfg = {}

    # normalize reporter config (ساده‌ترین شکل ممکن)
    reporter = cfg.get("reporter", {})
    # reporter.api_base می‌تواند در فایل یا در env باشد; اگر reporter.api_key_env_var ست شده باشد از آن استفاده شود
    api_key_env = reporter.get("api_key_env_var") or os.getenv("PANEL_API_KEY")
    if api_key_env:
        # اگر مقدار api_key_env خودش نام متغیر است (مثلاً "PANEL_API_KEY"), resolve کند
        reporter["api_key"] = os.getenv(api_key_env, os.getenv("PANEL_API_KEY", reporter.get("api_key", "")))
    else:
        # fallback: مستقیماً مقدار api_key در config یا env PANEL_API_KEY
        reporter["api_key"] = reporter.get("api_key") or os.getenv("PANEL_API_KEY", "")

    reporter["api_base"] = reporter.get("api_base") or os.getenv("PANEL_API_BASE", "http://localhost:8000/admin/api/report")
    cfg["reporter"] = reporter

    # bot related: اگر فایل config نام یک env var را دارد، resolve کن
    bot = cfg.get("bot", {})
    token_env = bot.get("token_env_var")
    if token_env:
        bot["token"] = os.getenv(token_env, bot.get("token", ""))
    else:
        bot["token"] = bot.get("token") or os.getenv("BOT_TOKEN") or os.getenv("bot_token")
    cfg["bot"] = bot

    # دیگر مقادیر مهم که ممکن است به صورت رشته در env باشند => normalize
    # برای مثال CHANNEL_CODES ممکن است به عنوان JSON string ارائه شده باشد
    if isinstance(cfg.get("CHANNEL_CODES"), str):
        s = cfg["CHANNEL_CODES"]
        try:
            cfg["CHANNEL_CODES"] = json.loads(s)
        except Exception:
            try:
                cfg["CHANNEL_CODES"] = ast.literal_eval(s)
            except Exception:
                cfg["CHANNEL_CODES"] = {}

    # merge simple env fallbacks for top-level keys (مثال: start_date)
    for key in ("start_date", "log_file", "loop_mode", "loop_interval"):
        if key not in cfg or cfg.get(key) in (None, ""):
            envv = os.getenv(key.upper())
            if envv is not None:
                cfg[key] = envv

    return cfg

# convenience: load at import time
CONFIG = load_config()

# Paths (برای سازگاری با کدهای فعلی)
BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
ROOT_DIR = BASE_DIR.parent
DB_DIR = ROOT_DIR / "data"
DB_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # --- Telegram/API ---
    api_id: Optional[int] = Field(default=None, alias="api_id")
    api_hash: Optional[str] = Field(default="", alias="api_hash")
    phone: str = Field(default="", alias="phone")
    bot_token: str = Field(default="", alias="bot_token")

    # --- Channels ---
    source_channels: Union[List[str], str] = Field(default_factory=list, alias="source_channels")
    target_channel: str = Field(default="", alias="target_channel")
    admin_chat_id: Optional[Union[int, str]] = Field(default=None, alias="admin_chat_id")

    # --- Messaging ---
    disable_web_preview: bool = Field(default=False, alias="disable_web_preview")

    # --- Database ---
    database_url: str = Field(
        default=f"sqlite+aiosqlite:///{(DB_DIR / 'asa-sanat.db').as_posix()}",
        alias="database_url"
    )

    # --- Tunables ---
    crawl_delay_seconds: float = Field(default=5.0, alias="crawl_delay_seconds")
    crawl_limit: int = Field(default=100, alias="crawl_limit")
    send_delay_seconds: float = Field(default=5.0, alias="send_delay_seconds")
    send_batch_size: int = Field(default=20, alias="send_batch_size")
    send_concurrency: int = Field(default=3, alias="send_concurrency")
    send_max_retries: int = Field(default=3, alias="send_max_retries")
    send_max_per_run: int = Field(default=50, alias="send_max_per_run")

    # --- Channel codes ---
    CHANNEL_CODES: Dict[str, int] = Field(default_factory=dict, alias="CHANNEL_CODES")

    model_config = SettingsConfigDict(
        env_file=str(ROOT_DIR / ".env"),
        env_file_encoding="utf-8",
        case_sensitive=False,
        extra="ignore",
    )

    @field_validator("disable_web_preview", mode="before")
    def _bool_cast(cls, v):
        if isinstance(v, str):
            return v.strip().lower() in ("1", "true", "yes", "on")
        return bool(v)

    @field_validator("source_channels", mode="before")
    def _split_channels(cls, v: Any) -> List[str]:
        items: List[str] = []
        if isinstance(v, str):
            s = v.strip()
            if s.startswith("[") and s.endswith("]"):
                try:
                    data = json.loads(s)
                    if isinstance(data, list):
                        items = [str(x) for x in data]
                except Exception:
                    items = [x.strip() for x in s.strip("[]").split(",") if x.strip()]
            else:
                items = [x.strip() for x in s.split(",") if x.strip()]
        elif isinstance(v, list):
            items = [str(x) for x in v]

        norm = []
        seen = set()
        for c in (x.strip().lstrip("@").lower() for x in items):
            if c and c not in seen:
                seen.add(c)
                norm.append(c)
        return norm

    @field_validator("CHANNEL_CODES", mode="before")
    def _parse_channel_codes(cls, v: Any) -> Dict[str, int]:
        data = None
        if isinstance(v, dict):
            data = v
        elif isinstance(v, str):
            s = v.strip()
            if s:
                try:
                    data = json.loads(s)
                except Exception:
                    try:
                        data = ast.literal_eval(s)
                    except Exception:
                        data = {}
        if isinstance(data, dict):
            return {str(k).strip().lstrip("@").lower(): int(v) for k, v in data.items()}
        return {}

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def _post_checks(self):
        # نمادین: حداقل یکی از bot_token یا phone باید ارائه شود (همان منطق قبلی)
        if not self.bot_token and not self.phone:
            logger.warning("Neither bot_token nor phone provided in Settings — some features may be disabled.")
        if self.crawl_delay_seconds <= 0:
            raise ValueError("crawl_delay_seconds must be > 0.")
        if self.send_delay_seconds <= 0:
            raise ValueError("send_delay_seconds must be > 0.")
        for name in ["send_batch_size", "send_concurrency", "send_max_retries", "send_max_per_run"]:
            if getattr(self, name) < 1:
                raise ValueError(f"{name} must be >= 1.")
        # cross-check
        for ch in self.source_channels:
            if ch not in (self.CHANNEL_CODES or {}):
                logger.debug(f"Source channel '{ch}' has no code in CHANNEL_CODES.")
        return self

    # helper
    def get_sync_db_url(self) -> str:
        replacements = {
            "sqlite+aiosqlite": "sqlite",
            "postgresql+asyncpg": "postgresql",
            "mysql+aiomysql": "mysql",
        }
        for async_driver, sync_driver in replacements.items():
            if self.database_url.startswith(async_driver):
                return self.database_url.replace(async_driver, sync_driver, 1)
        return self.database_url

    def channel_codes_normalized(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        return {k.lower().lstrip("@"): int(v) for k, v in (self.CHANNEL_CODES or {}).items()}

    def source_channels_normalized(self) -> List[str]:
        return self._split_channels(self.source_channels)

# ساخت شیء settings با تلاش برای استفاده از CONFIG از فایل قبل از env
try:
    # اگر CONFIG حاوی مقادیر است، سعی می‌کنیم آن را به Settings پاس دهیم.
    if CONFIG:
        settings = Settings(**CONFIG)
    else:
        settings = Settings()  # خواندن مستقیم از env/.env به عنوان fallback
except Exception as e:
    logger.exception("Failed to initialize Settings from CONFIG: %s. Falling back to env/.env", e)
    try:
        settings = Settings()
    except Exception as e2:
        logger.exception("Fatal: cannot initialize Settings: %s", e2)
        # حداقل یک شیء placeholder بساز
        settings = None

########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/db/base.py

"""
src/db/base.py

Sync SQLAlchemy Engine + Declarative Base + PRAGMA setup for synchronous SQLite connections.

این فایل فقط:
  1. Base مشترک ORM را تعریف می‌کند.
  2. موتور اتصال همگام (sync_engine) را می‌سازد.
  3. PRAGMAهای ضروری را برای هر اتصال جدید SQLite اعمال می‌کند.
  - موتور async و سشن‌های async در session.py تعریف شده‌اند.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

from sqlalchemy import create_engine, event
from sqlalchemy.orm import declarative_base
from src.core.config import settings

# ---------- SYNC ENGINE ----------
DATABASE_URL_SYNC: str = settings.get_sync_db_url()

engine = create_engine(
    DATABASE_URL_SYNC,
    connect_args={"check_same_thread": False},
    future=True,
)

# ---------- Declarative Base ----------
Base = declarative_base()

# ---------- SQLite PRAGMA Setup ----------
@event.listens_for(engine, "connect")
def _set_sqlite_pragmas_for_sync(dbapi_connection, connection_record):
    """
    Set recommended PRAGMA values for SQLite on each new sync connection.

    - WAL mode improves concurrency.
    - Synchronous=NORMAL for better balance between speed and safety.
    - Enforce foreign key constraints.
    """
    try:
        cur = dbapi_connection.cursor()
        cur.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
        cur.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
        cur.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON;")
        cur.close()
    except Exception:
        # Non-SQLite backends or unusual drivers will ignore silently.
        pass

# src/db/models.py
from sqlalchemy import (
    Column, Integer, String, Text, DateTime, Enum, Boolean,
    UniqueConstraint, func, Index
)
from src.db.base import Base
import enum

class PostStatus(str, enum.Enum):
    pending = "pending"
    sending = "sending"
    sent = "sent"
    failed = "failed"
    skipped = "skipped"

class Post(Base):
    __tablename__ = "posts"

    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, autoincrement=True)
    source_channel = Column(String, nullable=False, index=True)
    source_id = Column(Integer, nullable=False, index=True)
    channel_key = Column(String, nullable=False, index=True)

    raw_text = Column(Text)
    title = Column(String)
    location = Column(String)
    category = Column(String)
    tags = Column(Text)        # JSON string (or NULL)
    phone = Column(String)
    links = Column(Text)       # JSON string (or NULL)
    processed_text = Column(Text)

    serial = Column(Integer, nullable=False)
    serial_code = Column(String, index=True, nullable=False)
    jalali_date = Column(String, nullable=False, index=True)

    status = Column(Enum(PostStatus), nullable=False, default=PostStatus.pending, index=True)
    sent = Column(Boolean, nullable=False, default=False, index=True)
    try_count = Column(Integer, nullable=False, default=0)
    last_error = Column(Text)

    claim_token = Column(String, index=True)
    sending_at = Column(DateTime)
    next_retry_at = Column(DateTime)

    created_at = Column(DateTime, server_default=func.current_timestamp(), nullable=False)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, server_default=func.current_timestamp(),
                        onupdate=func.current_timestamp(), nullable=False)
    sent_at = Column(DateTime)

    __table_args__ = (
    UniqueConstraint("source_channel", "source_id", name="uq_posts_source"),
    UniqueConstraint("channel_key", "serial", name="uq_posts_serial"),
    Index("ix_posts_channel_created", "source_channel", "created_at"),
)

    def __repr__(self):
        return f"<Post id={self.id} src={self.source_channel}:{self.source_id} serial={self.serial_code}>"

class PostCounter(Base):
    __tablename__ = "post_counters"

    # composite primary key: channel_key + jalali_date (day-by-day counter)
    channel_key = Column(String, primary_key=True)
    jalali_date = Column(String, primary_key=True)
    value = Column(Integer, nullable=False, default=0)

    def __repr__(self):
        return f"<PostCounter {self.channel_key} {self.jalali_date}={self.value}>"
class Favorite(Base):
    __tablename__ = "favorites"

    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, autoincrement=True)
    user_id = Column(Integer, index=True, nullable=False)
    post_id = Column(Integer, nullable=False, index=True)  # FK نرم‌افزاری؛ قیود در schema.sql است
    created_at = Column(DateTime, server_default=func.current_timestamp(), nullable=False)

# src/db/schema.py
from pathlib import Path
import logging
import sqlite3
from sqlalchemy import text
from src.db.base import Base
from src.db.session import async_engine
from src import logger_setup

logger = logging.getLogger("asa.schema")

def _apply_script_sync(sync_conn, sql_text: str):
    """
    اجرای امن SQL چندبخشی روی کانکشن sync.
    - برای SQLite: استفاده از executescript
    - برای سایر دیتابیس‌ها: اجرای تک‌به‌تک دستورات
    """
    # حذف خطوطی که با # شروع می‌شوند (کامنت ناسازگار با SQLite)
    sql_text = "\n".join(
        line for line in sql_text.splitlines()
        if not line.strip().startswith("#")
    )

    driver_conn = None
    try:
        driver_conn = getattr(sync_conn, "connection", None) or getattr(sync_conn, "driver_connection", None)
    except Exception:
        pass

    # مسیر SQLite
    if isinstance(driver_conn, sqlite3.Connection):
        try:
            driver_conn.executescript(sql_text)
            logger.info("Applied SQL script via sqlite3.executescript")
            return
        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception("sqlite3.executescript failed: %s", e)
            # اجرای fallback split
            for stmt in [s.strip() for s in sql_text.split(";") if s.strip()]:
                try:
                    sync_conn.execute(text(stmt))
                except Exception as e2:
                    logger.warning("Failed statement: %s ... %s", stmt[:80], e2)
            return

    # مسیر دیتابیس‌های غیر SQLite
    for stmt in [s.strip() for s in sql_text.split(";") if s.strip()]:
        try:
            sync_conn.execute(text(stmt))
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning("Failed statement: %s ... %s", stmt[:80], e)

async def ensure_schema():
    """
    ساخت جداول ORM و سپس اجرای schema.sql
    """
    schema_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "schema.sql"

    async with async_engine.begin() as conn:
        # ساخت جداول ORM
        await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
        logger.info("Ensured ORM tables from Base.metadata.create_all")

        if not schema_path.exists():
            logger.info("schema.sql not found at %s", schema_path)
            return

        try:
            sql_text = schema_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace").strip()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception("Failed to read schema.sql: %s", e)
            return

        if not sql_text:
            logger.info("schema.sql is empty; skipping")
            return

        try:
            await conn.run_sync(_apply_script_sync, sql_text)
            logger.info("Applied schema.sql from %s", schema_path)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception("Error applying schema.sql: %s", e)

FILE: src/src/db/schema.sql
########################################################################################################################

-- /src/db/schema.sql

PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS posts (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    source_channel TEXT NOT NULL,
    source_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    channel_key TEXT NOT NULL,
    raw_text TEXT,
    title TEXT,
    location TEXT,
    category TEXT,
    tags TEXT,
    phone TEXT,
    links TEXT,
    processed_text TEXT,
    serial INTEGER NOT NULL,
    serial_code TEXT NOT NULL,
    jalali_date TEXT NOT NULL,
    status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending'
        CHECK (status IN ('pending','sending','sent','failed','skipped')),
    sent INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (sent IN (0,1)),
    try_count INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    last_error TEXT,
    claim_token TEXT,
    sending_at DATETIME,
    next_retry_at DATETIME,
    created_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    sent_at DATETIME,
    UNIQUE (source_channel, source_id),
    UNIQUE (channel_key, serial)
);

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS uq_posts_source
    ON posts (source_channel, source_id);

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS uq_posts_serial
    ON posts (channel_key, serial);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS ix_posts_serial_code
    ON posts (serial_code);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS ix_posts_channel_created
    ON posts (source_channel, created_at);

-- شمارنده قدیمی (روزانه) برای fallback
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS post_counters (
    channel_key TEXT NOT NULL,
    jalali_date TEXT NOT NULL,
    value INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    PRIMARY KEY (channel_key, jalali_date)
);

-- شمارنده جدید (یک شمارنده به‌ازای هر کانال)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS post_counters_v2 (
    channel_key TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    value INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
);

-- علاقه‌مندی‌ها: نگاشت کاربر→پست
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS favorites (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    post_id INTEGER NOT NULL REFERENCES posts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    created_at DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE (user_id, post_id)
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS ix_favorites_user ON favorites(user_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS ix_favorites_post ON favorites(post_id);

# src/db/session.py
from sqlalchemy import event
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import create_async_engine, AsyncSession
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker

from src.core.config import settings
from src.db.base import engine as sync_engine  # موجود در base.py

# ---------- SYNC SESSION FACTORY ----------
SessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=sync_engine, autocommit=False, autoflush=False)

# ---------- ASYNC ENGINE ----------
ASYNC_DATABASE_URL = settings.database_url  # e.g. sqlite+aiosqlite:///path/to.db

async_engine = create_async_engine(
    ASYNC_DATABASE_URL,
    future=True,
    echo=False,
)

@event.listens_for(async_engine.sync_engine, "connect")
def _set_sqlite_pragmas_async(dbapi_connection, connection_record):
    try:
        cur = dbapi_connection.cursor()
        cur.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
        cur.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
        cur.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON;")
        cur.close()
    except Exception:
        pass

async_session = sessionmaker(async_engine, expire_on_commit=False, class_=AsyncSession)

# src/db/upsert.py
import json
from sqlalchemy.dialects.sqlite import insert as sqlite_insert
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from src.db.models import Post, PostStatus
from src.services.serial import atomic_next_serial_async, atomic_next_serial, make_serial_code
from src.utils.date_utils import to_jalali_code  # فرض: تبدیل datetime/str -> 'YYYYMMDD'

# helper: convert lists/strings -> JSON array string or None
def _to_json_array_or_null(val):
    if val is None:
        return None
    if isinstance(val, (list, tuple)):
        if not val:
            return None
        return json.dumps(list(val), ensure_ascii=False)
    if isinstance(val, str):
        s = val.strip()
        if not s:
            return None
        return json.dumps([s], ensure_ascii=False)
    # other types -> stringify into single element array
    return json.dumps([str(val)], ensure_ascii=False)

def _sanitize_post_data(input_data: dict) -> dict:
    """
    Keep only columns defined on Post.__table__ and perform minimal casts.
    Caller is responsible to ensure 'channel_key', 'source_channel' and 'source_id' are present.
    """
    allowed = {c.name for c in Post.__table__.columns}
    out = {}
    for k, v in input_data.items():
        if k not in allowed:
            continue
        # minimal cast for integer fields
        if k == "source_id" and v is not None:
            try:
                out[k] = int(v)
            except Exception:
                out[k] = v
        else:
            out[k] = v
    return out

# ---------------- ASYNC ----------------
async def upsert_post_async(db: AsyncSession, data: dict):
    """
    Insert or update a Post row atomically (async).
    Excluded fields from update: id, jalali_date, serial, serial_code.
    Commits on success; rolls back on error.
    """
    if not data.get("jalali_date"):
        if "created_at" in data and data["created_at"]:
            data["jalali_date"] = to_jalali_code(data["created_at"])
        else:
            raise ValueError("jalali_date or created_at is required")

    # get next serial (1-based int) for (channel_key, jalali_date)
    serial_num = await atomic_next_serial_async(db, data["channel_key"], data["jalali_date"])
    data["serial"] = serial_num
    data["serial_code"] = make_serial_code(data["jalali_date"], data["channel_key"], serial_num)

    # prepare JSON fields
    for fld in ("tags", "links"):
        data[fld] = _to_json_array_or_null(data.get(fld))

    # sanitize to allowed columns only
    insert_data = _sanitize_post_data(data)

    # ensure status is enum instance if provided as string
    if "status" in insert_data and insert_data["status"] is not None:
        if not isinstance(insert_data["status"], PostStatus):
            try:
                insert_data["status"] = PostStatus(insert_data["status"])
            except Exception:
                # leave as-is; DB/ORM may coerce or raise
                pass

    table = Post.__table__
    stmt = sqlite_insert(table).values(**insert_data)

    # prepare excluded->update mapping
    exclude = {"id", "jalali_date", "serial", "serial_code"}
    update_map = {
        col: getattr(stmt.excluded, col.name)
        for col in table.columns
        if col.name not in exclude
    }

    stmt = stmt.on_conflict_do_update(
        index_elements=["source_channel", "source_id"],
        set_=update_map
    )

    try:
        await db.execute(stmt)
        await db.commit()
    except Exception:
        await db.rollback()
        raise

# ---------------- SYNC ----------------
def upsert_post(session: Session, data: dict):
    """
    Sync version of upsert_post.
    """
    if not data.get("jalali_date"):
        if "created_at" in data and data["created_at"]:
            data["jalali_date"] = to_jalali_code(data["created_at"])
        else:
            raise ValueError("jalali_date or created_at is required")

    serial_num = atomic_next_serial(session, data["channel_key"], data["jalali_date"])
    data["serial"] = serial_num
    data["serial_code"] = make_serial_code(data["jalali_date"], data["channel_key"], serial_num)

    for fld in ("tags", "links"):
        data[fld] = _to_json_array_or_null(data.get(fld))

    insert_data = _sanitize_post_data(data)

    if "status" in insert_data and insert_data["status"] is not None:
        if not isinstance(insert_data["status"], PostStatus):
            try:
                insert_data["status"] = PostStatus(insert_data["status"])
            except Exception:
                pass

    table = Post.__table__
    stmt = sqlite_insert(table).values(**insert_data)

    exclude = {"id", "jalali_date", "serial", "serial_code"}
    update_map = {
        col: getattr(stmt.excluded, col.name)
        for col in table.columns
        if col.name not in exclude
    }

    stmt = stmt.on_conflict_do_update(
        index_elements=["source_channel", "source_id"],
        set_=update_map
    )

    try:
        session.execute(stmt)
        session.commit()
    except Exception:
        session.rollback()
        raise
