#/root/ASASANATBOT/src/job_runner.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# job_runner نهایی: تولید run_id، قفل فایل، اجرای crawler/sender با env، لاگ ساخت‌یافته،
# ذخیره گزارش هر اجرا در reports/, و ارسال خلاصهٔ روزانه به تلگرام.

import sys
import os
import time
import json
import re
import subprocess
import uuid
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
import traceback
import logger_setup
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger("job_runner")  # define once

def slog(obj: dict):
    try:
        logger.info(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
    except Exception:
        logger.info(str(obj))


# ----------------------------
# مسیرها و خواندن کانفیگ
# ----------------------------
CONFIG_PATH = Path(os.getenv("ASASANAT_CONFIG", "/root/ASASANATBOT/config.json"))
REPORTS_DIR = Path(os.getenv("REPORTS_DIR", "/root/ASASANATBOT/reports"))
DAILY_REPORT_FILE = Path(os.getenv("DAILY_REPORT_FILE", "/root/ASASANATBOT/daily_report.json"))
LOCK_FILE = Path(os.getenv("JOB_RUNNER_LOCK", "/root/ASASANATBOT/job_runner.lock"))

REPORTS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

if not CONFIG_PATH.exists():
    print(f"Config not found at {CONFIG_PATH}", file=sys.stderr)
    sys.exit(2)

with open(CONFIG_PATH, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    config = json.load(f)


# تابع کمکی برای لاگ ساخت‌یافته تک‌خط (برای پارس آسان توسط job_runner)
def slog(obj: dict):
    try:
        logger.info(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
    except Exception:
        logger.info(str(obj))

# ----------------------------
# تولید run_id و قفل
# ----------------------------
def make_run_id():
    # فرمت خوانا به همراه UUID کوتاه
    return f"run-{datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime('%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ')}-{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"

def acquire_lock(lockfile: Path = LOCK_FILE):
    if lockfile.exists():
        try:
            pid = lockfile.read_text().strip()
            logger.warning(f"Lock file exists ({lockfile}), pid={pid} — aborting this run.")
        except Exception:
            logger.warning(f"Lock file exists ({lockfile}) — aborting this run.")
        return False
    try:
        lockfile.write_text(str(os.getpid()))
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception(f"Cannot write lock file {lockfile}: {e}")
        return False

def release_lock(lockfile: Path = LOCK_FILE):
    try:
        if lockfile.exists():
            lockfile.unlink()
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception(f"Error removing lock file: {e}")

# ----------------------------
# آمار (per-run) — هر اجرا جدا ذخیره می‌شود
# ----------------------------
def make_empty_stats(run_id):
    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
    return {
        "run_id": run_id,
        "started_at": now,
        "finished_at": None,
        "date": now.split("T", 1)[0],
        "crawler": {
            "started_at": None, "finished_at": None,
            "success": 0, "fail": 0,
            "items": 0, "total_fetched": 0, "total_new": 0, "from_date": None
        },
        "sender": {
            "started_at": None, "finished_at": None,
            "success": 0, "fail": 0,
            "items": 0, "total_attempted": 0, "total_sent": 0, "total_unsent": 0
        },
        "total_duration": 0.0,
        # نگه داشتن خروجی فشرده از زیرفرآیندها برای دیباگ سریع
        "steps": []
    }

# ----------------------------
# پارسر خروجی‌ها (crawler / sender)
# parse_func باید signature: (output_str, stats) داشته باشد
# ----------------------------
def parse_crawler_output(output: str, stats: dict):
    total_fetched = None
    total_new = None
    for line in output.splitlines():
        low = line.lower()
        m_from = re.search(r"(from[-_ ]?date)\s*[:=]\s*([0-9\-]+)", low)
        if m_from and not stats["crawler"]["from_date"]:
            stats["crawler"]["from_date"] = m_from.group(2)
        m_chan = re.search(r"fetched=(\d+).*?new=(\d+)", line)
        if m_chan:
            try:
                stats["crawler"]["total_fetched"] = stats["crawler"].get("total_fetched", 0) + int(m_chan.group(1))
                stats["crawler"]["total_new"] = stats["crawler"].get("total_new", 0) + int(m_chan.group(2))
            except Exception:
                pass
        m_tot = re.search(r"Crawler finished.*?total_fetched=(\d+)\s+total_new=(\d+)", line)
        if m_tot:
            try:
                total_fetched = int(m_tot.group(1)); total_new = int(m_tot.group(2))
            except Exception:
                pass
    if total_fetched is not None:
        stats["crawler"]["total_fetched"] = total_fetched
    if total_new is not None:
        stats["crawler"]["total_new"] = total_new
    if not stats["crawler"]["from_date"]:
        stats["crawler"]["from_date"] = config.get("start_date")
    stats["crawler"]["items"] = stats["crawler"].get("total_new", 0)

def parse_sender_output(output: str, stats: dict):
    attempted = None; sent = None; unsent_after = None
    for line in output.splitlines():
        m_pending = re.search(r"Pending posts to send:\s*(\d+)", line)
        if m_pending:
            try: attempted = int(m_pending.group(1))
            except: pass
        m_complete = re.search(r"Run complete\.\s*sent=(\d+)\s*/\s*attempted=(\d+)", line)
        if m_complete:
            try:
                sent = int(m_complete.group(1)); attempted = int(m_complete.group(2))
            except: pass
        m_unsent = re.search(r"DB after run.*?unsent=(\d+)", line)
        if m_unsent:
            try: unsent_after = int(m_unsent.group(1))
            except: pass
    if attempted is not None:
        stats["sender"]["total_attempted"] = attempted
    if sent is not None:
        stats["sender"]["total_sent"] = sent
    if unsent_after is not None:
        stats["sender"]["total_unsent"] = unsent_after
    stats["sender"]["items"] = stats["sender"].get("total_sent", 0)

# ----------------------------
# اجرای یک دستور فرعی با env تزریق‌شده (RUN_ID) و ثبت خروجی
# ----------------------------
def run_subprocess(name: str, cmd: list, env_vars: dict, stats: dict, step_name: str, parse_func=None):
    t0 = time.time()
    slog({"ev": "step.start", "step": step_name, "run_id": stats["run_id"], "cmd": cmd, "ts": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()})
    # آماده‌سازی env (اجرای زیرفرآیند با RUN_ID در env)
    env = os.environ.copy()
    if env_vars:
        env.update(env_vars)
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, env=env)
        duration = round(time.time() - t0, 3)
        stdout = (result.stdout or "").strip()
        stderr = (result.stderr or "").strip()
        ok = result.returncode == 0

        # ثبت ساخت‌یافتهٔ خلاصه
        slog({
            "ev": "step.done",
            "step": step_name,
            "run_id": stats["run_id"],
            "returncode": result.returncode,
            "duration_s": duration,
            "ok": ok,
            "stdout_snip": stdout[:800],
            "stderr_snip": stderr[:800]
        })

        # ذخیرهٔ خلاصه به stats.steps
        stats["steps"].append({
            "step": step_name, "ok": ok, "returncode": result.returncode,
            "duration_s": duration, "cmd": cmd
        })

        # پارس خروجی در صورت ارائه شده
        combined = "\n".join([s for s in [stdout, stderr] if s])
        if parse_func and combined:
            try:
                parse_func(combined, stats)
            except Exception:
                logger.exception("Error in parse_func for %s", step_name)

        return {"ok": ok, "returncode": result.returncode, "stdout": stdout, "stderr": stderr, "duration": duration}
    except Exception as e:
        duration = round(time.time() - t0, 3)
        logger.exception("Exception running subprocess %s: %s", name, e)
        stats["steps"].append({"step": step_name, "ok": False, "returncode": -1, "duration_s": duration, "cmd": cmd})
        slog({"ev": "step.error", "step": step_name, "run_id": stats["run_id"], "err": str(e)})
        return {"ok": False, "returncode": -1, "stdout": "", "stderr": str(e), "duration": duration}

# ----------------------------
# ذخیرهٔ گزارش هر run و روزانه
# ----------------------------
def save_run_report(stats: dict):
    try:
        REPORTS_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        p = REPORTS_DIR / f"{stats['run_id']}.json"
        p.write_text(json.dumps(stats, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
        # همچنین به daily_report مینویسیم (خلاصه آخرین اجرا)
        DAILY_REPORT_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(stats, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception("Error saving run report: %s", e)

# ----------------------------
# src/job_runner.py (جایگزین کامل تابع send_telegram_summary)

def send_telegram_summary(stats: dict):
    try:
        token = config.get("telegram_bot_token")
        chat_id = config.get("telegram_chat_id")
        if not token or not chat_id:
            logger.info("Telegram not configured; skipping summary send.")
            return

        msg = (
            f"📊 Report {stats['date']} ({stats['run_id']})\n"
            f"Crawler: fetched={stats['crawler'].get('total_fetched',0)} new={stats['crawler'].get('total_new',0)}\n"
            f"Sender: attempted={stats['sender'].get('total_attempted',0)} sent={stats['sender'].get('total_sent',0)} unsent={stats['sender'].get('total_unsent',0)}\n"
            f"Total duration: {round(stats['total_duration'],2)}s"
        )

        import requests
        url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{token}/sendMessage"
        payload = {"chat_id": chat_id, "text": msg, "parse_mode": "Markdown"}
        resp = requests.post(url, json=payload, timeout=10)
        if resp.status_code != 200:
            logger.warning("Telegram summary send failed: %s %s", resp.status_code, resp.text[:200])
    except Exception as e:
        logger.exception("send_telegram_summary error: %s", e)

# ----------------------------
# اجرای یک دور کامل (one run)
# ----------------------------
def run_once():
    # ساخت run_id و stats اولیه
    run_id = make_run_id()
    stats = make_empty_stats(run_id)

    if not acquire_lock():
        logger.error("Could not acquire lock — exiting run.")
        return

    slog({"ev": "job.start", "run_id": run_id, "ts": stats["started_at"]})
    try:
        # Inject RUN_ID into env for subprocesses
        env_vars = {"RUN_ID": run_id}

        # ---------- crawler ----------
        stats["crawler"]["started_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
        crawler_cmd = [
            sys.executable, "-m", "src.services.crawler",
            "--limit", str(config.get("crawler_limit", 100)),
            "--from-date", str(config.get("start_date", ""))
        ]
        res_c = run_subprocess("Crawler", crawler_cmd, env_vars, stats, "crawler", parse_func=parse_crawler_output)
        stats["crawler"]["finished_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
        if res_c.get("ok"):
            stats["crawler"]["success"] += 1
        else:
            stats["crawler"]["fail"] += 1

        # sleep بین مراحل (قابل کانفیگ)
        time.sleep(config.get("sleep_between", 5))

        # ---------- sender ----------
        stats["sender"]["started_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
        sender_cmd = [
            sys.executable, "-m", "src.services.sender",
            "--limit", str(config.get("sender_limit", 100))
        ]
        res_s = run_subprocess("Sender", sender_cmd, env_vars, stats, "sender", parse_func=parse_sender_output)
        stats["sender"]["finished_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
        if res_s.get("ok"):
            stats["sender"]["success"] += 1
        else:
            stats["sender"]["fail"] += 1

        # زمان کل اجرا
        stats["finished_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
        try:
            sd = datetime.fromisoformat(stats["started_at"])
            fd = datetime.fromisoformat(stats["finished_at"])
            stats["total_duration"] = (fd - sd).total_seconds()
        except Exception:
            # fallback
            stats["total_duration"] = stats.get("total_duration", 0)

        # ذخیره گزارش run
        save_run_report(stats)

        # لاگ خلاصهٔ ساخت‌یافته
        slog({
            "ev": "job.finish",
            "run_id": run_id,
            "crawler": stats["crawler"],
            "sender": stats["sender"],
            "total_duration": stats["total_duration"]
        })

        # آستانه هشدار نمونه: اگر sender sent کمتر از 70% باشد، هشدار تلگرام
        try:
            attempted = stats["sender"].get("total_attempted", 0)
            sent = stats["sender"].get("total_sent", 0)
            if attempted > 0 and sent / attempted < 0.7:
                send_telegram_summary(stats)
        except Exception:
            pass

        # ذخیرهٔ daily_report (آخرین اجرا)
        try:
            DAILY_REPORT_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(stats, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
        except Exception:
            logger.exception("Could not write daily report file")

    except Exception:
        logger.exception("Unhandled exception in run_once: %s", traceback.format_exc())
    finally:
        release_lock()
        slog({"ev": "job.end", "run_id": run_id, "ts": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()})

# ----------------------------
# main: loop یا یکبار اجرا
# ----------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    if config.get("loop_mode"):
        interval = int(config.get("loop_interval", 600))
        logger.info("Loop mode enabled. interval=%s", interval)
        while True:
            run_once()
            time.sleep(interval)
    else:
        run_once()



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/logger_setup.py
########################################################################################################################

import logging
import sys
import os
from logging.handlers import RotatingFileHandler

LOG_DIR = os.getenv("LOG_DIR", "/app/data")
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, os.getenv("LOG_FILE_NAME", "important.log"))
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)

# اینجا یک logger نام‌دار بساز، نه root logger
logger = logging.getLogger("app")

if not logger.handlers:
    level_name = os.getenv("LOG_LEVEL", "INFO").upper()
    level = getattr(logging, level_name, logging.INFO)
    logger.setLevel(level)

    console_level_name = os.getenv("LOG_CONSOLE_LEVEL", level_name).upper()
    console_level = getattr(logging, console_level_name, level)

    try:
        max_bytes = int(os.getenv("LOG_MAX_BYTES", str(5*1024*1024)))
    except ValueError:
        max_bytes = 5*1024*1024
    try:
        backup_count = int(os.getenv("LOG_BACKUP_COUNT", "5"))
    except ValueError:
        backup_count = 5

    json_mode = os.getenv("LOG_JSON", "false").lower() in ("1", "true", "yes")

    console_handler = logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    console_handler.setLevel(console_level)

    file_handler = RotatingFileHandler(LOG_FILE, maxBytes=max_bytes, backupCount=backup_count)
    file_handler.setLevel(logging.WARNING)

    if json_mode:
        formatter = logging.Formatter(
            '{"time":"%(asctime)s","level":"%(levelname)s","name":"%(name)s","msg":"%(message)s"}',
            datefmt="%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S"
        )
    else:
        formatter = logging.Formatter(
            "%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s",
            datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
        )

    console_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
    file_handler.setFormatter(formatter)

    logger.addHandler(console_handler)
    logger.addHandler(file_handler)
# 👇 این قسمت رو اضافه کن
    for name in ("repository", "sender"):
        child_logger = logging.getLogger(name)
        child_logger.setLevel(level)
        child_logger.handlers = logger.handlers
        child_logger.propagate = False

# کاهش نویز لاگ‌های کتابخانه‌ها
logging.getLogger("sqlalchemy").setLevel(logging.WARNING)
logging.getLogger("aiogram").setLevel(logging.WARNING)

########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/api/router.py
########################################################################################################################

import os, hmac
from fastapi import APIRouter, Header, HTTPException
from fastapi.responses import HTMLResponse, RedirectResponse
from src.news.core.db import get_conn
from src.news.status import Status

API_TOKEN = os.getenv("NEWS_API_TOKEN", "")

router = APIRouter(prefix="/news", tags=["news"])

def auth(authorization: str = Header(None)):
    if not authorization or not authorization.startswith("Bearer "):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")
    token = authorization.split(" ", 1)[1]
    if not (API_TOKEN and hmac.compare_digest(token, API_TOKEN)):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Unauthorized")

@router.get("/review", response_class=HTMLResponse)
def review_page(authorization: str = Header(None)):
    auth(authorization)
    with get_conn() as conn:
        rows = conn.execute("SELECT id,title,excerpt,status FROM news_items WHERE status IN (?,?,?) LIMIT 50",
                            (Status.PENDING, Status.QUEUED, Status.REVIEW)).fetchall()
    html = "<h2>News Review</h2><table border=1>"
    html += "<tr><th>ID</th><th>Title</th><th>Status</th><th>Action</th></tr>"
    for r in rows:
        html += f"<tr><td>{r['id']}</td><td>{r['title']}</td><td>{r['status']}</td>"
        html += f"<td><a href='/news/review/{r['id']}?action=approve&auth={authorization}'>Approve</a> | "
        html += f"<a href='/news/review/{r['id']}?action=reject&auth={authorization}'>Reject</a></td></tr>"
    html += "</table>"
    return HTMLResponse(content=html)

@router.get("/review/{item_id}")
def review_action(item_id: int, action: str, authorization: str = Header(None)):
    auth(authorization)
    with get_conn() as conn:
        if action == "approve":
            conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=? WHERE id=?", (Status.APPROVED, item_id))
        elif action == "reject":
            conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=? WHERE id=?", (Status.REJECTED, item_id))
        else:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Invalid action")
    return RedirectResponse("/news/review", status_code=303)



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/classify.py
########################################################################################################################

import re, os
from .logger import log_json
from .utils import normalize_text
from .config import Config
from .status import Status

INDUSTRY_FA = [
    "صنعت","صنعتی","کارخانه","کارخانجات","واحد تولیدی","شهرک صنعتی","کارگر","کارگران","استخدام","استخدامی",
    "تولید","فولاد","پتروشیمی","سیمان","قطعه","قطعه‌سازی","خودرو","پالایشگاه","نیروگاه","کارآفرینی","تجارت","بازرگانی","مالیات","بهره‌وری","اشتغال","نیروی کار","کارآفرین","قرارداد کاری","حقوق کارگر","تولید ملی","صادرات"
]
ECON_FA = [
    "اقتصاد","اقتصادی","بورس","سهام","دلار","یورو","ارز","تورم","نفت","طلا","بازار","بودجه","بانک","وام","کالا","بورس کالا","بازار سرمایه","شرکت","سرمایه‌گذاری","سهامدار","سود","شاخص"
]
INDUSTRY_EN = [
    "industry","industrial","factory","plant","worker","labor","hiring","recruitment","manufacturing","steel",
    "petrochemical","cement","auto","refinery","power plant","mining"
]
ECON_EN = [
    "economy","economic","stock","market","dollar","euro","currency","inflation","oil","gold","budget","bank","loan","index","profit"
]

KEYWORDS = [*INDUSTRY_FA, *ECON_FA, *INDUSTRY_EN, *ECON_EN]
KW_RE = [re.compile(rf"\b{re.escape(k)}\b", re.IGNORECASE) for k in KEYWORDS]

TRUSTED_DOMAINS = ["mehrnews.com","reuters.com","isna.ir","ilna.ir","tgju.org"]

OPENAI_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", "")
USE_AI = bool(OPENAI_KEY)

def _source_weight(source_url: str) -> float:
    source_url = source_url or ""
    for dom in TRUSTED_DOMAINS:
        if dom in source_url:
            return 0.15
    return 0.0

def _kw_score(title: str, content: str) -> (float,int):
    title = normalize_text(title or "")
    content = normalize_text(content or "")
    score = 0.0
    hits = 0
    for rx in KW_RE:
        if rx.search(title):
            score += 0.0
            hits += 0
        elif rx.search(content):
            score += 0.3
            hits += 1
    if hits >= 1:
        score += 0.2
    if hits >= 2:
        score += 0.15
    if hits >= 4:
        score += 0.1

    return min(score, 1.0), hits

def _ai_boost(title: str, content: str) -> float:
    if not USE_AI:
        return 0.0
    try:
        return 0.0  # Placeholder برای آینده
    except Exception as e:
        log_json(module="classifier", action="ai_fail", error=str(e))
        return 0.0

def classify_item(item):
    title = item.get("title","")
    content = item.get("content","")
    source = item.get("source","")
    base, hits = _kw_score(title, content)
    srcw = _source_weight(source)
    aiw = _ai_boost(title, content)
    score = min(base + srcw + aiw, 1.0)

    if score >= Config.AUTOPUBLISH_THRESHOLD:
        status = Status.APPROVED
        category = "industry_economy"
    elif score >= Config.REVIEW_THRESHOLD:
        status = Status.REVIEW
        category = "industry_economy_candidate"
    else:
        status = Status.REJECTED
        category = "other"

    return {"score": score, "status": status, "category": category, "hits": hits}



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/collector.py
########################################################################################################################

import feedparser
from datetime import datetime
from .core.db import get_conn
from .utils import clean_text, excerpt, text_hash
from .logger import log_json
from .config import Config
from .status import Status

def collect_items(run_id: str):
    inserted_total = 0
    for feed_url in Config.RSS_FEEDS:
        try:
            feed = feedparser.parse(feed_url)
            if getattr(feed, 'bozo', False):
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="collector", feed_url=feed_url,
                         error="feed_parse_error", bozo_exception=str(getattr(feed, 'bozo_exception', '')))
                continue
            inserted = 0
            for entry in feed.entries[:5]:
                title = clean_text(entry.get("title", ""))
                content = clean_text(entry.get("summary", "") or entry.get("description", ""))
                ex = excerpt(content, 800)
                url = entry.get("link", "")
                source = feed_url
                c_hash = text_hash(title + ex)
                created_at = getattr(entry, 'published', None) or datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

                with get_conn() as conn:
                    exists = conn.execute("SELECT 1 FROM news_items WHERE content_hash=? LIMIT 1", (c_hash,)).fetchone()
                    if not exists:
                        conn.execute("""
                            INSERT INTO news_items
                            (title, content, excerpt, url, source, category, score, status, created_at, content_hash)
                            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                        """, (title, content, ex, url, source, None, 0.0, Status.PENDING, created_at, c_hash))
                        inserted += 1

            inserted_total += inserted
            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="collector", feed_url=feed_url, inserted=inserted)
        except Exception as e:
            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="collector", feed_url=feed_url, error=str(e))
    return inserted_total

########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/core/db.py

import os
import sqlite3
from contextlib import contextmanager
from ..config import Config

@contextmanager
def get_conn():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(
        Config.DB_PATH,
        detect_types=sqlite3.PARSE_DECLTYPES | sqlite3.PARSE_COLNAMES,
        check_same_thread=False
    )
    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    try:
        yield conn
        conn.commit()
    except Exception:
        conn.rollback()
        raise
    finally:
        conn.close()

def init_db():
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(Config.DB_PATH), exist_ok=True)
    with get_conn() as conn:
        conn.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS news_items (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
            title TEXT NOT NULL,
            content TEXT,
            excerpt TEXT,
            url TEXT,
            source TEXT,
            category TEXT,
            score REAL DEFAULT 0,
            attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
            status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
            created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
            sent_at DATETIME,
            review_sent_at DATETIME,
            content_hash TEXT,
            failed_reason TEXT,
            media_type TEXT,
            media_file TEXT,
            media_url TEXT,
            webhook_attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
            failed_reason_webhook TEXT,
            last_worker TEXT
        );
        """)
        conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_status ON news_items(status);")
        conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_category ON news_items(category);")
        conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_created_at ON news_items(created_at);")
        conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sent_at ON news_items(sent_at);")
        conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_content_hash ON news_items(content_hash);")
        conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_media_file ON news_items(media_file);")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    init_db()
    print("✅ Database initialized at", Config.DB_PATH)



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/dedupe.py
########################################################################################################################

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from rapidfuzz import fuzz
from .core.db import get_conn
from .config import Config
from .status import Status
from .logger import log_json
import time

def dedupe_items(run_id: str):
    start_ts = time.time()
    window_start = (datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=Config.DEDUP_WINDOW_HOURS)).isoformat()
    dup_count = 0
    with get_conn() as conn:
        rows = conn.execute("SELECT id, title, content_hash, created_at FROM news_items WHERE status = ?", (Status.PENDING,)).fetchall()
        for r in rows:
            item_id = r["id"]
            ch = r["content_hash"]
            title = r["title"] or ""
            if not ch or len(title) < 4:
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="dedupe", item_id=item_id, status="skip", reason="empty_hash_or_short_title")
                continue

            exists = conn.execute("SELECT id FROM news_items WHERE content_hash = ? AND id != ?", (ch, item_id)).fetchone()
            if exists:
                conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, failed_reason=? WHERE id=?", (Status.DUPLICATE, "hash_duplicate", item_id))
                dup_count += 1
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="dedupe", item_id=item_id, status=Status.DUPLICATE, reason="hash")
                continue

            similar_rows = conn.execute("SELECT id, title FROM news_items WHERE id != ? AND datetime(created_at) >= ?", (item_id, window_start)).fetchall()
            for sr in similar_rows:
                score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(title, sr["title"] or "") / 100.0
                if score >= Config.FUZZY_THRESHOLD:
                    conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, failed_reason=? WHERE id=?", (Status.DUPLICATE, f"fuzzy:{score:.2f}", item_id))
                    dup_count += 1
                    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="dedupe", item_id=item_id, status=Status.DUPLICATE, reason=f"fuzzy:{score:.2f}", threshold=Config.FUZZY_THRESHOLD)
                    break

    latency_ms = int((time.time() - start_ts) * 1000)
    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="dedupe", duplicates=dup_count, latency_ms=latency_ms)
    return dup_count

# src/news/formatter.py
from datetime import datetime
import html

def format_date_iso(ts: str) -> str:
    try:
        dt = datetime.fromisoformat(ts.replace("Z",""))
        return dt.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")
    except:
        return ts or ""

def html_escape(text: str) -> str:
    return html.escape(text or "")

def format_news_item_html(item):
    nid = item.get("id")
    date = format_date_iso(item.get("created_at",""))
    title = html_escape(item.get("title",""))
    content_raw = item.get("content","") or ""
    # افزایش سقف تا 3500 کاراکتر
    content = html_escape(content_raw[:3800])
    source = html_escape(item.get("source",""))
    url = html_escape(item.get("url","") or "")
    category = html_escape(item.get("category","") or "بدون دسته‌بندی")

    signature = "✍️ سامانه اخبار آسا صنعت — @ASASANATBOT"

    link_line = f"🔗 <a href=\"{url}\">مشاهده منبع</a>" if url else f"🌐 منبع: {source}"

    text = (
        f"📰 <b>{title}</b>\n\n"
        f"📅 <b>{date}</b>  |  🆔 <b>{nid}</b>\n"
        f"🏷️ <b>{category}</b>\n\n"
        f"📖 <b>{content}</b>\n\n"
        f"{link_line}\n\n"
        f"<i>{signature}</i>"
    )
    return text

import os
import logging
from logging.handlers import RotatingFileHandler
from .config import Config

os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(Config.LOG_PATH), exist_ok=True)

handler = RotatingFileHandler(Config.LOG_PATH, maxBytes=10_000_000, backupCount=5)
formatter = logging.Formatter('%(message)s')
handler.setFormatter(formatter)

logger = logging.getLogger("news")
logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
logger.addHandler(handler)

def log_json(**kwargs):
    import json, datetime
    kwargs["ts"] = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
    logger.info(json.dumps(kwargs, ensure_ascii=False))

########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/proc.py
########################################################################################################################

from .core.db import get_conn
from .utils import clean_text, excerpt
from .status import Status
from .logger import log_json
import time

def process_items(run_id: str):
    start_ts = time.time()
    count = 0
    with get_conn() as conn:
        rows = conn.execute("SELECT id, content FROM news_items WHERE status=?", (Status.PENDING,)).fetchall()
        for r in rows:
            item_id = r["id"]
            cleaned = clean_text(r["content"] or "")
            ex = excerpt(cleaned, 800)
            conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET content=?, excerpt=? WHERE id=?", (cleaned, ex, item_id))
            count += 1
            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="proc", item_id=item_id, status="processed")
    latency_ms = int((time.time() - start_ts) * 1000)
    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="proc", processed=count, latency_ms=latency_ms)
    return count



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/review_bot.py
########################################################################################################################

# src/news/review_bot.py
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime
from aiogram import Bot, Dispatcher
from aiogram.types import InlineKeyboardButton, InlineKeyboardMarkup, CallbackQuery
from .core.db import get_conn
from .config import Config
from .status import Status
from .logger import log_json
from aiogram.client.default import DefaultBotProperties
from aiogram.enums import ParseMode

bot = Bot(
    token=Config.TELEGRAM_TOKEN,
    default=DefaultBotProperties(parse_mode=ParseMode.HTML)
)
dp = Dispatcher()

async def _send_review_batch():
    with get_conn() as conn:
        rows = conn.execute(
            "SELECT id, title, excerpt, url, review_sent_at FROM news_items WHERE status=?",
            (Status.REVIEW,)
        ).fetchall()

    for r in rows:
        if r["review_sent_at"]:
            continue

        kb = InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=[[
            InlineKeyboardButton(text="✅ Approve", callback_data=f"approve:{r['id']}"),
            InlineKeyboardButton(text="❌ Reject", callback_data=f"reject:{r['id']}")
        ]])

        try:
            await bot.send_message(
                chat_id=Config.REVIEW_CHAT_ID,
                text=f"{r['title']}\n{r['excerpt']}\n{r['url']}",
                reply_markup=kb
            )
            with get_conn() as conn:
                conn.execute(
                    "UPDATE news_items SET review_sent_at=? WHERE id=?",
                    (datetime.utcnow().isoformat(), r["id"])
                )
            log_json(module="review_bot", item_id=r["id"], action="sent_for_review")
        except Exception as e:
            log_json(module="review_bot", item_id=r["id"], action="send_failed", reason=str(e))

async def review_callback(query: CallbackQuery):
    try:
        action, sid = query.data.split(":")
        item_id = int(sid)
    except Exception:
        await query.answer("❌ داده نامعتبر")
        return

    with get_conn() as conn:
        item = conn.execute("SELECT id, status FROM news_items WHERE id=?", (item_id,)).fetchone()
        if not item:
            await query.answer("❌ آیتم پیدا نشد")
            return

        if action == "approve":
            res = conn.execute(
                "UPDATE news_items SET status=? WHERE id=? AND status=?",
                (Status.APPROVED, item_id, Status.REVIEW)
            )
            if res.rowcount == 0:
                await query.message.answer("⚠️ قبلاً تغییر وضعیت داده شده است.")
            else:
                await query.message.edit_reply_markup(reply_markup=None)
                await query.message.answer(f"✅ Approved: {item_id}")
                log_json(module="review_bot", item_id=item_id, status=Status.APPROVED)

        elif action == "reject":
            res = conn.execute(
                "UPDATE news_items SET status=? WHERE id=? AND status=?",
                (Status.REJECTED, item_id, Status.REVIEW)
            )
            if res.rowcount == 0:
                await query.message.answer("⚠️ قبلاً تغییر وضعیت داده شده است.")
            else:
                await query.message.edit_reply_markup(reply_markup=None)
                await query.message.answer(f"❌ Rejected: {item_id}")
                log_json(module="review_bot", item_id=item_id, status=Status.REJECTED)

async def review_bot_main():
    # ثبت هندلرها به‌صورت صریح در v3
    dp.callback_query.register(review_callback)

    async def loop_sender():
        while True:
            await _send_review_batch()
            await asyncio.sleep(300)

    asyncio.create_task(loop_sender())
    await dp.start_polling(bot)



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/runner.py
########################################################################################################################

#src/news/runner.py
import asyncio, uuid, time, os
from .core.db import init_db, get_conn
from .collector import collect_items as collect_rss
from .tgju_rss_collector import collect_tgju_rss
from .tgju_widget_collector import collect_tgju_widget
from .telegram_collector import collect_from_channels_sync
from .dedupe import dedupe_items
from .proc import process_items
from .classify import classify_item
from .send import send_items
from .logger import log_json
from .status import Status

LOCK_PATH = os.getenv("JOB_RUNNER_LOCK", "/root/ASASANATBOT/data/job_runner.lock")

def acquire_lock():
    try:
        fd = os.open(LOCK_PATH, os.O_CREAT | os.O_EXCL | os.O_WRONLY)
        os.close(fd)
        return True
    except FileExistsError:
        try:
            if (time.time() - os.path.getmtime(LOCK_PATH)) > 3600:  # stale >1h
                os.remove(LOCK_PATH)
                fd = os.open(LOCK_PATH, os.O_CREAT | os.O_EXCL | os.O_WRONLY)
                os.close(fd)
                return True
        except Exception:
            pass
        return False

def release_lock():
    try:
        os.remove(LOCK_PATH)
    except:
        pass

def pipeline_run(run_id: str):
    if not acquire_lock():
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="runner", event="skip_pipeline", reason="lock_present")
        return

    start_ts = time.time()
    try:
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="runner", event="start_pipeline")

        inserted_rss = collect_rss(run_id)
        inserted_tgju_rss = collect_tgju_rss(run_id)
        inserted_tgju_widget = collect_tgju_widget(run_id)
        inserted_tg = collect_from_channels_sync(run_id, limit=int(os.getenv("tg_limit_per_source", os.getenv("rss_limit_per_source", "5")))
)

        dedupe_items(run_id)
        process_items(run_id)

        approved = review = rejected = 0
        with get_conn() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute(
                "SELECT id, title, content, source, created_at FROM news_items WHERE status=?",
                (Status.PENDING,)
            ).fetchall()
            for r in rows:
                item = {
                    "id": r["id"],
                    "title": r["title"],
                    "content": r["content"],
                    "source": r["source"],
                    "created_at": r["created_at"]
                }
                cls = classify_item(item)
                conn.execute(
                    "UPDATE news_items SET score=?, status=?, category=? WHERE id=?",
                    (cls["score"], cls["status"], cls["category"], r["id"])
                )
                if cls["status"] == Status.APPROVED:
                     approved += 1
                elif cls["status"] == Status.REVIEW:
                     review += 1
                else:
                     rejected += 1

        asyncio.run(send_items(run_id))

        latency_ms = int((time.time() - start_ts) * 1000)
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="runner", event="end_pipeline",
                 inserted_rss=inserted_rss, inserted_tgju_rss=inserted_tgju_rss,
                 inserted_tgju_widget=inserted_tgju_widget, inserted_tg=inserted_tg,
                 approved=approved, review=review, rejected=rejected, latency_ms=latency_ms)
    except Exception as e:
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="runner", error=str(e))
    finally:
        release_lock()

def scheduler_loop():
    init_db()
    while True:
        run_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        try:
            pipeline_run(run_id)
        except Exception as e:
            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="runner", error=str(e))
        time.sleep(int(os.getenv("SCHED_INTERVAL", "900")))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    scheduler_loop()



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/send.py
########################################################################################################################

# src/news/send.py
import asyncio, random, time, os
import aiohttp
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from .core.db import get_conn
from .config import Config
from .status import Status
from .logger import log_json
from .formatter import format_news_item_html

TG_API = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{Config.TELEGRAM_TOKEN}"
MAX_BACKOFF = 60
MAX_ATTEMPTS = int(os.getenv("SEND_MAX_RETRIES", "5"))
N8N_URL = Config.N8N_WEBHOOK_PATH
N8N_SECRET = Config.N8N_WEBHOOK_SECRET

def _format_msg(item):
    return format_news_item_html(item)

async def _backoff(attempt: int):
    delay = min(2 ** attempt + random.random(), MAX_BACKOFF)
    await asyncio.sleep(delay)

async def send_items(run_id: str):
    start_run = time.time()
    n8n_sent_count = 0
    async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
        with get_conn() as conn:
            rows = conn.execute("""
                SELECT id, title, excerpt, url, source, category, score, created_at, attempts, status
                FROM news_items
                WHERE status IN (?, ?)
                ORDER BY CASE WHEN status = ? THEN 0 ELSE 1 END, created_at ASC
            """, (Status.APPROVED, Status.QUEUED, Status.APPROVED)).fetchall()

        for r in rows:
            item_id = r["id"]

            # Claim اتمیک
            with get_conn() as conn:
                res = conn.execute(
                    "UPDATE news_items SET status=?, attempts=attempts+1 WHERE id=? AND status IN (?,?)",
                    (Status.SENDING, item_id, Status.APPROVED, Status.QUEUED)
                )
                if res.rowcount == 0:
                    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                             status="skip", reason="claimed_by_other_or_status_changed")
                    continue
                attempts = conn.execute("SELECT attempts FROM news_items WHERE id=?",
                                        (item_id,)).fetchone()["attempts"]

            if attempts > MAX_ATTEMPTS:
                with get_conn() as conn:
                    conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, failed_reason=? WHERE id=?",
                                 (Status.FAILED, f"max_attempts_{attempts}", item_id))
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                         status=Status.FAILED, reason="max_attempts")
                continue

            # Rate-limit
            now = datetime.utcnow()
            with get_conn() as conn:
                sent_this_hour = conn.execute(
                    "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM news_items WHERE status=? AND sent_at>=?",
                    (Status.SENT, (now - timedelta(hours=1)).isoformat())
                ).fetchone()[0]
                sent_today = conn.execute(
                    "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM news_items WHERE status=? AND sent_at>=?",
                    (Status.SENT, now.replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0).isoformat())
                ).fetchone()[0]

            if sent_this_hour >= Config.MAX_PER_HOUR or sent_today >= Config.MAX_PER_DAY:
                with get_conn() as conn:
                    conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=? WHERE id=?",
                                 (Status.QUEUED, item_id))
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                         status=Status.QUEUED, reason="rate_limit")
                continue

            # build item dict
            item = {
                "id": item_id,
                "title": r["title"],
                "content": r["excerpt"] or r["title"],
                "source": r["source"],
                "category": r["category"],
                "score": r["score"],
                "created_at": r["created_at"]
            }

            text = _format_msg(item)
            payload = {
                "chat_id": Config.NEWS_CHAT_ID,
                "text": text,
                "disable_web_page_preview": True,
                "parse_mode": "HTML"
            }

            send_ok = False
            try:
                resp = await session.post(f"{TG_API}/sendMessage", json=payload, timeout=15)
                status_code = resp.status

                if status_code == 429 or status_code >= 500:
                    reason = f"tg_http_{status_code}"
                    with get_conn() as conn:
                        conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, failed_reason=? WHERE id=?",
                                     (Status.QUEUED, reason, item_id))
                    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                             status=Status.QUEUED, reason=reason)
                    await _backoff(min(attempts+1, 6))
                    continue
                if status_code >= 400:
                    reason = f"tg_http_{status_code}"
                    with get_conn() as conn:
                        conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, failed_reason=? WHERE id=?",
                                     (Status.FAILED, reason, item_id))
                    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                             status=Status.FAILED, reason=reason)
                    continue

                send_ok = True
                sent_at = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
                with get_conn() as conn:
                    conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, sent_at=? WHERE id=?",
                                 (Status.SENT, sent_at, item_id))
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                         status=Status.SENT, sent_at=sent_at)

            except Exception as e:
                reason = f"tg_exc_{str(e)}"
                with get_conn() as conn:
                    conn.execute("UPDATE news_items SET status=?, failed_reason=? WHERE id=?",
                                 (Status.QUEUED, reason, item_id))
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                         status=Status.QUEUED, reason=str(e))
                await _backoff(min(attempts+1, 6))
                continue

            # n8n webhook (بدون تغییر status اصلی)
            if send_ok and N8N_URL and n8n_sent_count < 2:
                headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
                if N8N_SECRET:
                    headers[Config.N8N_SECRET_HEADER_NAME] = N8N_SECRET
                payload = {
                    "id": item_id,
                    "title": r["title"],
                    "excerpt": r["excerpt"],
                    "url": r["url"],
                    "source": r["source"],
                    "category": r["category"],
                    "score": r["score"],
                    "sent_at": sent_at
                }
                try:
                    wresp = await session.post(N8N_URL, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)
                    n8n_sent_count += 1
                    if wresp.status >= 400:
                        with get_conn() as conn:
                            conn.execute("""UPDATE news_items
                                            SET webhook_attempts=COALESCE(webhook_attempts,0)+1,
                                                failed_reason_webhook=?
                                            WHERE id=?""",
                                         (f"n8n_http_{wresp.status}", item_id))
                        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                                 status="webhook_failed", reason=f"n8n:{wresp.status}")
                except Exception as we:
                    with get_conn() as conn:
                        conn.execute("""UPDATE news_items
                                        SET webhook_attempts=COALESCE(webhook_attempts,0)+1,
                                            failed_reason_webhook=?
                                        WHERE id=?""",
                                     (f"n8n_exc_{str(we)}", item_id))
                    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", item_id=item_id,
                             status="webhook_exc", reason=str(we))

            await asyncio.sleep(float(os.getenv("send_delay_seconds","1")))

    total_latency = int((time.time() - start_run) * 1000)
    log_json(run_id=run_id, module="send", event="send_cycle_complete", latency_ms=total_latency)



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/status.py

class Status:
    PENDING = "pending"
    DUPLICATE = "duplicate"
    REVIEW = "review"
    APPROVED = "approved"
    QUEUED = "queued"
    SENDING = "sending"
    SENT = "sent"
    FAILED = "failed"
    REJECTED = "rejected"

########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/telegram_collector.py
########################################################################################################################

import asyncio, os
from datetime import datetime
from telethon import TelegramClient
from .core.db import get_conn
from .utils import clean_text, excerpt, text_hash
from .logger import log_json
from .status import Status
from .config import Config

API_ID = int(os.getenv("API_ID", os.getenv("api_id", "0")))
API_HASH = os.getenv("API_HASH", os.getenv("api_hash", ""))
SESSION_PATH = os.getenv("NEWS_TELETHON_SESSION_PATH", "/root/ASASANATBOT/data/news_session")

SRC = os.getenv("source_channels", "")
SRC1 = os.getenv("source_channels1", "")
SOURCE_CHANNELS = [s.strip() for s in (SRC + "," + SRC1).split(",") if s.strip()]
ALL_CHANNELS = SOURCE_CHANNELS
LIMIT_PER_CHANNEL = int(os.getenv("rss_limit_per_source", "10"))

def _msg_text_or_caption(msg):
    txt = getattr(msg, "message", None) or getattr(msg, "text", None) or getattr(msg, "caption", None)
    return (txt or "").strip()

def _build_title_and_content(raw_text):
    content = clean_text(raw_text)
    first_line = content.split("\n")[0].strip() if content else ""
    title = first_line[:80] if first_line else (excerpt(content, 80) if content else "بدون عنوان")
    return title, content

async def collect_from_channels(run_id: str, limit: int = None):
    limit = limit or LIMIT_PER_CHANNEL
    inserted_total = 0
    if not API_ID or not API_HASH:
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tg_collector", error="no_api_creds")
        return 0

    os.makedirs(Config.MEDIA_DIR, exist_ok=True)

    async with TelegramClient(SESSION_PATH, API_ID, API_HASH) as client:
        if not await client.is_user_authorized():
            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tg_collector", error="telethon_not_authorized")
            return 0

        for ch in ALL_CHANNELS:
            inserted = 0
            try:
                seen_groups = set()
                async for msg in client.iter_messages(ch, limit=limit):
                    if getattr(msg, "action", None):
                        continue
                    gid = getattr(msg, "grouped_id", None)
                    if gid:
                        if gid in seen_groups:
                            continue
                        seen_groups.add(gid)

                    raw_text = _msg_text_or_caption(msg)
                    if not raw_text and not getattr(msg, "media", None):
                        continue

                    title, content = _build_title_and_content(raw_text or "")
                    ex = excerpt(content, 240)
                    url = f"https://t.me/{ch}/{msg.id}"
                    source = f"telegram:{ch}"
                    c_hash = text_hash(title + ex)
                    created_at = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

                    media_file = None
                    media_type = None
                    if Config.DOWNLOAD_MEDIA and getattr(msg, "media", None):
                        try:
                            media_type = type(msg.media).__name__
                            media_file = await client.download_media(
                                msg, file=os.path.join(Config.MEDIA_DIR, f"{ch}_{msg.id}")
                            )
                        except Exception as me:
                            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tg_collector", channel=ch, item_id=getattr(msg,'id',None), media_error=str(me))

                    with get_conn() as conn:
                        exists = conn.execute("SELECT 1 FROM news_items WHERE content_hash=? LIMIT 1", (c_hash,)).fetchone()
                        if not exists:
                            conn.execute("""
                                INSERT INTO news_items
                                (title, content, excerpt, url, source, category, score, status, created_at, content_hash, media_type, media_file)
                                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                            """, (title, content, ex, url, source, None, 0.0, Status.PENDING, created_at, c_hash, media_type, media_file))
                            inserted += 1

                inserted_total += inserted
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tg_collector", channel=ch, inserted=inserted)
            except Exception as e:
                log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tg_collector", channel=ch, error=str(e))
    return inserted_total

def collect_from_channels_sync(run_id: str, limit: int = None):
    return asyncio.run(collect_from_channels(run_id, limit=limit))



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/tg_helpers.py
########################################################################################################################

import re

_persian_nums = {ord(a): ord(b) for a,b in zip('۰۱۲۳۴۵۶۷۸۹','0123456789')}
_arabic_nums   = {ord(a): ord(b) for a,b in zip('٠١٢٣٤٥٦٧٨٩','0123456789')}

def normalize_numbers(s: str) -> str:
    if not s:
        return s
    s = s.translate(_persian_nums)
    s = s.translate(_arabic_nums)
    s = re.sub(r'[,\u066C\u066B\u2009\s]', '', s)
    return s

def extract_first_number(s: str):
    s2 = normalize_numbers(s or "")
    m = re.search(r'(-?\d+(\.\d+)?)', s2)
    return float(m.group(1)) if m else None

def percent_change(old, new):
    try:
        if old is None or new is None or old == 0:
            return None
        return (new - old) / old
    except Exception:
        return None



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/tgju_rss_collector.py
########################################################################################################################

import requests, re, feedparser
from datetime import datetime
from .core.db import get_conn
from .logger import log_json
from .status import Status
from .utils import clean_text, excerpt
from .tg_helpers import normalize_numbers

TGJU_RSS = "https://www.tgju.org/feed"
HEADERS = {
    "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) Chrome/120.0",
    "Accept": "application/rss+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8"
}

def _clean_rss_text(text: str) -> str:
    return (re.split(r'</rss>', text, 1)[0] + "</rss>") if "</rss>" in text else text

def collect_tgju_rss(run_id: str):
    inserted = 0
    try:
        resp = requests.get(TGJU_RSS, headers=HEADERS, timeout=10)
        cleaned = _clean_rss_text(resp.text)
        d = feedparser.parse(cleaned)

        for entry in d.entries[:20]:
            title = clean_text(entry.get('title','').strip())
            summary = clean_text((entry.get('summary','') or entry.get('description','')).strip())
            url = entry.get('link','')
            source = "https://www.tgju.org/news"
            ex = excerpt(summary, 240)
            content_hash = f"tgju:{normalize_numbers(title+summary)[:64]}"
            now = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

            with get_conn() as conn:
                exists = conn.execute("SELECT 1 FROM news_items WHERE content_hash=? LIMIT 1", (content_hash,)).fetchone()
                if not exists:
                    conn.execute("""
                        INSERT INTO news_items (title, content, excerpt, url, source, category, score, status, created_at, content_hash)
                        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                    """, (title, summary, ex, url, source, "economy", 0.0, Status.PENDING, now, content_hash))
                    inserted += 1

        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tgju_rss", feed=TGJU_RSS, inserted=inserted)
    except Exception as e:
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tgju_rss", feed=TGJU_RSS, error=str(e))
    return inserted

FILE: src/src/news/tgju_scraper.py

# src/news/tgju_scraper.py
import aiohttp, asyncio, re
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from datetime import datetime
from .core.db import get_conn
from .logger import log_json
from .status import Status
from .utils import excerpt
from .tg_helpers import extract_first_number, normalize_numbers

HEADERS = {
    "User-Agent": "AsaSanatBot/1.0 (+https://asatechnet.ir)",
    "Accept": "text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8",
    "Accept-Language": "fa-IR,fa;q=0.9,en-US;q=0.8,en;q=0.7",
    "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
}

KEYWORDS = ("بورس","شاخص","صنعت","دلار","طلا","سکه","انس","یورو","درهم","نقره")

def _is_html(resp: aiohttp.ClientResponse) -> bool:
    ctype = resp.headers.get("Content-Type", "")
    return "text/html" in ctype or "application/xhtml+xml" in ctype

async def fetch_page(session, url: str, timeout: int = 15) -> str:
    async with session.get(url, headers=HEADERS, timeout=timeout) as resp:
        status = resp.status
        text = await resp.text(errors="ignore")
        if status >= 400 or not _is_html(resp):
            raise RuntimeError(f"http_status={status}, content_type={resp.headers.get('Content-Type')}")
        return text

def _extract_rate_lines(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
    lines = []
    scanned = 0
    for txt in soup.stripped_strings:
        scanned += 1
        t = txt.strip()
        if len(t) > 200:
            continue
        if any(k in t for k in KEYWORDS):
            val = extract_first_number(t)
            if val is not None:
                if re.search(r'([^\d]{2,}\s+)?-?\d+(\.\d+)?', normalize_numbers(t)):
                    lines.append((t, val))
    return lines, scanned

async def scrape_rates_page(run_id: str, url: str, status_when_insert: str = Status.APPROVED):
    async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as s:
        try:
            html = await fetch_page(s, url)
            items, scanned = _extract_rate_lines(html)

            now = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
            inserted = 0
            with get_conn() as conn:
                for txt, val in items:
                    title = "نرخ بازار (TGJU)"
                    ex = excerpt(txt, 160)
                    url_ref = url
                    norm = normalize_numbers(txt)
                    content_hash = f"tgju_rate:{norm[:64]}"

                    exists = conn.execute(
                        "SELECT 1 FROM news_items WHERE content_hash=? LIMIT 1",
                        (content_hash,)
                    ).fetchone()
                    if not exists:
                        conn.execute("""
                            INSERT INTO news_items (title, content, excerpt, url, source, category, score, status, created_at, content_hash)
                            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                        """, (
                            title,
                            txt,
                            ex,
                            url_ref,
                            "tgju",
                            "rates",
                            0.9 if status_when_insert == Status.APPROVED else 0.5,
                            status_when_insert,
                            now,
                            content_hash
                        ))
                        inserted += 1

            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tgju_scraper", url=url, scanned=scanned, found=len(items), inserted=inserted)
            return inserted
        except Exception as e:
            log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tgju_scraper", url=url, error=str(e))
            return 0

########################################################################################################################

# src/news/tgju_widget_collector.py
import requests, datetime
from .core.db import get_conn
from .config import Config
from .logger import log_json
from .status import Status
from .utils import text_hash

TGJU_WIDGET_URL = "https://api.tgju.org/v1/widget/tmp"
HEADERS = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) Chrome/120.0"}

def _format_widget_post(indicators):
    today = datetime.date.today().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    lines = [f"📊 گزارش شاخص‌های TGJU ({today})", ""]
    for item in indicators:
        title = item.get("title","")
        p = item.get("p","")
        d = item.get("d","")
        dp = item.get("dp","")
        h = item.get("h","")
        l = item.get("l","")
        t = item.get("t","")
        lines.append(f"▫️ {title}")
        lines.append(f"   مقدار: {p}")
        lines.append(f"   تغییر: {d} ({dp}%)")
        lines.append(f"   بیشترین: {h} | کمترین: {l}")
        if t: lines.append(f"   زمان: {t}")
        lines.append("")
    return "\n".join(lines).strip()

def collect_tgju_widget(run_id: str):
    inserted = 0
    try:
        resp = requests.get(f"{TGJU_WIDGET_URL}?keys={Config.TGJU_WIDGET_ITEMS}", headers=HEADERS, timeout=10)
        indicators = resp.json()["response"]["indicators"]
        content = _format_widget_post(indicators)
        title = "گزارش روزانه شاخص‌های TGJU"
        ex = content[:240] + ("..." if len(content) > 240 else "")
        url = "https://www.tgju.org"
        source = "tgju_widget"
        c_hash = text_hash("tgju_widget:" + content[:512])
        now = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        with get_conn() as conn:
            exists = conn.execute("SELECT 1 FROM news_items WHERE content_hash=? LIMIT 1", (c_hash,)).fetchone()
            if not exists:
                conn.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO news_items (title, content, excerpt, url, source, category, score, status, created_at, content_hash)
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                """, (title, content, ex, url, source, "market_indices", 0.9, Status.APPROVED, now, c_hash))
                inserted = 1

        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tgju_widget", items=Config.TGJU_WIDGET_ITEMS, inserted=inserted)
    except Exception as e:
        log_json(run_id=run_id, module="tgju_widget", error=str(e))
    return inserted



########################################################################################################################
FILE: src/src/news/utils.py
########################################################################################################################

import hashlib, re
from .tg_helpers import normalize_numbers

def text_hash(text: str) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha256(text.encode("utf-8", errors="ignore")).hexdigest()

def clean_text(text: str) -> str:
    if not text:
        return ""
    txt = re.sub(r'http\S+', '', text)
    txt = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '', txt)
    txt = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', txt)
    return txt.strip()

def excerpt(text: str, length=200) -> str:
    t = (text or "").strip()
    return t[:length] + ("..." if len(t) > length else "")

def normalize_text(s: str) -> str:
    if not s:
        return ""
    s = s.replace('\u200c', ' ')
    s = normalize_numbers(s)
    s = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', s).strip()
    return s.lower()
