#/root/ASASANAT1/src/services/crawler.py
from __future__ import annotations

import asyncio
import random
import re
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, AsyncIterator, List, Optional, Tuple
from zoneinfo import ZoneInfo

from sqlalchemy import text
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
from sqlalchemy.exc import OperationalError, IntegrityError

from telethon import TelegramClient
from telethon.errors import FloodWaitError, RPCError, ChannelPrivateError
from src.utils.date_utils import to_jalali_code, parse_jalali_to_utc # returns 'YYYYMMDD'
from src.bot.utils.reporter import report_log, report_post_status, report_heartbeat

from src.core.config import settings
from src.db.schema import ensure_schema
from src.db.session import async_session
from src.services.serial import atomic_next_serial_async, make_serial_code
from src.services.utils import normalize_channel_key, extract_message_text

import logging
from src.logger_setup import logger
log = logger.getChild("crawler")

# -----------------------------
# Configs
# -----------------------------
CRAWL_DELAY: float = float(getattr(settings, "crawl_delay_seconds", 0.0))
LOG_DELAY: float = float(getattr(settings, "log_delay_seconds", 0.5))
FETCH_LIMIT_DEFAULT: int = int(getattr(settings, "crawl_limit", getattr(settings, "crawler_limit", 100)))
PER_CHANNEL_PAUSE: float = float(getattr(settings, "per_channel_pause_seconds", 0.5))
JITTER_MAX: float = float(getattr(settings, "crawl_jitter_seconds", 0.3))

UTC = ZoneInfo("UTC")

PENDING_STATUS = "pending"
SENT_FALSE = 0
TRY_COUNT_ZERO = 0


# -----------------------------
# Helpers
# -----------------------------
# add just below existing imports
import hashlib

def _clean_text_for_hash(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").replace("\u200c", " ").strip()
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s)
    return s.lower()

def _content_hash(s: str) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha1(s.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

def _parse_from_date(s: Optional[str]) -> Optional[datetime]:
    if not s:
        return None
    # ISO first
    try:
        dt = datetime.fromisoformat(s)
        return dt if dt.tzinfo else dt.replace(tzinfo=UTC)
    except Exception:
        pass
    # Jalali YYYY/MM/DD fallback (parse to UTC)
    try:
        if re.fullmatch(r"\d{4}/\d{2}/\d{2}", s.strip()):
            try:
                # prefer explicit helper if available
                from src.utils.date_utils import parse_jalali_to_utc  # type: ignore
                dt = parse_jalali_to_utc(s)  # expected tz-aware UTC
                if isinstance(dt, datetime):
                    return dt if dt.tzinfo else dt.replace(tzinfo=UTC)
            except Exception:
                # alternate helper name
                from src.utils.date_utils import parse_jalali_datetime  # type: ignore
                dt = parse_jalali_datetime(s)
                return dt if dt.tzinfo else dt.replace(tzinfo=UTC)
    except Exception:
        log.warning("from-date نامعتبر %s (نادیده گرفته شد)", s)
    return None


async def _get_dialect_name(db: AsyncSession) -> str:
    try:
        bind = db.get_bind()
        name = getattr(getattr(bind, "dialect", None), "name", None)
        return name or "sqlite"
    except Exception:
        return "sqlite"


async def _iter_messages(
    client: TelegramClient,
    ch_key: str,
    tail_mode: bool,
    fetch_limit: int,
    min_id: int,
) -> AsyncIterator[Any]:
    if tail_mode:
        # fetch newest->oldest then reverse for stable serial ordering
        msgs: List[Any] = []
        async for msg in client.iter_messages(ch_key, reverse=False, limit=fetch_limit):
            msgs.append(msg)
        for msg in reversed(msgs):
            yield msg
    else:
        iterator = client.iter_messages(ch_key, reverse=True, limit=fetch_limit, min_id=min_id)
        if hasattr(iterator, "__aiter__"):
            async for msg in iterator:
                yield msg
        else:
            batch = await asyncio.to_thread(lambda: list(iterator))  # type: ignore
            for msg in batch:
                yield msg


# -----------------------------
# Insert stubs (idempotent)
# -----------------------------
async def _insert_post_stub_sqlite(
    db: AsyncSession, ch_key: str, msg_id: int, raw_text: str, jalali_date: str
) -> Optional[int]:
    """
    درج پست با شمارنده اتمیک per-channel (SQLite v2) یا day-scoped (v1 fallback)
      - یکتا روی (source_channel, source_id) درج دوباره را بی‌اثر می‌کند.
      - در رقابت، ممکن است شکاف سریال رخ دهد (قابل قبول) اما دوبل نداریم.
    """
    next_serial = await atomic_next_serial_async(db, ch_key, jalali_date)
    serial_code = make_serial_code(jalali_date, ch_key, next_serial)

    await db.execute(
        text(
            """
            INSERT OR IGNORE INTO posts (
                source_channel,
                source_id,
                channel_key,
                raw_text,
                serial,
                serial_code,
                jalali_date,
                status,
                sent,
                try_count
            ) VALUES (
                :ch,
                :sid,
                :ck,
                :raw,
                :serial,
                :scode,
                :jd,
                :st,
                :se,
                :tc
            )
            """
        ),
        {
            "ch": ch_key,
            "sid": msg_id,
            "ck": ch_key,
            "raw": raw_text,
            "serial": next_serial,
            "scode": serial_code,
            "jd": jalali_date,
            "st": PENDING_STATUS,
            "se": SENT_FALSE,
            "tc": TRY_COUNT_ZERO,
        },
    )

    res = await db.execute(text("SELECT changes()"))
    changed = int(res.scalar_one() or 0)
    if changed == 0:
        return None

    row = await db.execute(
        text(
            """
            SELECT id FROM posts
            WHERE source_channel = :ch AND source_id = :sid
            LIMIT 1
            """
        ),
        {"ch": ch_key, "sid": msg_id},
    )
    val = row.scalar_one_or_none()
    return int(val) if val is not None else None


async def _insert_post_stub_pg(
    db: AsyncSession, ch_key: str, msg_id: int, raw_text: str, jalali_date: str
) -> Optional[int]:
    next_serial = await atomic_next_serial_async(db, ch_key, jalali_date)
    serial_code = make_serial_code(jalali_date, ch_key, next_serial)

    res = await db.execute(
        text(
            """
            INSERT INTO posts
                (source_channel, source_id, channel_key, raw_text, serial, serial_code, jalali_date, status, sent, try_count)
            VALUES
                (:ch, :sid, :ck, :raw, :serial, :scode, :jd, :st::poststatus, :se, :tc)
            ON CONFLICT (source_channel, source_id) DO NOTHING
            RETURNING id
            """
        ),
        {
            "ch": ch_key,
            "sid": msg_id,
            "ck": ch_key,
            "raw": raw_text,
            "serial": next_serial,
            "scode": serial_code,
            "jd": jalali_date,
            "st": PENDING_STATUS,
            "se": SENT_FALSE,
            "tc": TRY_COUNT_ZERO,
        },
    )
    row = res.first() if hasattr(res, "first") else None
    if row:
        try:
            return int(row[0])
        except Exception:
            return None
    return None


# -----------------------------
# Upsert flow
# -----------------------------
async def _upsert_with_retry(
    db: AsyncSession, ch_key: str, msg_id: int, raw_text: str, msg_dt: datetime, max_retries: int = 3
) -> Tuple[Optional[int], Optional[str]]:
    attempt = 0
    last_exc: Optional[Exception] = None
    while attempt <= max_retries:
        try:
            return await _upsert_post_and_assign_serial(db, ch_key, msg_id, raw_text, msg_dt)
        except (OperationalError, IntegrityError) as e:
            msg = str(e).lower()
            if ("locked" in msg) or ("busy" in msg) or ("timeout" in msg):
                wait = min(1.5 * (2 ** attempt), 5.0) + random.uniform(0, 0.25)
                await asyncio.sleep(wait)
                attempt += 1
                last_exc = e
                continue
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            last_exc = e
            break
    if last_exc:
        raise last_exc
    return None, None


async def _upsert_post_and_assign_serial(
    db: AsyncSession, ch_key: str, msg_id: int, raw_text: str, msg_dt: datetime
) -> Tuple[Optional[int], Optional[str]]:
    if msg_dt.tzinfo is None:
        msg_dt = msg_dt.replace(tzinfo=UTC)

    jalali_date = to_jalali_code(msg_dt)
    ch_key = normalize_channel_key(ch_key)
    dialect = await _get_dialect_name(db)

    # --- soft dedup check ---
    raw_text_clean = _clean_text_for_hash(raw_text or "")
    h_new = _content_hash(raw_text_clean) if raw_text_clean else None

    if h_new:
        recent_rows = await db.execute(
            text("""
                SELECT id, raw_text, processed_text
                FROM posts
                WHERE (raw_text IS NOT NULL OR processed_text IS NOT NULL)
                ORDER BY created_at DESC
                LIMIT 500
            """)
        )
        for rid, r_raw, r_proc in recent_rows.fetchall():
            base = (r_proc or r_raw or "")
            if not base:
                continue
            base_clean = _clean_text_for_hash(base)
            if base_clean and _content_hash(base_clean) == h_new:
                # duplicate content detected (soft check) -> skip insert
                return None, None
    # --- end dedup ---

    if dialect == "sqlite":
        post_id = await _insert_post_stub_sqlite(db, ch_key, msg_id, raw_text, jalali_date)
        if post_id is None:
            return None, None
    else:
        post_id = await _insert_post_stub_pg(db, ch_key, msg_id, raw_text, jalali_date)
        if post_id is None:
            return None, None

    res = await db.execute(
        text("SELECT serial FROM posts WHERE id = :pid"),
        {"pid": post_id},
    )
    serial_value = res.scalar_one_or_none()

    serial_code = make_serial_code(jalali_date, ch_key, int(serial_value) if serial_value else 0)
    await db.execute(
        text(
            """
            UPDATE posts
            SET serial_code = :sc,
                status = COALESCE(status, :st),
                sent = COALESCE(sent, :se),
                try_count = COALESCE(try_count, :tc)
            WHERE id = :pid
            """
        ),
        {
            "sc": serial_code,
            "pid": post_id,
            "st": PENDING_STATUS,
            "se": SENT_FALSE,
            "tc": TRY_COUNT_ZERO,
        },
    )

    return (int(serial_value) if serial_value is not None else None), jalali_date

def _parse_from_date_arg(v: str) -> Optional[datetime]:
    """
    ورودی تاریخ را به UTC-aware datetime تبدیل می‌کند.
    پشتیبانی:
      - Jalali: YYYY/MM/DD یا YYYY-MM-DD
      - ISO: YYYY-MM-DD[THH:MM[:SS][+ZZ:ZZ]]
    """
    s = (v or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return None

    # Jalali با / یا -
    if re.fullmatch(r"\d{4}[/-]\d{2}[/-]\d{2}", s):
        try:
            dt = parse_jalali_to_utc(s)  # انتظار: tz-aware UTC
            if isinstance(dt, datetime):
                return dt if dt.tzinfo else dt.replace(tzinfo=UTC)
        except Exception as e:
            log.warning("Invalid Jalali date %s: %s", s, e)
            return None

    # سایر حالت‌ها را به پارسر امن موجود بسپار
    try:
        dt = _parse_from_date(s)
        if dt and dt.tzinfo is None:
            dt = dt.replace(tzinfo=UTC)
        return dt
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("Invalid date format %s: %s", s, e)
        return None

# -----------------------------
# Main crawler (summary mode)
# -----------------------------
async def crawl_summary(
    limit: Optional[int] = None,
    dry_run: bool = False,
    from_date: Optional[str] = None,
    jalali_year: Optional[str] = None,
    tail: bool = False,
) -> None:
    log.info("Starting crawler (dry_run=%s, tail=%s, year=%s)", bool(dry_run), bool(tail), jalali_year)
    report_heartbeat("crawler")
    await ensure_schema()

    raw_channels: List[str] = list(getattr(settings, "source_channels", []) or [])
    if not raw_channels:
        log.warning("No source_channels configured in settings")
        report_log("crawler", "No source_channels configured", level="WARNING")
        return

    source_channels = [normalize_channel_key(ch) for ch in raw_channels if ch and str(ch).strip()]
    fetch_limit = int(limit or FETCH_LIMIT_DEFAULT)
    from_date_utc = _parse_from_date_arg(from_date) if from_date else None

    data_dir = Path(getattr(settings, "data_dir", "data"))
    data_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    session_path = str(data_dir / "asa_crawler_summary")

    client = TelegramClient(
        session_path,
        getattr(settings, "api_id", None),
        getattr(settings, "api_hash", None),
    )

    tail_mode = bool(tail or (limit is not None and not from_date and not jalali_year))

    try:
        phone = getattr(settings, "phone", None)
        bot_token = getattr(settings, "bot_token", None)
        if phone:
            await client.start(phone=phone)
            log.info("Telegram client started via phone auth")
        elif bot_token:
            await client.start(bot_token=bot_token)
            log.info("Telegram client started via bot token")
        else:
            await client.start()
            log.info("Telegram client started interactively")
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception("Failed to start Telegram client")
        report_log("crawler", f"Failed to start Telegram client: {e}", level="ERROR")
        return

    overall_fetched = 0
    overall_new = 0
    start_time = datetime.now(tz=UTC)
    overall_attempted = 0
    overall_fail = 0


    async def get_max_id_for_channel(db_session, channel_key: str) -> Optional[int]:
        """آخرین message_id ذخیره‌شده برای کانال را از DB می‌گیرد."""
        result = await db_session.execute(
            text("SELECT MAX(source_id) FROM posts WHERE source_channel = :ch"),
            {"ch": channel_key}
        )
        return result.scalar()

    try:
        async with async_session() as db:
            for ch_key in source_channels:
                min_id = await get_max_id_for_channel(db, ch_key)
                fetched = attempted = new_count = fail_count = 0
                last_jalali = None
                channel_private = False
                channel_start = datetime.now(tz=UTC)

                try:
                    async for msg in _iter_messages(client, ch_key, tail_mode, fetch_limit, min_id):
                        msg_id = int(getattr(msg, "id", 0))
                        msg_date: datetime = getattr(msg, "date", datetime.now(tz=UTC))
                        if msg_date.tzinfo is None:
                            msg_date = msg_date.replace(tzinfo=UTC)

                        jalali_code = to_jalali_code(msg_date)

                        if not tail_mode and min_id and msg_id <= min_id:
                            continue
                        if from_date_utc and msg_date < from_date_utc:
                            continue
                        if jalali_year and jalali_code[:4] != str(jalali_year):
                            continue

                        fetched += 1

                        if dry_run:
                            log.info("dry-run  ch=%s sid=%s date_utc=%s jalali=%s",
                                     ch_key, msg_id, msg_date.isoformat(), jalali_code)
                            report_log("crawler",
                                       f"Dry-run fetch {ch_key} sid={msg_id} jalali={jalali_code}")
                            if LOG_DELAY:
                                await asyncio.sleep(LOG_DELAY + random.uniform(0, JITTER_MAX))
                            continue

                        raw_text = extract_message_text(msg) or ""
                        if raw_text:
                            tags = re.findall(r"#\w+", raw_text)
                            if tags:
                                log.info("Tags found %s", tags)

                        log.info("Fetch  ch=%s sid=%s date_utc=%s jalali=%s",
                                 ch_key, msg_id, msg_date.isoformat(), jalali_code)

                        attempted += 1
                        try:
                            serial_value, jalali_date = await _upsert_with_retry(
                                db, ch_key, msg_id, raw_text, msg_date
                            )

                            if serial_value is not None:
                                try:
                                    await db.commit()
                                except Exception as e:
                                    await db.rollback()
                                    fail_count += 1
                                    report_log("crawler", f"DB commit failed: {e}", level="ERROR")
                                    continue

                                new_count += 1
                                last_jalali = jalali_date
                                report_post_status(ch_key, msg_id, "pending")
                                report_log("crawler", f"Pending stored ch={ch_key} sid={msg_id} serial={serial_value} jalali={jalali_date}")
                                log.info("NEW  ch=%s sid=%s serial=%s jalali=%s",
                                         ch_key, msg_id, serial_value, jalali_date)
                                report_log("crawler",
                                           f"New post {ch_key} sid={msg_id} serial={serial_value} jalali={jalali_date}")
                            else:
                                await db.rollback()
                                log.info("DUP  ch=%s sid=%s jalali=%s", ch_key, msg_id, jalali_code)
                                report_log("crawler",
                                           f"DUP post {ch_key} sid={msg_id} jalali={jalali_code}")

                            if LOG_DELAY:
                                await asyncio.sleep(LOG_DELAY + random.uniform(0, JITTER_MAX))
                            if CRAWL_DELAY:
                                await asyncio.sleep(CRAWL_DELAY + random.uniform(0, JITTER_MAX))

                        except ChannelPrivateError:
                            log.warning("Channel %s is private or inaccessible", ch_key)
                            report_log("crawler", f"Channel {ch_key} private", level="WARNING")
                            channel_private = True
                            break
                        except FloodWaitError as fw:
                            report_log("crawler", f"FloodWaitError: {fw}", level="WARNING")
                            wait_s = int(getattr(fw, "seconds", 5)) + 1 + random.uniform(0, 1.0)
                            await asyncio.sleep(wait_s)
                        except RPCError as e:
                            await db.rollback()
                            fail_count += 1
                            report_log("crawler", f"RPCError: {e}", level="ERROR")
                        except Exception as e:
                            try:
                                await db.rollback()
                            except Exception:
                                pass
                            fail_count += 1
                            report_log("crawler", f"Unexpected error: {e}", level="ERROR")

                finally:
                    elapsed = (datetime.now(tz=UTC) - channel_start).total_seconds()
                    dup_count = max(attempted - new_count - fail_count, 0)
                    send_rate = (attempted / fetched * 100) if fetched else 0.0
                    success_rate = (new_count / attempted * 100) if attempted else 0.0
                    fail_rate = (fail_count / attempted * 100) if attempted else 0.0

                    log.info(
                        "Channel summary %s  fetched=%s attempted=%s new=%s dup=%s failed=%s send=%.1f%% success=%.1f%% fail=%.1f%% jalali=%s elapsed=%.2fs",
                        ch_key,
                        fetched,
                        attempted,
                        new_count,
                        dup_count,
                        fail_count,
                        send_rate,
                        success_rate,
                        fail_rate,
                        last_jalali or "",
                        elapsed,
                    )
                    report_log(
                        "crawler",
                        f"Channel {ch_key} summary fetched={fetched} new={new_count} dup={dup_count} failed={fail_count}",
                    )

                    overall_fetched += fetched
                    overall_new += new_count
                    overall_attempted += attempted
                    overall_fail += fail_count


                    if not channel_private:
                        await asyncio.sleep(PER_CHANNEL_PAUSE + random.uniform(0, JITTER_MAX))

    finally:
        try:
            await client.disconnect()
        except Exception:
            pass

        elapsed_total = (datetime.now(tz=UTC) - start_time).total_seconds()
        dup_total = max(overall_attempted - overall_new - overall_fail, 0)
        send_rate_total = (overall_attempted / overall_fetched * 100) if overall_fetched else 0.0
        success_rate_total = (overall_new / overall_attempted * 100) if overall_attempted else 0.0
        fail_rate_total = (overall_fail / overall_attempted * 100) if overall_attempted else 0.0


        log.info(
            "Crawler finished  channels=%s total_fetched=%s total_new=%s total_dup=%s "
            "send=%.1f%% success=%.1f%% fail=%.1f%% elapsed=%.2fs",
            len(source_channels),
            overall_fetched,
            overall_new,
            dup_total,
            send_rate_total,
            success_rate_total,
            fail_rate_total,
            elapsed_total,
        )

        report_log(
            "crawler",
            f"Finished channels={len(source_channels)} "
            f"total_fetched={overall_fetched} total_new={overall_new} total_dup={dup_total} "
            f"send={send_rate_total:.1f}% success={success_rate_total:.1f}% fail={fail_rate_total:.1f}% "
            f"elapsed={elapsed_total:.2f}s",
        )


# -----------------------------
# CLI
# -----------------------------
def _parse_args():
    import argparse

    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Telegram crawler summary")
    p.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="Max messages per channel to fetch in one batch")
    p.add_argument("--dry-run", action="store_true", help="Do not write to DB, only log actions")
    p.add_argument(
        "--from-date", type=str, help="ISO format YYYY-MM-DD, full ISO (UTC), or Jalali YYYY/MM/DD (local)"
    )
    p.add_argument("--jalali-year", type=str, help="Filter messages by Jalali year, e.g., 1404")
    p.add_argument(
        "--tail",
        action="store_true",
        help="Fetch last N messages per channel (oldest->newest order for stable serials)",
    )
    return p.parse_args()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    args = _parse_args()
    asyncio.run(
        crawl_summary(
            limit=args.limit,
            dry_run=args.dry_run,
            from_date=args.from_date,
            jalali_year=args.jalali_year,
            tail=args.tail,
        )
    )

# src/services/message_builder.py
import re
from src.core.constants import FIXED_HEADER_TEMPLATE, SIGNATURE

# --- ثابت‌ها ---
PERSIAN_DIGITS = str.maketrans("0123456789", "۰۱۲۳۴۵۶۷۸۹")
SEPARATOR = "〰️〰️〰️〰️〰️"


# --- توابع کمکی ---
def _to_persian_digits(text: str) -> str:
    return (text or "").translate(PERSIAN_DIGITS)


def _normalize_date_ymd(date_str: str) -> str:
    """تاریخ را از yyyymmdd به yyyy/mm/dd تبدیل می‌کند."""
    s = re.sub(r"\D", "", date_str or "")
    if len(s) == 8:
        return f"{s[0:4]}/{s[4:6]}/{s[6:8]}"
    return date_str or ""

# --- تابع اصلی ---
def build_message(
    title: str,
    serial_code: str,
    fa_date: str,
    body: str,
    include_signature: bool = True,
    include_separator: bool = True
) -> str:
    """پیام نهایی تلگرام را بر اساس ورودی‌ها می‌سازد."""
    fa_date_disp = _to_persian_digits(_normalize_date_ymd(fa_date))

    header = FIXED_HEADER_TEMPLATE.format(
        serial_code=serial_code,
        fa_date=fa_date_disp
    )
    if include_separator:
        header += f"\n{SEPARATOR}"

    parts = [header]
    if body:
        parts.append(body)


    if include_signature and SIGNATURE.strip():
        parts.append(SIGNATURE.strip())

    return "\n\n".join(p.strip() for p in parts if p and p.strip())

# src/services/repository.py

from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional, Set
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from itertools import zip_longest
import logging

from sqlalchemy import asc, func, case
from sqlalchemy.exc import IntegrityError

from src.services.utils import parse_json_list as _parse_json_list
from src.db.session import SessionLocal
from src.db.models import Post, Favorite

from src import logger_setup

log = logging.getLogger("repository")


def _post_to_dict(p: Post) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Convert a Post ORM object into a serializable dictionary."""
    return {
        "id": p.id,
        "serial_code": p.serial_code,
        "source_channel": p.source_channel,
        "raw_text": p.raw_text or "",
        "title": p.title,
        "location": p.location,
        "category": p.category,
        "tags": _parse_json_list(p.tags),
        "phone": p.phone,
        "links": _parse_json_list(p.links),
        "processed_text": p.processed_text or "",
        "serial": p.serial,
        "jalali_date": p.jalali_date,
        "status": p.status.value if hasattr(p.status, "value") else p.status,
        "sent": p.sent,
        "created_at": p.created_at,
        "sent_at": p.sent_at,
    }


class Repository:
    def __init__(self, db):
        self.db = db

    def fetch_recent_posts(self, channel: str, limit: int = 10) -> List[Post]:
        """Return the last `limit` posts for a channel, oldest-to-newest."""
        subq = (
            self.db.query(Post)
            .filter(Post.source_channel == channel)
            .order_by(Post.created_at.desc())
            .limit(limit)
            .subquery()
        )
        return (
            self.db.query(Post)
            .select_entity_from(subq)
            .order_by(asc(subq.c.created_at))
            .all()
        )


# ------------------- Fetch unsent posts -------------------

def fetch_unsent_full_sorted_by_serial(limit: int = 50) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Fair distribution of unsent posts per channel, then fill globally."""
    if not limit or limit <= 0:
        limit = 50

    with SessionLocal() as session:
        cutoff = datetime.now(timezone.utc) - timedelta(minutes=30)

        def _apply_base_filter(q):
            return (
                q.filter(Post.sent == False)
                 .filter((Post.status == None) | (Post.status != "sent"))
                 .filter(
                     (Post.status != "sending")
                     | (Post.sending_at == None)
                     | (Post.sending_at < cutoff)
                 )
            )

        # 1. Count unsent per channel
        counts = (
            session.query(Post.source_channel, func.count().label("cnt"))
        )
        counts = _apply_base_filter(counts).group_by(Post.source_channel).all()
        channels = [(row[0], int(row[1])) for row in counts]

        if not channels:
            log.info("[repository] fetched unsent posts: count=0 sources=[]")
            return []

        total_unsent = sum(cnt for _, cnt in channels)
        if total_unsent == 0:
            log.info("[repository] fetched unsent posts: count=0 sources=[]")
            return []

        # 2. Compute per-channel quotas
        quotas: Dict[str, int] = {}
        num_ch = len(channels)

        if limit < num_ch:
            for i, (ch, _) in enumerate(sorted(channels, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)):
                quotas[ch] = 1 if i < limit else 0
        else:
            for ch, cnt in channels:
                quotas[ch] = max(1, round(limit * cnt / total_unsent))
            total_q = sum(quotas.values())

            if total_q > limit:
                for ch, _ in sorted(quotas.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):
                    while quotas[ch] > 1 and total_q > limit:
                        quotas[ch] -= 1
                        total_q -= 1
                        if total_q <= limit:
                            break
            elif total_q < limit:
                for ch, _ in sorted(channels, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):
                    quotas[ch] += 1
                    total_q += 1
                    if total_q >= limit:
                        break

        # 3. Fetch per-channel slices
        per_channel_rows: List[List[Post]] = []
        order_clause = [
            case((Post.serial == None, 1), else_=0).asc(),
            asc(Post.serial),
            asc(Post.created_at),
        ]

        for ch, _ in channels:
            q = quotas.get(ch, 0)
            if q <= 0:
                per_channel_rows.append([])
                continue
            rows_q = session.query(Post).filter(Post.source_channel == ch)
            rows = _apply_base_filter(rows_q).order_by(*order_clause).limit(q).all()
            per_channel_rows.append(rows)

        # 4. Interleave round-robin
        interleaved: List[Post] = []
        seen_ids: Set[int] = set()

        for group in zip_longest(*per_channel_rows):
            for post in group:
                if post and post.id not in seen_ids:
                    interleaved.append(post)
                    seen_ids.add(post.id)
                    if len(interleaved) >= limit:
                        break
            if len(interleaved) >= limit:
                break

        # 5. Fill remaining slots globally
        if len(interleaved) < limit:
            needed = limit - len(interleaved)
            q = session.query(Post)
            q = _apply_base_filter(q).order_by(*order_clause)
            if seen_ids:
                q = q.filter(~Post.id.in_(seen_ids))
            extras = q.limit(needed * 2).all()
            for post in extras:
                if post.id not in seen_ids:
                    interleaved.append(post)
                    seen_ids.add(post.id)
                    if len(interleaved) >= limit:
                        break

        sources = list({p.source_channel for p in interleaved})
        log.info("[repository] fetched unsent posts: count=%d sources=%s", len(interleaved), sources)
        return [_post_to_dict(p) for p in interleaved]


def fetch_unsent_ads(limit: int = 30) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Simple fetch of oldest unsent posts (no fairness)."""
    if not limit or limit <= 0:
        limit = 30
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        rows = (
            session.query(Post)
            .filter(Post.sent == False)
            .order_by(asc(Post.created_at))
            .limit(limit)
            .all()
        )
        sources = list({p.source_channel for p in rows})
        log.info(f"[repository] fetched unsent ads: count={len(rows)} sources={sources}")
        return [
            {"serial_code": p.serial_code, "processed_text": p.processed_text, "source_channel": p.source_channel}
            for p in rows
        ]

# ------------------- Marking status -------------------
def mark_sending_by_id(post_id: int, claim_token: Optional[str] = None) -> None:
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        try:
            post = session.query(Post).filter(Post.id == post_id).first()
            if not post:
                log.warning("[repository] no post found for id=%d", post_id)
            elif post.sent:
                log.info("[repository] post already sent, cannot mark sending: id=%d", post_id)
            else:
                post.status = "sending"
                if claim_token:
                    post.claim_token = claim_token
                session.commit()
                log.info(
                    "[repository] marked sending: id=%d, serial=%s, channel=%s, claim_token=%s",
                    post_id, post.serial_code, post.source_channel, claim_token
                )
        except Exception:
            session.rollback()
            log.exception("[repository] error in mark_sending_by_id")
            raise


def mark_sent_by_id(post_id: int, sent_at: Optional[datetime] = None) -> None:
    sent_time = sent_at or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        try:
            post = session.query(Post).filter(Post.id == post_id).first()
            if not post:
                log.warning("[repository] no post found for id=%d", post_id)
            elif post.sent:
                log.info("[repository] post already marked as sent: id=%d", post_id)
            else:
                post.sent = True
                post.status = "sent"
                post.sent_at = sent_time
                session.commit()
                log.info(
                    "[repository] marked sent: id=%d, serial=%s, channel=%s, sent_at=%s",
                    post_id, post.serial_code, post.source_channel, sent_time
                )
        except Exception:
            session.rollback()
            log.exception("[repository] error in mark_sent_by_id")
            raise


def mark_failed_by_id(post_id: int, reason: str = "") -> None:
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        try:
            post = session.query(Post).filter(Post.id == post_id).first()
            if not post:
                log.warning("[repository] no post found for id=%d", post_id)
            elif post.sent:
                log.info("[repository] post already sent, cannot mark failed: id=%d", post_id)
            else:
                post.status = "failed"
                post.fail_reason = reason
                session.commit()
                log.info(
                    "[repository] marked failed: id=%d, serial=%s, channel=%s, reason=%s",
                    post_id, post.serial_code, post.source_channel, reason
                )
        except Exception:
            session.rollback()
            log.exception("[repository] error in mark_failed_by_id")
            raise


def mark_sent(serial_code: str, source_channel: str, sent_at: Optional[datetime] = None) -> None:
    sent_time = sent_at or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        try:
            post = (
                session.query(Post)
                .filter(Post.serial_code == serial_code, Post.source_channel == source_channel)
                .first()
            )
            if not post:
                log.warning("[repository] no post found for serial=%s, channel=%s",
                            serial_code, source_channel)
            elif post.sent:
                log.info("[repository] post already marked as sent: serial=%s, channel=%s",
                         serial_code, source_channel)
            else:
                post.sent = True
                post.status = "sent"
                post.sent_at = sent_time
                session.commit()
                log.info(
                    "[repository] marked sent: id=%d, serial=%s, channel=%s, sent_at=%s",
                    post.id, serial_code, source_channel, sent_time
                )
        except Exception:
            session.rollback()
            log.exception("[repository] error in mark_sent")
            raise

# ------------------- Stats -------------------

def get_channel_counts() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Return per-channel counts of sent vs. unsent posts."""
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        rows = (
            session.query(
                Post.source_channel.label("channel"),
                func.sum(case((Post.sent == False, 1), else_=0)).label("unsent"),
                func.sum(case((Post.sent == True, 1), else_=0)).label("sent"),
            )
            .group_by(Post.source_channel)
            .all()
        )
        return [
            {"source_channel": r.channel, "unsent": int(r.unsent or 0), "sent": int(r.sent or 0)}
            for r in rows
        ]


# ------------------- Favorites -------------------

def is_favorite(user_id: int, post_id: int) -> bool:
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        q = session.query(Favorite.id).filter(Favorite.user_id == user_id, Favorite.post_id == post_id)
        return session.query(q.exists()).scalar()


def toggle_favorite(user_id: int, post_id: int) -> bool:
    """Toggle favorite: True if added, False if removed."""
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        fav = session.query(Favorite).filter(Favorite.user_id == user_id, Favorite.post_id == post_id).first()
        if fav:
            session.delete(fav)
            session.commit()
            log.info("[fav] removed user=%s post=%s", user_id, post_id)
            return False
        try:
            session.add(Favorite(user_id=user_id, post_id=post_id))
            session.commit()
            log.info("[fav] added user=%s post=%s", user_id, post_id)
            return True
        except IntegrityError:
            session.rollback()
            return False


def list_favorites(user_id: int, limit: int = 10, offset: int = 0) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        rows = (
            session.query(Post)
            .join(Favorite, Favorite.post_id == Post.id)
            .filter(Favorite.user_id == user_id)
            .order_by(Post.created_at.desc())
            .limit(limit)
            .offset(offset)
            .all()
        )
        return [_post_to_dict(p) for p in rows]


def count_favorites(user_id: int) -> int:
    with SessionLocal() as session:
        return session.query(Favorite).filter(Favorite.user_id == user_id).count()

# Rate state
class RateState:
    def __init__(self, hourly_limit: int = 0, daily_limit: int = 0):
        self.hourly_limit = hourly_limit
        self.daily_limit  = daily_limit
        now = datetime.utcnow()
        self._hour_start = now
        self._day_start  = now
        self._h = 0
        self._d = 0

    def _reset_if_needed(self) -> None:
        now = datetime.utcnow()
        if now - self._hour_start >= timedelta(hours=1):
            self._hour_start = now
            self._h = 0
        if now - self._day_start >= timedelta(days=1):
            self._day_start = now
            self._d = 0

    def allow(self) -> bool:
        if self.hourly_limit <= 0 and self.daily_limit <= 0:
            return True
        self._reset_if_needed()
        if self.hourly_limit > 0 and self._h >= self.hourly_limit:
            return False
        if self.daily_limit > 0 and self._d >= self.daily_limit:
            return False
        return True

    def mark(self) -> None:
        if self.hourly_limit > 0:
            self._h += 1
        if self.daily_limit > 0:
            self._d += 1

# Helpers
def normalize_chat_id(val: Optional[str]) -> Optional[Union[int, str]]:
    if not val:
        return None
    v = val.strip().replace("\u200c", "").translate(PERSIAN_DIGITS)
    v = re.sub(r"\s+", "", v)
    if v.startswith("@"):
        return v
    if re.fullmatch(r"-?\d{6,20}", v):
        try:
            return int(v)
        except ValueError:
            return v
    return v

def escape_html(s: str) -> str:
    return _html_escape(s or "", quote=False)

def _format_tags_for_post(tags: List[str]) -> str:
    formatted: List[str] = []
    for tag in tags:
        t = str(tag).strip().replace(" ", "_").replace("\u200c", "")
        if not t:
            continue
        if not t.startswith("#"):
            t = "#" + t
        formatted.append(t)
    seen = set()
    result: List[str] = []
    for t in formatted:
        if t not in seen:
            seen.add(t)
            result.append(t)
    if MAX_TAGS > 0:
        result = result[:MAX_TAGS]
    return " ".join(result)

def _detect_has_media(post: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    for k in ("has_media", "media_only", "is_media_only", "is_media"):
        if str(post.get(k)).lower() in ("1", "true", "yes"):
            return True
        if post.get(k) is True:
            return True
    file_id_keys = (
        "media_file_id", "photo_file_id", "video_file_id", "document_file_id",
        "animation_file_id", "voice_file_id", "audio_file_id"
    )
    if any(post.get(k) for k in file_id_keys):
        return True
    list_keys = ("media_urls", "photos", "videos", "documents", "album", "attachments")
    for k in list_keys:
        v = post.get(k)
        if isinstance(v, (list, tuple)) and len(v) > 0:
            return True
        if isinstance(v, str) and v.strip():
            return True
    return False

def _make_session(retries=2, backoff_factor=0.5, status_forcelist=(500,502,503,504)):
    s = requests.Session()
    retry = Retry(total=retries,
                  read=retries,
                  connect=retries,
                  status=retries,
                  backoff_factor=backoff_factor,
                  status_forcelist=status_forcelist,
                  allowed_methods=frozenset(['GET','POST','PUT','DELETE','HEAD','OPTIONS']))
    adapter = HTTPAdapter(max_retries=retry)
    s.mount("https://", adapter)
    s.mount("http://", adapter)
    return s

def _post_sync(url, json_payload, headers, timeout=15):
    sess = _make_session(retries=2, backoff_factor=0.7)
    resp = sess.post(url, json=json_payload, headers=headers, timeout=timeout, verify=True)
    return resp

def build_counter_from_post(post: Dict[str, Any], as_numeric: bool = False) -> Optional[str]:
    if not isinstance(post, dict):
        return None
    channel_key = (post.get("source_channel") or "").lstrip("@").lower()
    channel_code = CHANNEL_CODES.get(channel_key)
    jalali = post.get("jalali_date")
    serial_val = post.get("serial")
    if channel_code is None or not jalali or serial_val is None:
        return None
    try:
        serial_int = int(serial_val)
    except Exception:
        return None
    counter_val = channel_code * 1000 + serial_int
    return str(counter_val) if as_numeric else f"{jalali}-{counter_val}"

def _maybe_prepend_numeric_counter(core: str, source_channel: str, serial: Optional[int]) -> str:
    if not SHOW_NUMERIC_COUNTER:
        return core
    ch_key = (source_channel or "").strip().lstrip("@").lower()
    code = CHANNEL_CODES.get(ch_key)
    if code is None or serial is None:
        return core
    try:
        counter = int(code) * 1000 + int(serial)
    except Exception:
        return core
    return f"🔢 {counter}\n{core}"

def get_signature_text() -> str:
    return (DEFAULT_SIGNATURE or "").strip()

_access_cache: Dict[Union[int, str], tuple[bool, float]] = {}

async def ensure_access(bot: Bot, chat_id: Union[int, str]) -> bool:
    now = monotonic()
    cached = _access_cache.get(chat_id)
    if cached:
        ok, ts = cached
        if now - ts < ACCESS_CACHE_TTL_S:
            return ok
    try:
        await bot.get_chat(chat_id)
        _access_cache[chat_id] = (True, now)
        return True
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("Access check failed for %r: %s", chat_id, e)
        report_log("sender", f"Access check failed for {chat_id}: {e}", level="ERROR")
        _access_cache[chat_id] = (False, now)
        return False

TAG_LINE_RE = re.compile(r"^(?:\s*#\w+\s*)+$")
HTML_TAG_RE = re.compile(r"<[^>]+>")

def _strip_html(s: str) -> str:
    if not s:
        return ""
    return HTML_TAG_RE.sub("", s)

def _is_low_value_text(text: str) -> bool:
    body = (_strip_html(text) or "").strip()
    if TAG_LINE_RE.fullmatch(body or ""):
        return True
    body_wo_tags = re.sub(r"#\w+", "", body).strip()
    sig = get_signature_text()
    if sig:
        body_wo_tags = body_wo_tags.replace(sig, "").strip()
    body_wo_tags = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", body_wo_tags)
    if len(body_wo_tags) < MIN_PREVIEW_BODY_LENGTH:
        return True
    return False

def build_text_from_db_or_fallback(post: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    raw_text = (post.get("raw_text") or "").strip()
    processed_text = (post.get("processed_text") or "").strip()

    meta = PostMeta(
        serial_code = post.get("serial_code", ""),
        fa_date     = post.get("jalali_date") or to_jalali_code(datetime.now(timezone.utc)),
        title       = post.get("title", ""),
        channel     = (post.get("source_channel") or "").lstrip("@").lower(),
        location    = post.get("location", ""),
        phone       = post.get("phone", ""),
        tags        = (post.get("tags") if isinstance(post.get("tags"), list) else []) or [],
        links       = (post.get("links") if isinstance(post.get("links"), list) else []) or [],
    )
    try:
        setattr(meta, "has_media", _detect_has_media(post))
    except Exception:
        setattr(meta, "has_media", False)

    if not processed_text and (raw_text or getattr(meta, "has_media", False)):
        try:
            processed_text = process_and_build(raw_text, meta).strip()
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception("Fallback build failed for %s: %s", meta.serial_code, e)
            report_log("sender", f"Fallback build failed for {meta.serial_code}: {e}", level="ERROR")
            processed_text = raw_text

    body = processed_text or raw_text

    if not meta.tags:
        try:
            from src.services.text_processing import _extract_tags
            meta.tags = _extract_tags(raw_text or processed_text)
        except Exception:
            meta.tags = []

    try:
        has_media = bool(getattr(meta, "has_media", False))
        b = (body or "").strip()

        if has_media:
            if b:
                if MEDIA_POST_MARKER not in b:
                    b = f"{b}\n\n{MEDIA_POST_MARKER}"
            else:
                b = f"{PLACEHOLDER}\n\n{MEDIA_POST_MARKER}"
        else:
            b = b or PLACEHOLDER

        body = b
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("Enforce media marker failed for %s: %s", meta.serial_code, e)

    title = meta.title
    serial_code = meta.serial_code.strip()

    if not serial_code:
        jalali = meta.fa_date
        serial_val = post.get("serial")
        ch_key = meta.channel
        ch_code = CHANNEL_CODES.get(ch_key)
        try:
            if ch_code is not None and serial_val is not None:
                serial_int = int(serial_val)
                counter_val = ch_code * 1000 + serial_int
                serial_code = f"{jalali}-{counter_val}"
            elif serial_val is not None:
                serial_code = f"{jalali}-{int(serial_val):04d}"
            else:
                serial_code = f"unknown-{ch_key or ''}"
        except Exception:
            serial_code = f"unknown-{ch_key or ''}"

    fa_date = meta.fa_date

    try:
        core = build_message(
            title=title,
            serial_code=serial_code,
            fa_date=fa_date,
            body=body,
            include_signature=False,
        )
    except Exception:
        header = (
            "🔹 آگهی استخدام و نیازمندی ها | ASA SANAT | آساصنعت |\n"
            f"🆔 {escape_html(serial_code)}\n"
            f"📅 تاریخ : {escape_html(fa_date)}"
        )
        core = "\n\n".join([header, f"📌 {escape_html(title)}" if title else "", escape_html(body)]).strip()

    source_channel = post.get("source_channel") or ""
    try:
        serial_int = int(post["serial"]) if post.get("serial") is not None else None
    except Exception:
        serial_int = None
    core = _maybe_prepend_numeric_counter(core, source_channel, serial_int)

    parts = [core.rstrip()]
    tags_line = _format_tags_for_post(meta.tags)
    if tags_line:
        parts.append(tags_line)
    sig = get_signature_text()
    if sig:
        parts.append(f"<b>{escape_html(sig)}</b>")

    if not body:
        log.warning("Post %s has no body (processed_text/raw_text empty)", post.get("id"))
        report_log("sender", f"Post {post.get('id')} has no body", level="WARNING")

    return "\n\n".join(parts).strip()

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def _has_meaningful_url(s: str) -> bool:
    for m in URL_RE.finditer(s or ""):
        url = m.group(0).lower()
        if not re.search(r'(?:t\.me|telegram\.me|eitaa\.|rubika\.|gap\.)', url):
            return True
    return False

async def send_message(
    bot: Bot,
    channel_id: Union[int, str],
    serial_code: str,
    text: str
) -> bool:
    text_stripped = (text or "").strip()
    if not text_stripped:
        log.warning("%s: empty text, skipping", serial_code)
        report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: empty text, skipping", level="WARNING")
        return False

    has_url_any = bool(URL_RE.search(text_stripped))
    meaningful_url = _has_meaningful_url(text_stripped)

    disable_preview = (
        DEFAULT_DISABLE_PREVIEW
        or (_is_low_value_text(text_stripped) and not meaningful_url)
    )

    try:
        target_key = str(channel_id).lstrip("@").lower()
    except Exception:
        target_key = ""

    if target_key in FORCE_NO_PREVIEW_TARGETS:
        disable_preview = True

    chunks = safe_html_chunks(text_stripped, TELEGRAM_MESSAGE_LIMIT)

    for idx, (chunk, mode) in enumerate(chunks, start=1):
        tried_plain = False
        retries = 0

        while True:
            if retries >= MAX_CHUNK_RETRIES:
                log.error("%s: chunk %d/%d exceeded max retries (%d)", serial_code, idx, len(chunks), MAX_CHUNK_RETRIES)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: chunk {idx}/{len(chunks)} exceeded retries", level="ERROR")
                return False

            try:
                await bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=channel_id,
                    text=chunk,
                    disable_web_page_preview=disable_preview,
                    parse_mode=ParseMode.HTML if mode == 'HTML' else None,
                )
                log.debug("%s: chunk %d/%d sent (preview=%s)", serial_code, idx, len(chunks), not disable_preview)
                break

            except TelegramForbiddenError as e:
                log.warning("%s: forbidden to send to %r: %s", serial_code, channel_id, e)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: forbidden to send to {channel_id}: {e}", level="ERROR")
                return False

            except TelegramBadRequest as e:
                log.exception("%s: HTML send failed on chunk %d/%d (len=%d): %s", serial_code, idx, len(chunks), len(chunk), e)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: HTML send failed on chunk {idx}/{len(chunks)}: {e}", level="WARNING")

                if not tried_plain:
                    tried_plain = True
                    plain_text = re.sub(r"<[^>]+>", "", chunk).strip()
                    log.info("%s: retrying chunk %d/%d as plain text", serial_code, idx, len(chunks))
                    try:
                        await bot.send_message(
                            chat_id=channel_id,
                            text=plain_text,
                            disable_web_page_preview=disable_preview,
                            parse_mode=None,
                        )
                        log.info("%s: fallback plain send succeeded for chunk %d/%d", serial_code, idx, len(chunks))
                        break
                    except TelegramForbiddenError as e2:
                        log.warning("%s: forbidden on plain retry to %r: %s", serial_code, channel_id, e2)
                        report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: forbidden on plain retry to {channel_id}: {e2}", level="ERROR")
                        return False
                    except Exception as e2:
                        retries += 1
                        log.error("%s: fallback plain send failed for chunk %d/%d: %s", serial_code, idx, len(chunks), e2)
                        report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: fallback plain send failed: {e2}", level="ERROR")
                        await asyncio.sleep(min(2 ** retries, 30))
                        continue
                else:
                    log.warning("%s: plain send also failed on chunk %d/%d, skipping", serial_code, idx, len(chunks))
                    report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: plain send failed twice on chunk {idx}/{len(chunks)}", level="WARNING")
                    break

            except TelegramRetryAfter as e:
                delay = float(getattr(e, "retry_after", 1))
                log.warning("%s: rate limited; sleeping %.1fs", serial_code, delay)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: rate limited, sleeping {delay}s", level="WARNING")
                await asyncio.sleep(delay + 0.5)
                retries += 1

            except TelegramNetworkError as e:
                retries += 1
                backoff = min(2 ** retries, 30)
                log.warning("%s: network error: %s. retry %d/%d in %.1fs", serial_code, e, retries, MAX_CHUNK_RETRIES, backoff)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: network error {e}, retry {retries}", level="WARNING")
                await asyncio.sleep(backoff)

            except Exception as e:
                log.exception("%s: unexpected send error: %s", serial_code, e)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial_code}: unexpected send error {e}", level="ERROR")
                return False

    return True
# ---------- DB summary log ----------
def _log_db_summary(prefix: str = "DB summary") -> None:
    try:
        rows = repository.get_channel_counts()
        total_unsent = sum(int(r.get("unsent") or 0) for r in rows)
        total_sent   = sum(int(r.get("sent") or 0) for r in rows)
        log.info("%s: channels=%d total_sent=%d total_unsent=%d", prefix, len(rows), total_sent, total_unsent)
        report_log("sender", f"{prefix}: channels={len(rows)} total_sent={total_sent} total_unsent={total_unsent}")
        # سازگاری با regex فعلی job_runner:
        log.info("DB after run: unsent=%d", total_unsent)
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception("Failed to log DB summary: %s", e)
        report_log("sender", f"{prefix}: failed to get DB summary: {e}", level="ERROR")

# ---------- Admin helpers ----------
async def _send_admin_report(bot: Bot, admin_chat: Optional[Union[int, str]], title: str, body: str) -> None:
    if not admin_chat:
        return
    try:
        await bot.send_message(
            chat_id=admin_chat,
            text=f"{title}\n\n{body}",
            disable_web_page_preview=True,
            parse_mode=None,
        )
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("Failed to send admin report to %r: %s", admin_chat, e)
        report_log("sender", f"Failed to send admin report to {admin_chat}: {e}", level="WARNING")

def _ensure_bot_token() -> Optional[str]:
    return getattr(settings, "bot_token", None) or getattr(settings, "telegram_bot_token", None)

async def _close_bot_safely(bot: Bot) -> None:
    try:
        session = getattr(bot, "session", None)
        if session is None:
            return
        close_fn = getattr(session, "close", None)
        if not callable(close_fn):
            return
        result = close_fn()
        if inspect.isawaitable(result):
            await result
        await asyncio.sleep(0)
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("bot session close failed: %s", e)
        report_log("sender", f"Bot session close failed: {e}", level="WARNING")

# ---------- Main send flow ----------
async def send_pending_posts(limit: Optional[int] = None) -> None:
    report_heartbeat("sender")
    token = _ensure_bot_token()
    if not token:
        log.error("Bot token not configured.")
        report_log("sender", "Bot token not configured.", level="ERROR")
        return

    target = normalize_chat_id(getattr(settings, "target_channel", None))
    if not target:
        log.error("target_channel not configured.")
        report_log("sender", "target_channel not configured.", level="ERROR")
        return

    _log_db_summary(prefix="DB before run")

    fetch_limit = int(limit or MAX_SEND_PER_RUN)
    try:
        posts = repository.fetch_unsent_full_sorted_by_serial(fetch_limit)
    except Exception as e:
        log.exception("Failed to fetch unsent posts: %s", e)
        report_log("sender", f"Failed to fetch unsent posts: {e}", level="ERROR")
        return

    total_found = len(posts or [])
    log.info("Pending posts to send: %d", total_found)
    report_log("sender", f"Pending posts to send: {total_found}")
    if not posts:
        log.info("Nothing to send. Exiting.")
        return

    bot = Bot(token=token, default=DefaultBotProperties(parse_mode=ParseMode.HTML))
    admin_chat = normalize_chat_id(getattr(settings, "admin_chat_id", None))

    sent_count = 0
    start_time = time.time()
    sent_list: list[tuple[str, int]] = []
    failed_list: list[tuple[str, int, str]] = []
    skipped_list: list[tuple[str, int, str]] = []
    pending_list: list[tuple[str, int]] = []

    # sync requests in thread
    def _post_sync(url, payload, headers, timeout):
        return requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=timeout)

    async def _send_with_retries(payload, headers, serial: str = "", tries: int = N8N_MAX_TRIES, initial_backoff: float = N8N_BACKOFF, timeout: int = 15):
        # لاگ "ارسال" فقط یکبار
        log.info(json.dumps({"ev": "n8n.send", "run_id": RUN_ID, "serial": serial}, ensure_ascii=False))
        last_exc = None
        for attempt in range(1, tries + 1):
            try:
                t0 = time.time()
                resp = await asyncio.to_thread(_post_sync, N8N_WEBHOOK_URL, payload, headers, timeout)
                ms = int((time.time() - t0) * 1000)
                log.info(json.dumps({
                    "ev": "n8n.resp",
                    "run_id": RUN_ID,
                    "serial": serial,
                    "status": getattr(resp, "status_code", None),
                    "ms": ms,
                    "attempt": attempt
                }, ensure_ascii=False))
                return resp
            except Exception as exc:
                last_exc = exc
                log.error(json.dumps({
                    "ev": "n8n.error",
                    "run_id": RUN_ID,
                    "serial": serial,
                    "attempt": attempt,
                    "err": str(exc)
                }, ensure_ascii=False))
                await asyncio.sleep(initial_backoff * (2 ** (attempt - 1)))
        log.error(json.dumps({
            "ev": "n8n.final_error",
            "run_id": RUN_ID,
            "serial": serial,
            "err": str(last_exc)
        }, ensure_ascii=False))
        return None

    # MAIN
    try:
        try:
            has_access = await ensure_access(bot, target)
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception("ensure_access failed: %s", e)
            report_log("sender", f"ensure_access failed: {e}", level="ERROR")
            return

        if not has_access:
            log.error("No access to target %r", target)
            report_log("sender", f"No access to target {target}", level="ERROR")
            return

        rate = RateState(hourly_limit=HOURLY_LIMIT, daily_limit=DAILY_LIMIT)

        for idx, post in enumerate(posts, start=1):
            if not rate.allow():
                log.info("Rate limit reached. Stopping early.")
                report_log("sender", "Rate limit reached. Stopping early.")
                for p in posts[idx-1:]:
                    src = p.get("source_channel") or "unknown"
                    pid = p.get("id")
                    serial_code = p.get("serial_code") or ""
                    pending_list.append((src, pid or serial_code))
                break

            serial = post.get("serial_code") or ""
            if not serial:
                try:
                    serial = build_counter_from_post(post) or serial
                except Exception:
                    pass
                if not serial:
                    jalali = post.get("jalali_date") or to_jalali_code(datetime.now(timezone.utc))
                    serial = f"{jalali}-{post.get('serial') or 'unknown'}"

            source = post.get("source_channel") or "unknown"
            post_id = post.get("id")

            log.debug("Processing %s (%d/%d) from %s", serial, idx, total_found, source)

            try:
                text = build_text_from_db_or_fallback(post)
            except Exception as e:
                log.exception("build_text failed for id=%s serial=%s: %s", post.get("id"), post.get("serial_code"), e)
                report_log("sender", f"build_text failed for id={post.get('id')} serial={post.get('serial_code')}: {e}", level="ERROR")
                skipped_list.append((source, post_id or serial, "BuildTextFailed"))
                continue

            if not text.strip():
                log.warning("%s: empty message, skipping", serial)
                report_log("sender", f"{serial}: empty message, skipping", level="WARNING")
                skipped_list.append((source, post_id or serial, "EmptyMessage"))
                continue

            log.info("Sending %s (%d/%d) → %s", serial, idx, total_found, target)

            # تلاش برای ارسال
            ok = await send_message(bot, target, serial, text)

            # اگر پست دیتابیس دارد، قبل از ارسال آن را claim کنیم
            if post_id:
                try:
                    repository.mark_sending_by_id(int(post_id), claim_token=RUN_ID)
                except Exception:
                    log.exception("mark_sending_by_id failed for id=%s", post_id)

            if ok:
                # ارسال موفق
                sent_count += 1
                rate.mark()  # ثبت در محدودیت‌های نرخ

                if post_id:
                    try:
                        repository.mark_sent_by_id(int(post_id))
                        report_post_status("sender", int(post_id), "sent")
                        sent_list.append((source, int(post_id)))
                    except Exception:
                        log.exception("mark_sent_by_id/report_post_status failed for id=%s", post_id)

            else:
                # ارسال ناموفق
                if post_id:
                    try:
                        repository.mark_failed_by_id(int(post_id), err_text="SendFailed")
                        report_post_status("sender", int(post_id), "failed")
                    except Exception:
                        log.exception("mark_failed_by_id/report_post_status failed for id=%s", post_id)

                failed_list.append((source, post_id or serial, "SendFailed"))
                report_log("sender", f"Send failed for {serial}", level="WARNING")

            # mirror policy
            should_mirror = True
            if os.getenv("MIRROR_ONLY_ON_TG_SUCCESS", "0").lower() in ("1", "true", "yes") and not ok:
                should_mirror = False

            if not should_mirror:
                log.info(json.dumps({
                    "ev": "n8n.skipped",
                    "run_id": RUN_ID,
                    "serial": serial,
                    "reason": "telegram_failed"
                }, ensure_ascii=False))
                # بعدی
                delay = random.uniform(MIN_SEND_DELAY_S, MAX_SEND_DELAY_S)
                await asyncio.sleep(delay)
                log.info("Run partial. sent=%d / attempted=%d", sent_count, total_found)
                report_log("sender", f"Run partial. sent={sent_count} attempted={total_found}")
                _log_db_summary(prefix="DB after run")
                continue

            # payload to n8n with run_id
            payload = {
                "channel_post": {"text": text or "", "entities": post.get("entities", []) or []},
                "message": {"text": text or "", "entities": post.get("entities", []) or []},
                "meta": {
                    "serial_code": post.get("serial_code"),
                    "source_channel": post.get("source_channel"),
                    "source_id": post.get("source_id"),
                    "jalali_date": post.get("jalali_date"),
                    "links": post.get("links", []) or [],
                    "location": post.get("location"),
                    "phone": post.get("phone"),
                    "run_id": RUN_ID
                }
            }

            headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Run-Id": RUN_ID}
            if N8N_SECRET_HEADER_NAME and N8N_SECRET_TOKEN:
                headers[N8N_SECRET_HEADER_NAME] = N8N_SECRET_TOKEN

            # ارسال با retry/backoff و لاگ‌های JSON
            await _send_with_retries(payload, headers, serial=serial, tries=N8N_MAX_TRIES, initial_backoff=N8N_BACKOFF, timeout=15)

            # delay + partial log (یک‌بار کافی است)
            delay = random.uniform(MIN_SEND_DELAY_S, MAX_SEND_DELAY_S)
            await asyncio.sleep(delay)
            log.info("Run partial. sent=%d / attempted=%d", sent_count, total_found)
            report_log("sender", f"Run partial. sent={sent_count} attempted={total_found}")
            _log_db_summary(prefix="DB after run")

        # خلاصه نهایی برای job_runner (JSON و legacy)
        log.info(json.dumps({
            "ev": "sender.summary",
            "run_id": RUN_ID,
            "total_attempted": total_found,
            "total_sent": sent_count
        }, ensure_ascii=False))
        log.info("Run complete. sent=%d / attempted=%d", sent_count, total_found)

    finally:
        # گزارش مدیریتی و جمع‌بندی
        try:
            await send_sender_report(bot, admin_chat, sent_list, failed_list, skipped_list, pending_list, start_time)
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception("Failed to send sender report: %s", e)
            report_log("sender", f"Failed to send sender report: {e}", level="ERROR")
        try:
            await _close_bot_safely(bot)
        except Exception as e:
            log.exception("Failed to close bot: %s", e)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Send pending posts to target channel")
    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="Max posts to send in this run")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    asyncio.run(send_pending_posts(limit=args.limit))

# src/services/serial.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from src import logger_setup
import asyncio
from sqlalchemy import text
from sqlalchemy.dialects.sqlite import insert as sqlite_insert
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy.exc import OperationalError, DatabaseError

from src.core.constants import CHANNEL_CODES
from src.core.config import settings
from src.db.models import PostCounter

logger = logging.getLogger("asa.serial")


def make_serial_code(jalali_date: str, channel_key: str, serial: int) -> str:
    """
    Build serial_code = '{jalali_date}-{channel_code*1000 + serial}'
    Accepts channel_key in any of: 'name', '@name', 'https://t.me/name'.
    """
    key = (channel_key or "").strip()
    if key.startswith("https://t.me/"):
        key = key.split("/")[-1]
    key = key.lstrip("@").lower()

    # prefer env-configured codes, fallback to constants
    codes = settings.channel_codes_normalized() or CHANNEL_CODES
    ch_code = codes.get(key)
    if ch_code is None:
        # Fallback: jalali + serial ساده تا جریان نخوابد
        return f"{jalali_date}-{int(serial):04d}"
    counter = int(ch_code) * 1000 + int(serial)
    return f"{jalali_date}-{counter}"



# ---------- retry helpers ----------
async def _retry_async(fn, *args, max_retries: int = 5, base_delay: float = 0.05, **kwargs):
    last_exc = None
    for attempt in range(1, max_retries + 1):
        try:
            return await fn(*args, **kwargs)
        except (OperationalError, DatabaseError) as exc:
            last_exc = exc
            msg = str(exc).lower()
            if "database is locked" in msg or "sqlite_busy" in msg or "sqlite3.operationalerror" in msg:
                delay = base_delay * (2 ** (attempt - 1))
                logger.warning("Database busy/locked (attempt %d/%d). Sleeping %.3fs", attempt, max_retries, delay)
                await asyncio.sleep(delay)
                continue
            raise
    logger.error("Retries exhausted for async DB call: %s", last_exc)
    raise last_exc


def _retry_sync(fn, *args, max_retries: int = 5, base_delay: float = 0.05, **kwargs):
    import time
    last_exc = None
    for attempt in range(1, max_retries + 1):
        try:
            return fn(*args, **kwargs)
        except (OperationalError, DatabaseError) as exc:
            last_exc = exc
            msg = str(exc).lower()
            if "database is locked" in msg or "sqlite_busy" in msg:
                delay = base_delay * (2 ** (attempt - 1))
                logger.warning("Database busy/locked (attempt %d/%d). Sleeping %.3fs", attempt, max_retries, delay)
                time.sleep(delay)
                continue
            raise
    logger.error("Retries exhausted for sync DB call: %s", last_exc)
    raise last_exc


# ---------- async ----------
async def atomic_next_serial_async(db: AsyncSession, ch_key: str, fa_date_code: str) -> int:
    """
    Atomically increment and return the per-channel counter.

    Primary path (v2):
      - Table: post_counters_v2(channel_key PRIMARY KEY, value INTEGER NOT NULL)
      - Ignores jalali_date (fa_date_code) because the counter is global per channel.

    Fallback (v1):
      - Table: post_counters(channel_key, jalali_date) PRIMARY KEY
      - Uses jalali_date for day-scoped counter.

    Note:
      - This function DOES NOT commit; caller manages transaction boundaries.
      - Retries transient SQLite lock errors.
    """
    async def _do_v2_with_returning() -> int:
        stmt = text(
            "INSERT INTO post_counters_v2 (channel_key, value) VALUES (:ch, 1) "
            "ON CONFLICT(channel_key) DO UPDATE SET value = value + 1 "
            "RETURNING value"
        )
        res = await db.execute(stmt, {"ch": ch_key})
        val = res.scalar_one_or_none()
        if val is not None:
            new_val = int(val)
            logger.debug("[ASYNC][V2] Counter %s -> %d (RETURNING path)", ch_key, new_val)
            return new_val
        return await _do_v2_no_returning()

    async def _do_v2_no_returning() -> int:
        await db.execute(
            text("INSERT INTO post_counters_v2 (channel_key, value) VALUES (:ch, 0) "
                 "ON CONFLICT(channel_key) DO NOTHING"),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        await db.execute(
            text("UPDATE post_counters_v2 SET value = value + 1 WHERE channel_key = :ch"),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        r = await db.execute(
            text("SELECT value FROM post_counters_v2 WHERE channel_key = :ch"),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        val = r.scalar_one()
        new_val = int(val)
        logger.debug("[ASYNC][V2] Counter %s -> %d (no-returning path)", ch_key, new_val)
        return new_val

    async def _do_v1_fallback() -> int:
        table = PostCounter.__table__
        stmt = (
            sqlite_insert(table)
            .values(channel_key=ch_key, jalali_date=fa_date_code, value=1)
            .on_conflict_do_update(
                index_elements=[table.c.channel_key, table.c.jalali_date],
                set_={"value": table.c.value + 1},
            )
            .returning(table.c.value)
        )
        res = await db.execute(stmt)
        val = res.scalar_one_or_none()
        if val is not None:
            new_val = int(val)
            logger.debug("[ASYNC][V1] Counter %s-%s -> %d (RETURNING path)", ch_key, fa_date_code, new_val)
            return new_val

        await db.execute(
            sqlite_insert(table)
            .values(channel_key=ch_key, jalali_date=fa_date_code, value=0)
            .on_conflict_do_nothing()
        )
        await db.execute(
            text("UPDATE post_counters SET value = value + 1 WHERE channel_key = :ch AND jalali_date = :d"),
            {"ch": ch_key, "d": fa_date_code},
        )
        r = await db.execute(
            text("SELECT value FROM post_counters WHERE channel_key = :ch AND jalali_date = :d"),
            {"ch": ch_key, "d": fa_date_code},
        )
        val2 = r.scalar_one()
        new_val = int(val2)
        logger.debug("[ASYNC][V1] Counter %s-%s -> %d (fallback path)", ch_key, fa_date_code, new_val)
        return new_val

    async def _do() -> int:
        try:
            return await _do_v2_with_returning()
        except (OperationalError, DatabaseError) as e:
            msg = str(e).lower()
            if "near \"returning\"" in msg or ("returning" in msg and "syntax error" in msg):
                logger.debug("[ASYNC][V2] RETURNING not supported; switching to no-returning path")
                return await _do_v2_no_returning()
            if "no such table: post_counters_v2" in msg:
                logger.debug("[ASYNC][V2] post_counters_v2 missing; falling back to V1")
                return await _do_v1_fallback()
            raise

    return await _retry_async(_do)


# ---------- sync ----------
def atomic_next_serial(session: Session, ch_key: str, fa_date_code: str) -> int:
    """Sync counterpart of atomic_next_serial_async with same behavior and fallbacks. DOES NOT commit."""
    def _do_v2_with_returning() -> int:
        res = session.execute(
            text(
                "INSERT INTO post_counters_v2 (channel_key, value) VALUES (:ch, 1) "
                "ON CONFLICT(channel_key) DO UPDATE SET value = value + 1 "
                "RETURNING value"
            ),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        val = res.scalar_one_or_none()
        if val is not None:
            new_val = int(val)
            logger.debug("[SYNC][V2] Counter %s -> %d (RETURNING path)", ch_key, new_val)
            return new_val
        return _do_v2_no_returning()

    def _do_v2_no_returning() -> int:
        session.execute(
            text("INSERT INTO post_counters_v2 (channel_key, value) VALUES (:ch, 0) "
                 "ON CONFLICT(channel_key) DO NOTHING"),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        session.execute(
            text("UPDATE post_counters_v2 SET value = value + 1 WHERE channel_key = :ch"),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        r = session.execute(
            text("SELECT value FROM post_counters_v2 WHERE channel_key = :ch"),
            {"ch": ch_key},
        )
        val = r.scalar_one()
        new_val = int(val)
        logger.debug("[SYNC][V2] Counter %s -> %d (no-returning path)", ch_key, new_val)
        return new_val

    def _do_v1_fallback() -> int:
        table = PostCounter.__table__
        stmt = (
            sqlite_insert(table)
            .values(channel_key=ch_key, jalali_date=fa_date_code, value=1)
            .on_conflict_do_update(
                index_elements=[table.c.channel_key, table.c.jalali_date],
                set_={"value": table.c.value + 1},
            )
            .returning(table.c.value)
        )
        res = session.execute(stmt)
        val = res.scalar_one_or_none()
        if val is not None:
            new_val = int(val)
            logger.debug("[SYNC][V1] Counter %s-%s -> %d (RETURNING path)", ch_key, fa_date_code, new_val)
            return new_val

        session.execute(
            sqlite_insert(table)
            .values(channel_key=ch_key, jalali_date=fa_date_code, value=0)
            .on_conflict_do_nothing()
        )
        session.execute(
            text("UPDATE post_counters SET value = value + 1 WHERE channel_key = :ch AND jalali_date = :d"),
            {"ch": ch_key, "d": fa_date_code},
        )
        r = session.execute(
            text("SELECT value FROM post_counters WHERE channel_key = :ch AND jalali_date = :d"),
            {"ch": ch_key, "d": fa_date_code},
        )
        val2 = r.scalar_one()
        new_val = int(val2)
        logger.debug("[SYNC][V1] Counter %s-%s -> %d (fallback path)", ch_key, fa_date_code, new_val)
        return new_val

    def _do() -> int:
        try:
            return _do_v2_with_returning()
        except (OperationalError, DatabaseError) as e:
            msg = str(e).lower()
            if "near \"returning\"" in msg or ("returning" in msg and "syntax error" in msg):
                logger.debug("[SYNC][V2] RETURNING not supported; switching to no-returning path")
                return _do_v2_no_returning()
            if "no such table: post_counters_v2" in msg:
                logger.debug("[SYNC][V2] post_counters_v2 missing; falling back to V1")
                return _do_v1_fallback()
            raise

    return _retry_sync(_do)
